### [1] [Coverage is not enough: Frequentist tests of simulation-based inference for primordial non-Gaussianity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00980)
*Toka Alokda,Cristiano Porciani,Alexander Eggemeier*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Summary generation failed


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Method: Method extraction failed

Result: Result analysis unavailable

Conclusion: Conclusion extraction failed

Abstract: (Abridged) Simulation-based inference (SBI) has emerged as a powerful framework for extracting cosmological information from complex, non-linear data where analytical likelihoods are unavailable. Its reliability is commonly assessed using coverage-based diagnostics under the prior predictive distribution, which probe calibration only in an averaged sense and do not constrain posterior behavior at fixed parameter value, the regime relevant for practical inference. We investigate these limitations in the context of primordial non-Gaussianity, parameterized by $f_\mathrm{NL}$, using simulations of the dark matter halo field. We compare SBI based on contrastive neural ratio estimation (CNRE) with likelihood-based inference (LBI) using the power spectrum, bispectrum, and wavelet scattering transform (WST) coefficients across 1000 realizations. SBI and LBI agree well on posterior means and skewness, while the variance agrees on average but shows weaker realization-by-realization consistency. Larger differences arise in the kurtosis, indicating discrepancies in the posterior tails. These effects are already present for the power spectrum - where the Gaussian likelihood assumed in LBI is best justified - and are most pronounced for the combined power spectrum and bispectrum, where SBI posteriors are often underconfident and can yield weaker constraints than either statistic individually, despite passing coverage tests. WST coefficients further tighten constraints on $f_\mathrm{NL}$, even when restricted to large scales. Our results highlight both the potential of higher-order statistics and the need for validation strategies that probe the posterior shape beyond standard coverage diagnostics.

</details>


### [2] [Implications of \textit{SARAS3} data for Coulomb-like interacting dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00991)
*Shikhar Mittal,Prakhar Bansal,Harry Bevins,Saurabh Singh*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the implications of the SARAS3 non-detection in the 55.5-84.4 MHz band for Coulomb-like interacting dark matter (IDM). The study includes both gas cooling and the suppression of structure formation, leading to a delay in star formation. A joint Bayesian fit is performed on the 21-cm signal and foreground models, with the data disfavoring deep absorption features within the observed band. No statistically significant preference for IDM over standard cold dark matter is found, but an upper bound on the global 21-cm signal amplitude is established.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The 21-cm signal from cosmic dawn can be a sensitive probe of interactions between dark matter (DM) and baryons. Previous studies have focused mainly on baryon cooling. This work aims to model the interaction self-consistently by including both excess cooling of the gas and the suppression of structure formation, which delays the onset of star formation and suppresses the Ly$\alpha$, X-ray, and ionizing backgrounds at early times.

21厘米信号来自宇宙黎明，可以作为暗物质（DM）和重子之间相互作用的敏感探测器。以往的研究主要集中在重子冷却上。这项工作旨在通过包括气体的额外冷却和结构形成的抑制来一致地建模这种相互作用，这会延迟恒星形成的开始，并在早期抑制Ly$\alpha$、X射线和电离背景。

Method: The authors perform a joint Bayesian fit of a global 21-cm signal model and a flexible foreground model to the SARAS3 antenna temperature. They include both the excess cooling of the gas and the suppression of structure formation, which delays the onset of star formation and hence suppresses the Ly$\alpha$, X-ray, and ionizing backgrounds at early times. The analysis accounts for the marginalization over the foregrounds, allowing for a more robust constraint on the 21-cm signal parameters.

作者对SARAS3天线温度进行了全球21厘米信号模型和灵活前景模型的联合贝叶斯拟合。他们同时考虑了气体的额外冷却和结构形成的抑制，这会延迟恒星形成的开始，从而在早期抑制Ly$\alpha$、X射线和电离背景。分析中考虑了对前景的边缘化处理，从而对21厘米信号参数提供了更稳健的约束。

Result: The data disfavor deep absorption features within the observed band, with the strongest bound at $z = 23.6$ ($\nu \approx 57.7$ MHz), where $T_{21} \gtrsim -277.6$ mK at $3\sigma$. The null result indicates that no statistically significant preference for IDM over standard cold dark matter is found, with a Bayes factor $B \approx 1.7$. The SARAS3 non-detection places a meaningful upper bound on the amplitude of the global 21-cm signal in this class of models.

数据不支持观测频段内的深吸收特征，在$z = 23.6$（$\nu \approx 57.7$ MHz）处最强的约束为$T_{21} \gtrsim -277.6$ mK（$3\sigma$）。零结果表明，没有发现IDM相对于标准冷暗物质有统计学上的显著偏好，贝叶斯因子$B \approx 1.7$。SARAS3未检测到信号为这类模型中的全球21厘米信号幅度提供了一个有意义的上限。

Conclusion: The SARAS3 non-detection provides a meaningful upper bound on the amplitude of the global 21-cm signal for Coulomb-like interacting dark matter (IDM) models. While the data do not favor IDM over standard cold dark matter, the inclusion of both excess cooling and structure formation suppression in the modeling offers a more comprehensive understanding of the 21-cm signal. Further observations and analyses are needed to better constrain the strength of baryon-DM interactions.

SARAS3未检测到信号为库仑型相互作用暗物质（IDM）模型中的全球21厘米信号幅度提供了一个有意义的上限。尽管数据并未显示IDM优于标准冷暗物质，但将额外冷却和结构形成抑制纳入模型中，为我们提供了对21厘米信号更全面的理解。需要进一步的观测和分析以更好地约束重子-暗物质相互作用的强度。

Abstract: The 21-cm signal from cosmic dawn is a potentially sensitive probe of interactions between dark matter (DM) and baryons. We investigate the implications of the SARAS3 non-detection in the 55.5-84.4 MHz band for Coulomb-like interacting DM (IDM). In contrast to earlier constraint analyses that focused primarily on baryon cooling, we model the interaction self-consistently by including both excess cooling of the gas and the suppression of structure formation, which delays the onset of star formation and hence suppresses the Ly$α$, X-ray, and ionizing backgrounds at early times. We perform a joint Bayesian fit of a global 21-cm signal model and a flexible foreground model to the SARAS3 antenna temperature, and find that the signal parameters remain weakly constrained after marginalizing over the foregrounds. The null result is nonetheless informative: the data disfavour deep absorption features within the observed band, with the strongest bound at $z = 23.6$ ($ν\approx 57.7$ MHz), where $T_{21} \gtrsim -277.6$ mK at $3σ$. Comparing the IDM and standard cold dark matter scenarios, we find no statistically significant preference for IDM (Bayes factor $B \approx 1.7$). While we do not constrain the strength of baryon-DM interactions, the SARAS3 non-detection places a meaningful upper bound on the amplitude of the global 21-cm signal in this class of models.

</details>


### [3] [Formation and Redshift Evolution of Dark Matter Spikes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01023)
*Gonzalo Herrera,Abdelaziz Hussein,Lina Necib,Elliot Y. Davies,Xuejian Shen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper presents a semi-analytic framework to study the evolution of dark matter density spikes around growing black holes, including the effects of finite seed masses, stellar cusps, and non-circular orbits. The results show that stellar gravitational heating significantly reduces the inner slope of the dark matter profile over time, leading to overdensities that are lower than canonical predictions but still significant for indirect dark matter detection signals.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Canonical predictions for dark matter density spikes around black holes assume a zero-mass seed in a purely dark matter environment, neglecting the long-term dynamical impact of surrounding stars. This work aims to generalize adiabatic spike formation to include realistic conditions such as finite seed masses, stellar cusps, and non-circular orbits, and to study the subsequent cosmic evolution of these spikes under the influence of stellar gravitational heating. 

传统的暗物质密度尖峰预测假设黑洞在纯暗物质环境中以零质量种子形成，忽略了周围恒星的长期动力学影响。这项工作旨在将绝热尖峰形成推广到包括有限种子质量、恒星核球和非圆形轨道等现实条件，并研究这些尖峰在恒星引力加热影响下的后续宇宙演化。

Method: A semi-analytic framework is developed to model the formation and evolution of dark matter density spikes. The framework incorporates finite seed masses, stellar cusps, and non-circular orbits, and solves coupled Fokker-Planck equations for the phase-space distributions of both dark matter and stars. The heating rate due to stellar interactions is modulated by the cosmic star formation rate, allowing for a comprehensive study of the spike's evolution over cosmic timescales. 

开发了一个半解析框架来模拟暗物质密度尖峰的形成和演化。该框架包括有限种子质量、恒星核球和非圆形轨道，并求解了描述暗物质和恒星相空间分布的耦合Fokker-Planck方程。由于恒星相互作用导致的加热速率由宇宙恒星形成率调节，这使得能够全面研究尖峰在宇宙时间尺度上的演化。

Result: The analysis shows that stellar gravitational heating drives the inner slope of the dark matter profile towards $\gamma_\chi \simeq 1.5$ within a few Gyrs, resulting in overdensities two to four orders of magnitude below canonical expectations. Despite this reduction, the overdensities remain well above an NFW-like cusp, indicating that the dark matter distribution is still significantly enhanced compared to standard models. Redshift-dependent benchmarks for the column density and $J$-factor, relevant to scattering, decay, and annihilation signatures, are provided. 

分析表明，恒星引力加热在几Gyr内使暗物质轮廓的内斜率趋向于$\gamma_\chi \simeq 1.5$，导致过密度比标准预期低两到四个数量级。尽管有所减少，但过密度仍远高于NFW型核球，表明暗物质分布与标准模型相比仍有显著增强。提供了与散射、衰变和湮灭信号相关的红移依赖性柱密度和$J$因子基准。

Conclusion: The inclusion of realistic astrophysical processes, such as the presence of stellar cusps and the effect of stellar gravitational heating, significantly alters the expected dark matter density profiles around black holes. These findings imply that any robust interpretation of indirect dark matter signals from galactic nuclei must account for the evolution of these spikes, which can be substantially different from the canonical predictions. 

包含现实的天体物理过程，如恒星核球的存在和恒星引力加热的影响，显著改变了黑洞周围的暗物质密度轮廓。这些发现意味着，对来自银河系核心的间接暗物质信号的任何稳健解释都必须考虑到这些尖峰的演化，这可能与标准预测大不相同。

Abstract: Dark matter density spikes forming around adiabatically growing black holes can dramatically enhance indirect and direct detection signals. Canonical predictions, however, assume a zero-mass seed in a purely dark matter environment and do not track the long-term dynamical impact of surrounding stars. We present a semi-analytic framework that first generalizes adiabatic spike formation to include finite seed masses, stellar cusps, and non-circular orbits, and then studies the subsequent cosmic evolution by solving coupled Fokker-Planck equations for the dark matter and stellar phase-space distributions, with a heating rate modulated by the cosmic star formation rate. Starting conservatively from canonical Gondolo-Silk spikes and marginalizing over astrophysical uncertainties, we find that stellar gravitational heating drives the inner slope towards $γ_χ\simeq 1.5$ within a few Gyrs (e.g by $z \lesssim 2$ for spikes formed at $z\simeq 10$), yielding overdensities two to four orders of magnitude below canonical expectations but still well above an NFW-like cusp. We provide redshift-dependent benchmarks for the column density and $J$-factor relevant to scattering, decay and annihilation signatures. Any robust interpretation of indirect dark matter signals from galactic nuclei must account for this evolution.

</details>


### [4] [A structural degeneracy explains reionization tensions and limits dark matter constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01380)
*Zihan Wang,Huanyuan Shan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper identifies a structural degeneracy in reionization studies, where the ionizing photon rate is only sensitive to the product of the ionizing escape fraction and peak star formation efficiency, leading to non-invertible mappings between model parameters and observations. This degeneracy is demonstrated using N-body simulations, and it limits the use of reionization-based probes for dark matter. The only way to break this degeneracy is through observables that are sensitive to the spatial topology of ionized regions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of the paper is to address the persistent discrepancies in the inferred ionizing escape fraction $f_{\mathrm{esc}}$ and peak star formation efficiency $f_{*,0}$ in reionization studies, which have been further complicated by the discovery of unexpectedly bright galaxies at $z>10$ by JWST. The authors aim to provide a unified explanation for the scatter among published constraints and establish a framework for interpreting reionization observations and their implications for early galaxy formation and dark matter.

Method: The authors demonstrate the robustness of the structural degeneracy using a large suite of N-body simulations of self-interacting dark matter haloes spanning $10^9$-$10^{11} M_\\odot$. They show that despite substantial changes to galaxy-scale structure, observables remain indistinguishable once the effective ionizing emissivity is matched. The study also identifies that only observables sensitive to the spatial topology of ionized regions can break this degeneracy.

Result: The results indicate that there is an algebraically exact structural degeneracy in reionization-history probes, where the ionizing photon rate $\\dot{n}_{\\mathrm{ion}} \\propto f_{\\mathrm{esc}} \\times f_{*,0}$, making all such probes sensitive only to the product of these two parameters. This leads to an intrinsically non-invertible mapping between model parameters and observations, severely limiting reionization-based dark matter probes. Observables sensitive to the spatial topology of ionized regions are the key to breaking this degeneracy.

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the structural degeneracy provides a unified explanation for the scatter among published constraints on reionization. It establishes a framework for interpreting reionization observations and their implications for early galaxy formation and dark matter. The findings suggest that future reionization studies should focus on observables that are sensitive to the spatial topology of ionized regions to break the degeneracy and improve the accuracy of parameter inference.

Abstract: Over the past decade, reionization studies have yielded persistent factor-of-two-to-five disagreements in the inferred ionizing escape fraction $f_{\mathrm{esc}}$ and peak star formation efficiency $f_{*,0}$, compounded by JWST's discovery of unexpectedly bright $z>10$ galaxies. We show that this discrepancy arises from an algebraically exact structural degeneracy: the ionizing photon rate $\dot{n}_{\mathrm{ion}} \propto f_{\mathrm{esc}} \times f_{*,0}$ renders all reionization-history probes, including Thomson optical depth, neutral hydrogen fraction, UV luminosity function, and quasar proximity zones, sensitive only to their product, leading to an intrinsically non-invertible mapping between model parameters and observations. We demonstrate the robustness of this degeneracy using a large suite of N-body simulations of self-interacting dark matter haloes spanning $10^9$-$10^{11} M_\odot$. Despite substantial changes to galaxy-scale structure, observables remain indistinguishable once the effective ionizing emissivity is matched, severely limiting reionization-based dark matter probes. We identify that only observables sensitive to the spatial topology of ionized regions can break this degeneracy. Our results provide a unified explanation for the scatter among published constraints and establish a framework for interpreting reionization observations and their implications for early galaxy formation and dark matter.

</details>


### [5] [Alleviating the Hubble Tension Using $Λ$sCDM Model: A Coupled Dark Energy - Dark Matter Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01904)
*Yismaw Wassie Ambelu,Amare Abebe Gidelew,Solomon Belay Tessema,Shambel Sahlu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper introduces the $Λ_s$CDM model, an interacting dark matter-dark energy model, to address the Hubble tension. The model predicts a value of $H_0 = 71.8_{-0.3}^{+0.4}\mathrm{kms^{-1}Mpc^{-1}}$, reducing the tension with local measurements from about $5σ$ in $Λ$CDM to $1.2σ$. It also suppresses late-time structure growth, providing $σ_8 = 0.744 \pm 0.0185$, which is more consistent with weak lensing surveys. The interaction term is suppressed at high redshift, indicating that the tension alleviation mainly comes from late-time expansion.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to address the significant discrepancy, known as the Hubble tension, between early and late universe measurements of the Hubble constant, $H_0$. This discrepancy poses a challenge to the standard $Λ$CDM cosmological model. The authors propose an interacting dark matter-dark energy model, $Λ_s$CDM, to explore whether such a model can alleviate the Hubble tension while remaining consistent with other cosmological observations.

本文的动机是解决哈勃常数$H_0$在早期宇宙和晚期宇宙测量之间的显著差异，即所谓的哈勃张力。这种差异对标准的$Λ$CDM宇宙学模型提出了挑战。作者提出了一种相互作用的暗物质-暗能量模型$Λ_s$CDM，以探讨该模型是否能在缓解哈勃张力的同时与其他宇宙学观测保持一致。

Method: The method employed in this paper involves the development and analysis of the $Λ_s$CDM model, characterized by a gauge-invariant coupling $Q = ξHρ_{\mathrm{de}}$ and an effective pressure dynamically induced within the dark matter fluid. The authors modify the CLASS Boltzmann code to analyze both the background and perturbation observables. They perform an extensive Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) analysis using the latest cosmological datasets, including observational Hubble parameter data, Planck 2018 CMB compressed likelihood, BAO (from DESI DR2), Pantheon+ Type Ia supernovae, and redshift-space distortion measurements.

本文采用的方法涉及$Λ_s$CDM模型的发展和分析，该模型的特点是一个规范不变耦合$Q = ξHρ_{\mathrm{de}}$以及在暗物质流体中动态诱导的有效压力。作者修改了CLASS玻尔兹曼代码，以分析背景和扰动可观测值。他们使用最新的宇宙学数据集进行了广泛的马尔可夫链蒙特卡罗（MCMC）分析，包括观测哈勃参数数据、Planck 2018 CMB压缩似然、BAO（来自DESI DR2）、Pantheon+ Ia型超新星和红移空间扭曲测量。

Result: The $Λ_s$CDM model predicts a value of $H_0 = 71.8_{-0.3}^{+0.4}\mathrm{kms^{-1}Mpc^{-1}}$, significantly reducing the Hubble tension from about $5σ$ in the standard $Λ$CDM model to $1.2σ$. Additionally, the model suppresses late-time structure growth, resulting in $σ_8 = 0.744 \pm 0.0185$, which is lower than the $Λ$CDM value and aligns better with weak lensing surveys. The interaction term in the model is suppressed at high redshift, implying that the resolution of the Hubble tension primarily stems from late-time expansion rather than early-universe effects.

$Λ_s$CDM模型预测的$H_0 = 71.8_{-0.3}^{+0.4}\mathrm{kms^{-1}Mpc^{-1}}$，显著地将哈勃张力从标准$Λ$CDM模型中的约$5σ$降低到$1.2σ$。此外，该模型抑制了晚期结构的增长，导致$σ_8 = 0.744 \pm 0.0185$，低于$Λ$CDM模型的值，并更好地与弱引力透镜调查结果一致。模型中的相互作用项在高红移时被抑制，表明哈勃张力的缓解主要来自于晚期膨胀而不是早期宇宙效应。

Conclusion: The $Λ_s$CDM model provides a phenomenologically viable framework for addressing key cosmological tensions, particularly the Hubble tension. By modifying the late-time expansion history through the energy transfer from dark matter to dark energy, the model reduces the Hubble tension and aligns with other cosmological observations. The suppression of the interaction term at high redshift suggests that the alleviation of the tension is primarily due to late-time expansion, making $Λ_s$CDM a promising candidate for resolving current cosmological discrepancies.

$Λ_s$CDM模型为解决关键的宇宙学张力提供了一个现象学上可行的框架，特别是哈勃张力。通过暗物质向暗能量的能量转移来修改晚期膨胀历史，该模型减少了哈勃张力，并与其他宇宙学观测结果一致。高红移时相互作用项的抑制表明，张力的缓解主要是由于晚期膨胀，这使得$Λ_s$CDM成为解决当前宇宙学差异的一个有希望的候选者。

Abstract: The considerable difference between early and late universe measurements of the Hubble constant, called the Hubble tension, poses a potential challenge to the standard $Λ$CDM cosmological model. We examine an interacting dark matter-dark energy model, $Λ_s$CDM, characterized by a gauge-invariant coupling $Q = ξHρ_{\mathrm{de}}$ and an effective pressure dynamically induced within the dark matter fluid. Using the CLASS Boltzmann code modified in this work, we analyze both the background and perturbation observables and compute an extensive Markov Chain Monte Carlo analysis with the latest cosmological datasets, including observational Hubble parameter data, Planck 2018 CMB compressed likelihood, BAO (from DESI DR2), Pantheon+ Type Ia supernovae, and redshift-space distortion measurements. The model predicts $H_0 = 71.8_{-0.3}^{+0.4}\mathrm{kms^{-1}Mpc^{-1}}$, reducing the tension with the SH0ES local measurement from about $5σ$ in $Λ$CDM to $1.2σ$ in $Λ_s$CDM. In contrast to the early dark energy model, the resolution emerges from late-time modification of the expansion history induced by the energy transfer from dark matter to dark energy. Moreover, the model suppresses late-time structure growth, providing $σ_8 = 0.744 \pm 0.0185$, lying below the $Λ$CDM value and moves in the direction preferred by weak lensing surveys. Since the interaction term is suppressed at high redshift, the pre-recombination sound horizon departs by less than $1\%$ from its $Λ$CDM value, suggesting that the alleviation of the tension dominantly originates from the late-time expansion rather than early-universe effects. We conclude that $Λ_s$CDM constitutes a phenomenologically viable interacting dark sector framework that addresses key cosmological tensions while remaining consistent with current precision data.
  }

</details>


### [6] [Constraints on Phenomenological Amplitudes of CMB Anisotropy with Multi-Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01946)
*Yang Han,Lu Chen,Guo-Hao Li,Pei-Yuan Xu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper investigates six phenomenological amplitude parameters related to CMB anisotropy and their impact on the $\Lambda$CDM model. The study finds that only the $\Lambda$CDM+$A_{\rm{L}}$ model is favored, with significant deviations from the standard $\Lambda$CDM. No improvement in Hubble and $\sigma_8$ tensions is observed, and ACT DR6 high-$\ell$ data enhances the preference for the $\Lambda$CDM+$A_{\rm{L}}$ model.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the internal consistency of the $\Lambda$CDM model by introducing six phenomenological amplitude parameters, each corresponding to a key effect related to CMB anisotropy. The aim is to address persistent cosmological tensions and small-scale anomalies that challenge the $\Lambda$CDM model. By modifying the CAMB and Cobaya packages, the authors seek to constrain these extended models using different combinations of observational data, including Planck, DESI, PantheonPlus, and ACT.

本文的动机是通过引入六个与CMB各向异性相关的关键效应的表观振幅参数来探索$\Lambda$CDM模型的内部一致性。目标是解决挑战$\Lambda$CDM模型的持续存在的宇宙学张力和小尺度异常。通过修改CAMB和Cobaya软件包，作者试图使用包括Planck、DESI、PantheonPlus和ACT在内的不同观测数据组合来约束这些扩展模型。

Method: The method employed in this paper involves the modification of the CAMB and Cobaya software packages to incorporate six new phenomenological amplitude parameters, $A_{\rm{new}}$, into the $\Lambda$CDM model. These parameters represent the Lensing, Sachs-Wolfe, Doppler, early Integrated Sachs-Wolfe, late Integrated Sachs-Wolfe, and Polarization effects. The modified models are then constrained using two sets of observational data: Planck+DESI+PantheonPlus (PDP) and Planck+ACT+DESI+PantheonPlus (PADP). The Akaike Information Criterion (AIC) is used to evaluate the statistical significance of the results.

本文采用的方法涉及修改CAMB和Cobaya软件包，以将六个新的表观振幅参数$A_{\rm{new}}$纳入$\Lambda$CDM模型中。这些参数分别代表透镜效应、Sachs-Wolfe效应、多普勒效应、早期综合Sachs-Wolfe效应、晚期综合Sachs-Wolfe效应和极化效应。然后使用两组观测数据：Planck+DESI+PantheonPlus（PDP）和Planck+ACT+DESI+PantheonPlus（PADP）来约束修改后的模型。使用Akaike信息准则（AIC）来评估结果的统计显著性。

Result: The results show that only the $\Lambda$CDM+$A_{\rm{L}}$ model is statistically favored, with $A_{\rm{L}}=1.0656_{-0.0303}^{+0.0304}$ from PDP and $A_{\rm{L}}=1.0795_{-0.0289}^{+0.0260}$ from PADP, indicating 2.16$\sigma$ and 3.06$\sigma$ deviations from the $\Lambda$CDM model. Other parameters, such as $A_{\rm{SW}}$, show smaller deviations, while $A_{\rm{lISW}}$ is poorly constrained due to its negligible influence at $\ell \geq 30$. The Hubble and $\sigma_8$ tensions are not alleviated by these one-parameter extensions. Additionally, the inclusion of ACT DR6 high-$\ell$ data strengthens the preference for the $\Lambda$CDM+$A_{\rm{L}}$ model and reduces the uncertainty in $A_{\rm Pol}$ significantly.

结果显示，只有$\Lambda$CDM+$A_{\rm{L}}$模型在统计上受到青睐，PDP给出的$A_{\rm{L}}=1.0656_{-0.0303}^{+0.0304}$，PADP给出的$A_{\rm{L}}=1.0795_{-0.0289}^{+0.0260}$，这表明相对于$\Lambda$CDM模型有2.16$\sigma$和3.06$\sigma$的偏差。其他参数如$A_{\rm{SW}}$显示出较小的偏差，而由于在$\ell \geq 30$时影响微乎其微，$A_{\rm{lISW}}$的约束较差。Hubble和$\sigma_8$张力并未通过这些单参数扩展得到缓解。此外，加入ACT DR6高$\ell$数据增强了对$\Lambda$CDM+$A_{\rm{L}}$模型的偏好，并显著减少了$A_{\rm Pol}$的不确定性。

Conclusion: The conclusion of this paper is that among the six phenomenological amplitude parameters introduced, only the $\Lambda$CDM+$A_{\rm{L}}$ model shows a statistically significant deviation from the standard $\Lambda$CDM model. The inclusion of ACT DR6 high-$\ell$ data further supports this result and highlights the importance of ground-based high-$\ell$ observations for future CMB analyses. However, no significant improvement in the Hubble and $\sigma_8$ tensions was found within these one-parameter extended scenarios.

本文的结论是，在引入的六个表观振幅参数中，只有$\Lambda$CDM+$A_{\rm{L}}$模型显示出相对于标准$\Lambda$CDM模型的统计显著偏差。加入ACT DR6高$\ell$数据进一步支持了这一结果，并强调了基于地面的高$\ell$观测对于未来CMB分析的重要性。然而，在这些单参数扩展情景中，Hubble和$\sigma_8$张力没有显著改善。

Abstract: Cosmic microwave background anisotropies encode crucial information about the early Universe and fundamental cosmological physics. Although the standard $Λ$CDM model provides a successful description of cosmic evolution, persistent cosmological tensions and subtle small-scale anomalies still challenge its internal consistency. In this paper, we investigate six phenomenological amplitude parameters $A_{\rm{new}}$ (new=L, SW, Dop, eISW, lISW, Pol) corresponding to the key effects related to CMB anisotropy: the Lensing, Sachs-Wolfe, Doppler, early Integrated Sachs-Wolfe, late Integrated Sachs-Wolfe, and Polarization effects, respectively. Using modified CAMB and Cobaya packages, we constrain the $Λ$CDM$+A_{\rm{new}}$ models with two data combinations: Planck+DESI+PantheonPlus (PDP) and Planck+ACT+DESI+PantheonPlus (PADP). Only the $Λ$CDM+$A_{\rm{L}}$ is favored by AIC, with $A_{\rm{L}}=1.0656_{-0.0303}^{+0.0304}$ from PDP and $A_{\rm{L}}=1.0795_{-0.0289}^{+0.0260}$ from PADP, which implies 2.16$σ$ and 3.06$σ$ deviation from the $Λ$CDM model; values of $A_{\rm{SW}}$ show 1.21$σ$ and 1.96$σ$ deviations to 1; $A_{\rm{lISW}}$ is poorly constrained because the lISW effect has negligible influence at $\ell \geq 30$; and others are consistent with the $Λ$CDM model. Moreover, no noticeable improvement on the Hubble and $σ_8$ tensions is found within these one-parameter extended scenarios. ACT DR6 high-$\ell$ data strengthens the $Λ$CDM$+A_{\rm{L}}$ preference over the $Λ$CDM model, and reduces $A_{\rm Pol}$ uncertainty by more than one order of magnitude, highlighting the importance of ground-based high-$\ell$ observations for future CMB analyses.

### [7] [Constraints on Halo Gas Profiles from Joint kSZ and Galaxy Clustering Analysis of ACT DR6 and CMASS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01963)
*Shaohong Li,Yi Zheng*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper measures the kinetic Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (kSZ) signal using CMASS galaxies and ACT DR6 maps, achieving a high signal-to-noise ratio and rejecting the no-kSZ hypothesis. The observed kSZ signal is more extended than in simulations, suggesting stronger baryonic feedback in the real Universe.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to measure the kinetic Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (kSZ) signal by combining the pairwise kSZ effect and galaxy clustering data. This joint analysis aims to break degeneracies between the optical depth and other nuisance parameters, allowing for a more accurate reconstruction of the halo optical depth profile as a function of aperture scale. Additionally, the study seeks to compare the observed kSZ signal with that from simulations to infer the strength and effects of baryonic feedback in the real Universe.

本文的动机是通过结合成对的kSZ效应和星系团聚数据来测量动能Sunyaev-Zel'dovich（kSZ）信号。这种联合分析旨在打破光学深度和其他干扰参数之间的简并，从而能够更准确地重建光晕光学深度剖面作为视场尺度的函数。此外，该研究还试图将观测到的kSZ信号与模拟信号进行比较，以推断真实宇宙中重子反馈的强度和影响。

Method: The method involves a joint analysis of the pairwise kSZ effect and galaxy clustering using CMASS galaxies and ACT DR6 maps. By breaking the degeneracies between the optical depth and nuisance parameters, the researchers reconstruct the halo optical depth profile as a function of aperture scale. The same analysis pipeline is applied to the Websky simulation to compare the observed and simulated kSZ signals, which helps in understanding the role of baryonic feedback.

该方法涉及使用CMASS星系和ACT DR6地图对成对kSZ效应和星系团聚进行联合分析。通过打破光学深度和其他干扰参数之间的简并，研究人员重建了光晕光学深度剖面作为视场尺度的函数。同样的分析流程应用于Websky模拟，以比较观测到的和模拟的kSZ信号，这有助于理解重子反馈的作用。

Result: The kSZ signal reaches its highest signal-to-noise ratio of 7.2 at an aperture radius of $θ_{\rm AP} = 2$ arcmin, and the full profile rejects the no-kSZ hypothesis at $8.7σ$. The observed kSZ signal is found to be more extended than in the Websky simulation, indicating that baryonic feedback in the real Universe may be stronger and more efficient in redistributing gas to larger radii than modeled in the simulation.

kSZ信号在视场半径为$θ_{\rm AP} = 2$弧分时达到最高的信噪比7.2，并且整个剖面在$8.7σ$水平上拒绝了无kSZ假设。观察到的kSZ信号比Websky模拟中的信号更为扩展，表明真实宇宙中的重子反馈可能比模拟中更强，更有效地将气体重新分布到更大的半径上。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the joint analysis of the kSZ effect and galaxy clustering provides a robust measurement of the kSZ signal, with the observed signal being more extended than in simulations. This suggests that baryonic feedback in the real Universe may be stronger and redistribute gas to larger radii more efficiently than currently modeled. However, further investigation is needed to account for residual systematic effects and modeling uncertainties.

研究结论指出，kSZ效应和星系团聚的联合分析提供了对kSZ信号的稳健测量，观察到的信号比模拟中的信号更为扩展。这表明真实宇宙中的重子反馈可能比当前模型中更强，更有效地将气体重新分布到更大的半径上。然而，还需要进一步的研究来考虑剩余的系统效应和建模不确定性。

Abstract: We measure the kinetic Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (kSZ) signal through a joint analysis of the pairwise kSZ effect and galaxy clustering using CMASS galaxies and ACT DR6 maps. This approach breaks degeneracies between the optical depth and nuisance parameters, enabling a reconstruction of the halo optical depth profile as a function of aperture scale. The kSZ signal reaches its highest signal-to-noise ratio of 7.2 at an aperture radius of $θ_{\rm AP} = 2$ arcmin, while the full profile rejects the no-kSZ hypothesis at $8.7σ$. Applying the same analysis pipeline to the Websky simulation, we find that the observed optical depth profile is somewhat more extended than the simulated one. This difference suggests that baryonic feedback in the real Universe may be stronger and redistribute gas to larger radii more efficiently than modeled in the simulation, although residual systematic effects and modeling uncertainties remain to be further investigated.

<details>

Additionally, it addresses current challenges, including the Hubble tension and $\sigma_8$ discrepancies, and discusses the future of cosmology with upcoming surveys like DESI.

The review also identifies current tensions in cosmological parameters, particularly the Hubble tension and $\sigma_8$ discrepancies, and discusses the potential of future surveys like DESI to resolve these issues.

该综述的结果包括从大爆炸模型的确立到当前$\Lambda$CDM范式的宇宙学演变的详细时间线。关键的观测里程碑，如COBE发现的CMB波动、WMAP和Planck测量的平坦宇宙以及Ia型超新星观测到的宇宙加速膨胀都得到了强调。该综述还确定了当前宇宙学参数中的张力，特别是哈勃张力和$\sigma_8$差异，并讨论了未来DESI等调查解决这些问题的潜力。

Conclusion: The conclusion emphasizes the profound paradigm shift from a model based on standard physics to a dynamical cosmos dominated by dark matter and dark energy. The current tensions in cosmological parameters, such as the Hubble tension and $\sigma_8$ discrepancies, suggest that new physics beyond the $\Lambda$CDM model may be required. Future large-scale structure surveys, like DESI, will play a crucial role in resolving these tensions and advancing our understanding of the cosmos.

结论强调了从基于标准物理的模型到以暗物质和暗能量为主的动态宇宙的重大范式转变。当前宇宙学参数中的张力，如哈勃张力和$\sigma_8$差异，表明可能需要超越$\Lambda$CDM模型的新物理。未来的大型结构调查，如DESI，将在解决这些张力和推进我们对宇宙的理解方面发挥关键作用。

Abstract: This paper presents a necessarily incomplete review of the evolution of cosmology since the first Astro/Cosmo Moriond meeting in 1981. I trace the journey from the classical Big Bang model based on three pillars -- universe expansion, primordial nucleosynthesis, and the cosmic microwave background -- to the modern $Λ$CDM paradigm and the discovery of cosmic acceleration. I discuss major observational milestones: the COBE discovery of CMB fluctuations, the CMB measurements of the flat universe, the pivotal discovery of accelerated expansion through Type Ia supernovae and the emergence of precision cosmology with Planck. I review current tensions in cosmological parameters, particularly the Hubble tension and $\s8$ discrepancies, and discuss future prospects from large-scale structure surveys like DESI. The emergence of ``Big Bang 2.0'' reflects the profound paradigm shift from a model based on standard physics to a dynamical cosmos dominated by dark matter and dark energy, the description of which requires a physics that has yet to be developed and validated.

### [9] [Constraints on the baryon density from fast radio bursts using a non-parametric reconstruction of the Hubble parameter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01990)
*Lázaro L. Sales,Klecio E. L. de Farias,Amilcar R. Queiroz,Rafael A. Batista,Bruno W. Ribeiro,Raiff H. Santos*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study uses 130 well-localized fast radio bursts (FRBs) to constrain the physical baryon density $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ and the astrophysical contribution from host galaxies. A non-parametric reconstruction of the Hubble parameter $H(z)$ is used, and a Bayesian analysis infers $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ and parameters of a log-normal host-galaxy distribution. The results are consistent with Big Bang Nucleosynthesis and Planck CMB determinations, and future FRB samples could reduce the uncertainty on $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ to the sub-percent level.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to use fast radio bursts (FRBs) as a new probe to constrain the physical baryon density $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ and the astrophysical contributions from their host galaxies. By combining FRB dispersion measures with a non-parametric reconstruction of the expansion history, the authors aim to provide a robust method for constraining both cosmological and astrophysical parameters. This approach can potentially complement other low-redshift probes of the baryon density.

本文的动机是利用快速射电暴（FRBs）作为新的探针来约束物理重子密度 $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ 及其宿主星系的天体物理贡献。通过将FRB色散测度与膨胀历史的非参数重构相结合，作者旨在提供一种稳健的方法来约束宇宙学和天体物理学参数。这种方法有可能补充其他低红移的重子密度探测手段。

Method: The authors use a sample of 130 well-localized FRBs to constrain the physical baryon density $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ and the astrophysical contribution from host galaxies. They employ a non-parametric reconstruction of the Hubble parameter $H(z)$ using the \texttt{ReFANN} neural-network framework, based on cosmic chronometer data. A Bayesian analysis is then performed to jointly infer $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ and the parameters of a log-normal host-galaxy distribution, including its median $e^\mu$ and logarithmic scatter $\sigma_{\rm host}$. Both real FRB data and a mock catalog are used in the analysis.

作者使用130个精确定位的快速射电暴（FRBs）样本，来约束物理重子密度 $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ 和宿主星系的天体物理贡献。他们基于宇宙时钟数据，使用 \texttt{ReFANN} 神经网络框架进行哈勃参数 $H(z)$ 的非参数重构。然后，通过贝叶斯分析共同推断重子密度 $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ 以及对数正态宿主星系分布的参数，包括其中位数 $e^\mu$ 和对数离散度 $\sigma_{\rm host}$。分析中同时使用了真实的FRB数据和模拟目录。

Result: For the real sample, the authors obtain $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2=0.02236\pm0.00090$, $e^\mu=178.15^{+16.51}_{-16.97}~\mathrm{pc}\,\mathrm{cm}^{-3}$, and $\sigma_{\rm host}=0.794^{+0.064}_{-0.067}$. For the mock catalog, they find $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2=0.02248\pm0.00018$, $e^\mu=182.36^{+6.83}_{-6.48}~\mathrm{pc}\,\mathrm{cm}^{-3}$, and $\sigma_{\rm host}=0.711^{+0.024}_{-0.025}$. The baryon density constraint from the real FRB sample is in excellent agreement with both Big Bang Nucleosynthesis and Planck CMB determinations, differing from their central values by only $\simeq 0.05\%$. The mock analysis further illustrates the potential of future FRB samples, reducing the uncertainty on $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ to the sub-percent level while remaining statistically consistent with early-Universe constraints.

对于真实样本，作者得到 $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2=0.02236\pm0.00090$, $e^\mu=178.15^{+16.51}_{-16.97}~\mathrm{pc}\,\mathrm{cm}^{-3}$, 和 $\sigma_{\rm host}=0.794^{+0.064}_{-0.067}$。对于模拟目录，他们发现 $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2=0.02248\pm0.00018$, $e^\mu=182.36^{+6.83}_{-6.48}~\mathrm{pc}\,\mathrm{cm}^{-3}$, 和 $\sigma_{\rm host}=0.711^{+0.024}_{-0.025}$。真实FRB样本的重子密度约束与大爆炸核合成和普朗克CMB测定结果非常一致，仅相差约 $\simeq 0.05\%$。模拟分析进一步说明了未来FRB样本的潜力，可以将 $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ 的不确定性降低到亚百分比水平，同时在统计上与早期宇宙约束保持一致。

Conclusion: The findings show that combining FRB dispersion measures with a non-parametric reconstruction of the expansion history provides a robust pathway to constrain both cosmological and astrophysical parameters. The baryon density constraint from the real FRB sample is in excellent agreement with both Big Bang Nucleosynthesis and Planck CMB determinations, and future FRB samples have the potential to reduce the uncertainty on $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ to the sub-percent level, establishing FRBs as a complementary low-redshift probe of the baryon density.

研究结果表明，将FRB色散测度与膨胀历史的非参数重构相结合，为约束宇宙学和天体物理学参数提供了一种稳健的途径。真实FRB样本的重子密度约束与大爆炸核合成和普朗克CMB测定结果非常一致，未来FRB样本有潜力将 $\Omega_{\rm b}h^2$ 的不确定性降低到亚百分比水平，从而确立FRBs作为低红移重子密度的互补探测手段。

Abstract: In this study, we use a sample of 130 well-localized fast radio bursts (FRBs) to constrain the physical baryon density $Ω_{\rm b}h^2$, and the astrophysical contribution from host galaxies. The cosmological dependence entering the intergalactic dispersion measure is described through a non-parametric reconstruction of the Hubble parameter $H(z)$ obtained from cosmic chronometer data using the \texttt{ReFANN} neural-network framework, independently of the FRB sample. Within a Bayesian analysis, we jointly infer $Ω_{\rm b}h^2$ and the parameters of a log-normal host-galaxy distribution, namely its median $e^μ$ and logarithmic scatter $σ_{\rm host}$, using both real FRB data and a mock catalog. For the real sample, we obtain $Ω_{\rm b}h^2=0.02236\pm0.00090$, $e^μ=178.15^{+16.51}_{-16.97}~\mathrm{pc}\,\mathrm{cm}^{-3}$, and $σ_{\rm host}=0.794^{+0.064}_{-0.067}$. For the mock catalog, we find $Ω_{\rm b}h^2=0.02248\pm0.00018$, $e^μ=182.36^{+6.83}_{-6.48}~\mathrm{pc}\,\mathrm{cm}^{-3}$, and $σ_{\rm host}=0.711^{+0.024}_{-0.025}$. The baryon density constraint from the real FRB sample is in excellent agreement with both Big Bang Nucleosynthesis and Planck CMB determinations, differing from their central values by only $\simeq 0.05\%$. The mock analysis further illustrates the potential of future FRB samples, reducing the uncertainty on $Ω_{\rm b}h^2$ to the sub-percent level while remaining statistically consistent with early-Universe constraints. Our findings show that combining FRB dispersion measures with a non-parametric reconstruction of the expansion history provides a robust pathway to constrain both cosmological and astrophysical parameters, establishing FRBs as a complementary low-redshift probe of the baryon density.

*Kritti Sharma,Vikram Ravi,Dhayaa Anbajagane,William R. Coulton,Elisabeth Krause,Nico Schuster,Alice Pisani,Samuel McCarty,Liam Connor,Simone Ferraro,Nico Hamaus,Pranjal R. S*

Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Abstract: The pristine underdense patches of the Universe, cosmic voids, are powerful cosmological laboratories, uniquely sensitive to dark energy, modified gravity, and neutrino masses, yet their baryonic content remains uncharacterized. We present the first observational constraint on baryon underdensity in void interiors, exploiting the dispersion measures (DMs) of Fast Radio Bursts (FRBs) as tracers of the free electron column, independent of gas phase, temperature, and metallicity. By stacking 3,455 sightlines from CHIME/FRB on 1,288 SDSS BOSS voids over redshifts $0.2 < z < 0.7$, we measure a DM deficit toward void centers at $3.2σ$ significance, establishing that diffuse baryons inhabit the emptiest corners of the cosmic web at a suppressed level. The measured signal amplitude is consistent with an effective Universe model built directly from the observed galaxy underdensity in these voids, and a baryonic model calibrated to the FRB DM-redshift relation ($α_v = 1.80 \pm 0.87$). A uniform-density void model yields an electron density contrast of $δ_\mathrm{e,v} = -0.58 \pm 0.30$, implying a $\sim 60$% underdensity of baryons in void interiors relative to the cosmic mean. Jointly interpreting our FRB measurement with existing stacks of the thermal Sunyaev-Zel'dovich effect on voids further constrains the mean void gas temperature to $T_\mathrm{e} \lesssim (1.1 \pm 0.7) \times 10^6$ K, pointing to a warm-hot diffuse phase, consistent with hydrodynamical simulation predictions. With forthcoming FRB (CHORD, DSA, SKA) and galaxy (DESI, LSST, Euclid, PFS-Subaru, SPHEREx, Roman) surveys, set to expand both samples by orders of magnitude, this approach opens a new window onto tomographic baryon mapping, with direct implications for feedback models governing gas expulsion into low-density environments, and for the use of cosmic voids to extract cosmological constraints.

### [11] [Constraints on Ultralight Scalar and Dark Photon Dark Matter from PPTA-DR3 and EPTA-DR2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02172)

TL;DR: The paper uses Pulsar Timing Array (PTA) data to search for ultralight dark matter (ULDM) signals, focusing on scalar ULDM and dark photon dark matter (DPDM). No significant evidence for ULDM was found, but the analysis placed 95% confidence-level upper limits on relevant parameters. The constraints from PPTA-DR3 show improvements over earlier data and are consistent with other PTAs. The EPTA-DR2 and PPTA-DR3 provide comparable bounds on DPDM.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The cold dark matter model, while successful at large scales, faces challenges at sub-galactic scales. Ultralight dark matter (ULDM), with particle masses around $10^{-22} \mathrm{eV}$, is a promising solution to these issues. Pulsar Timing Arrays (PTAs) designed to detect nanohertz gravitational waves can also probe ULDM signals effectively.\n\n冷暗物质模型在大尺度上成功描述了宇宙，但在亚星系尺度上遇到了挑战。超轻暗物质（ULDM），其粒子质量约为$10^{-22} \mathrm{eV}$，为这些问题提供了一个有希望的解决方案。设计用于探测纳赫兹引力波的脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）也可以有效探测ULDM信号。

Result: No statistically significant evidence for ULDM has been found, leading to the placement of 95% confidence-level upper limits on the relevant parameters. For scalar ULDM, the scenario where ULDM constitutes all of dark matter is not excluded. The PPTA-DR3 constraints show significant improvements over the earlier PPTA-DR2 across most of the mass range and are consistent with recent uncorrelated limits from other PTAs. Conclusion: The study provides new constraints on ULDM and DPDM using PTA data, with significant improvements over previous results. While no direct evidence for ULDM was found, the analysis places important limits on the possible parameter space, contributing to the ongoing efforts to understand the nature of dark matter.\n\n该研究使用PTA数据提供了关于ULDM和DPDM的新约束，相对于之前的结果有了显著改进。虽然没有直接找到ULDM的证据，但分析对可能的参数空间设置了重要限制，有助于理解暗物质的本质。

Abstract: The cold dark matter model successfully describes the Universe on large scales, yet faces challenges at sub-galactic scales. Ultralight dark matter (ULDM), with particle masses around $10^{-22} \mathrm{eV}$, offers a promising solution to these small-scale issues. Pulsar Timing Arrays (PTAs), designed to detect nanohertz gravitational waves, can also provide a sensitive probe for ULDM signals. In this work, we perform a Bayesian search for ULDM using PTA data sets, focusing on two types of signals: the oscillatory gravitational potential from scalar ULDM and the fifth-force interaction mediated by dark photon dark matter (DPDM). We incorporate pulsar distances in the analysis to better model the ULDM density. No statistically significant evidence for ULDM has been found, therefore we place 95% confidence-level upper limits on the relevant parameters. For scalar ULDM, our analysis does not exclude the scenario in which ULDM constitutes all of dark matter. The constraints from PPTA-DR3 show significant improvements over the earlier PPTA-DR2 (2018 Preview) across most of the mass range, and are consistent with the recent uncorrelated limits from other PTAs. We also present for the first time the DPDM constraints using EPTA data. The obtained bounds on the DPDM from the EPTA-DR2 and PPTA-DR3 are comparable to existing constraints.

</details>


### [12] [Beyond collective fluctuations: probing micro-image swarms in lensed quasars with intensity interferometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02181)
*Ashish Kumar Meena,Prasenjit Saha*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper explores the use of intensity interferometry to determine the size of micro-image swarms in strongly lensed quasar images, focusing on QSO 2237+0305 and PS J0147+4630. The authors suggest that with technical advancements, observing these micro-image swarms is feasible, especially for the brightest lensed quasars.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation behind this work is to unlock the hidden information within micro-image swarms, which are currently observable only through collective intensity fluctuations. By using intensity interferometry (the Hanbury Brown & Twiss effect), the study aims to determine the size of these micro-image swarms and gain insights into the stellar and compact dark matter mass functions within the swarm.

这项工作的动机是解锁微图像群中的隐藏信息，这些信息目前只能通过集体强度波动来观察。通过使用强度干涉测量（汉伯里布朗和特威斯效应），研究旨在确定这些微图像群的大小，并深入了解群内的恒星和致密暗物质质量函数。

Method: The method involves the application of intensity interferometry to analyze the visibility space features of micro-image swarms in lensed quasar images. Specifically, the study focuses on two of the brightest lensed quasars, QSO 2237+0305 and PS J0147+4630, and examines both macro-minimum and macro-saddle-point images. The analysis aims to determine the size of the micro-image swarms and to infer the underlying mass distribution.

该方法涉及应用强度干涉测量来分析透镜类星体图像中微图像群的可见空间特征。具体而言，研究重点关注两个最亮的透镜类星体QSO 2237+0305和PS J0147+4630，并检查宏观最小值和宏观鞍点图像。分析旨在确定微图像群的大小并推断其背后的质量分布。

Result: The results indicate that by using intensity interferometry, it is possible to observe the micro-image swarms and to determine their size. The study shows that the visibility space features of the micro-image swarms can be used to infer the underlying stellar and compact dark matter mass functions. The authors also argue that with ongoing and expected technical advances, such observations are plausible, particularly for the brightest lensed quasars.

结果表明，通过使用强度干涉测量，可以观察到微图像群并确定它们的大小。研究表明，微图像群的可见空间特征可用于推断其背后的恒星和致密暗物质质量函数。作者还指出，随着正在进行和预期的技术进步，这种观测是可行的，特别是对于最亮的透镜类星体。

Conclusion: The conclusion of the paper is that intensity interferometry offers a promising technique for determining the size of micro-image swarms in lensed quasar images. This approach could provide valuable insights into the stellar and compact dark matter mass functions, and with future technological advancements, such observations may become feasible for the brightest lensed quasars.

论文的结论是，强度干涉测量为确定透镜类星体图像中微图像群的大小提供了一种有前景的技术。这种方法可以为了解恒星和致密暗物质质量函数提供有价值的见解，并且随着未来技术的进步，对于最亮的透镜类星体，这种观测可能变得可行。

Abstract: Each strongly lensed image of a quasar behind a lensing galaxy (or galaxy cluster) is composed of a swarm of micro-images. This is a result of microlensing due to stellar-scale substructure in the lens. The presence of microlenses forms a network of micro-caustics, and a source transiting these micro-caustics gives rise to variation in observed strongly lensed images. These micro-image swarms are currently observable only through collective intensity fluctuations, which hide the underlying information on the stellar (and compact dark matter, if any) mass functions within the swarm. To unlock the information present in micro-image swarms, it is necessary to explore new techniques. In this work, we study the prospects of determining the micro-image swarm size in lensed quasar images using the intensity interferometry (i.e., the Hanbury Brown & Twiss effect). We consider QSO 2237+0305 and PS J0147+4630, two of the brightest lens quasars in the sky, and study micro-image swarm features in visibility space for both macro-minimum and macro-saddle-point images. At the end, we argue that, with ongoing and expected technical advances, observations of micro-image swarms are plausible, at least for the brightest lensed quasars.

</details>


### [13] [Investigating cosmic distance duality and dark energy evolution through intermediate and high-z probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02428)
*Anna Chiara Alfano*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper investigates deviations from the cosmic distance duality relation using various parameterizations and observational data, finding no significant violation of duality but a slight preference for flat scenarios. It also addresses the $H_0$ tension, with different preferred values depending on the data sets used.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to test the validity of the cosmic distance duality relation (CDDR) using multiple parameterizations and a wide range of observational data, including Hubble data, galaxy clusters, type Ia supernovae, DESI data, and gamma-ray bursts. The goal is to derive constraints on the parameters and to investigate any potential violations of the CDDR.

动机是使用多种参数化方法和广泛的观测数据（包括哈勃数据、星系团、Ia型超新星、DESI数据和伽马射线暴）来测试宇宙距离对偶关系（CDDR）的有效性。目的是推导参数的约束，并研究任何可能违反CDDR的情况。

Method: The authors use five different parameterizations to model deviations from the CDDR: Taylor expansion, power-law parameterization, logarithmic correction, (2;1) Padé polynomial, and second order Chebyshev parameterization. They then apply Monte-Carlo Markov chain analyses with the Metropolis Hastings algorithm to constrain the parameters using the observational data.

作者使用五种不同的参数化方法来模拟偏离CDDR的情况：泰勒展开、幂律参数化、对数修正、(2;1) 帕德多项式和二阶切比雪夫参数化。然后，他们应用蒙特卡洛马尔可夫链分析与Metropolis Hastings算法，利用观测数据来约束参数。

Result: The analysis shows no significant violation of the CDDR, and model selection criteria favor flat scenarios, although a slight curvature is not entirely ruled out. For the $H_0$ tension, the study finds a preference at 1-$\sigma$ for $h^R_0=0.730\pm0.010$ from supernovae when excluding DESI data, and for $h^P_0=0.674\pm 0.005$ from Planck when including DESI and gamma-ray bursts.

分析显示没有显著违反CDDR的情况，模型选择标准倾向于平坦场景，尽管轻微的曲率并未完全排除。对于$H_0$张力问题，研究发现，在排除DESI数据时，从超新星得到的1-$\sigma$偏好值为$h^R_0=0.730\pm0.010$；而在包含DESI和伽马射线暴时，从Planck得到的偏好值为$h^P_0=0.674\pm 0.005$。

Conclusion: The study concludes that there is no significant evidence for a violation of the cosmic distance duality relation, and that the preferred cosmological models are flat. The results also provide insights into the $H_0$ tension, suggesting that different data sets can lead to slightly different preferred values for the Hubble constant.

研究结论是没有显著证据表明违反了宇宙距离对偶关系，且首选的宇宙学模型是平坦的。结果还提供了关于$H_0$张力的见解，表明不同的数据集可能导致略微不同的哈勃常数值偏好。

Abstract: We investigate deviations from the cosmic distance duality relation adopting model-dependent and -independent approaches using i) a Taylor expansion, ii) a power-law parameterization, iii) a logarithmic correction, iv) a (2;1) Padé polynomial and v) a second order Chebyshev parameterization. We derive constraints on all parameters using observational Hubble data, galaxy clusters, type Ia supernovae, DESI data and gamma-ray bursts. Through Monte-Carlo Markov chain analyses adopting the Metropolis Hastings algorithm, we find no significant violation of duality, then model selection criteria favor flat scenarios even though a slight curvature is not totally ruled out. For the $H_0$ tension we find a preference at $1$-$σ$ for $h^R_0=0.730\pm0.010$ from supernovae when dropping DESI data and for $h^P_0=0.674\pm 0.005$ from Planck when using DESI and gamma-ray bursts.

Nesseris,F. Oppizzi,F. Pace,D. Paoletti,F. Passalacqua,K. Paterson,C. Pattison,R. Paviot,D. Potter,G. W. Pratt,S. Quai,M. Radovich,W. Roster,S. Sacquegna,M. Sahlén,D. B. Sanders,A. Schneider,D. Sciotti,E. Sellentin,S. Serjeant,I. Szapudi,K. Tanidis,F. Tarsitano,G. Testera,R. Teyssier,S. Tosi,A. Troja,C. Uhlemann,C. Valieri,A. Venhola,D. Vergani,G. Verza,S. Vinciguerra,M. von Wietersheim-Kramsta,N. A. Walton,L. Wang,A. H. Wright*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper introduces CosmoPostProcess, a forward-modelling algorithm that corrects stacked surface-density profiles of galaxy clusters in Euclid data. It accounts for selection systematics, baryonic effects, and miscentring, providing radial profile corrections with uncertainties.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a robust method for correcting the systematic biases in the stacked surface-density profiles of galaxy clusters selected by richness in the Euclid survey. This is crucial for accurate cosmological analyses, especially at higher redshifts where the projection-induced selection bias becomes more significant.

Method: The method involves using $N$-body simulations, painting galaxies with a halo-occupation model, and emulating survey detection and richness assignment. A novel estimate of optical cluster centers is implemented and validated against Euclid pipelines. Baryonic effects are included through a correction calibrated on hydrodynamical simulations. The algorithm assesses selection-bias contributions by varying cosmology and the mass--richness relation.

Result: The results show that the baryon-corrected excess surface density agrees within $2\%$ over $r \in [0.1, 5] h^{-1} \mathrm{Mpc}$. Projection-induced selection bias enhances the stacked profile near the one-halo to two-halo transition, peaking at about $1 h^{-1} \mathrm{Mpc}$ with an amplitude of $20-40\%$, depending on richness and redshift. The effect is mild at low and intermediate redshift ($z \lesssim 0.7$) but becomes more relevant at higher redshift ($z \gtrsim 0.7$).

Conclusion: CosmoPostProcess provides a framework for delivering radial profile corrections with uncertainties, combining projection-induced selection bias, baryonic physics, and miscentring, to control systematics in Euclid DR1 cluster cosmology.

Abstract: We present \texttt{CosmoPostProcess}, a simulation-based forward-modelling algorithm calibrated to reproduce Euclid optical cluster observables. Its main deliverable is a correction for stacked surface-density profiles, binned in richness and redshift, accounting for selection systematics in richness-selected samples relative to unbiased references. We focus on the Euclid richness definition foreseen for cosmological analyses, which does not apply a colour selection; red-sequence richness is not considered. The algorithm processes $N$-body simulations by painting galaxies with a halo-occupation model and emulating survey detection and richness assignment. We also implement a novel estimate of optical cluster centres from projected galaxy densities, validated against Euclid pipelines. Baryonic effects are included through a correction calibrated on hydrodynamical simulations; the baryon-corrected excess surface density agrees within \(2\,\%\) over \(r\in[0.1,\,5]\,h^{-1}\,\mathrm{Mpc}\). Selection-bias contributions are assessed by varying cosmology and the mass--richness relation. Projection-induced selection bias follows a robust pattern: correlated large-scale structure projected along the line of sight enhances the stacked profile near the one-halo to two-halo transition, peaking at about \(1\,h^{-1}\,\mathrm{Mpc}\) with an amplitude of \(20\!-\!40\,\%\), depending on richness and redshift. The effect is mild at low and intermediate redshift ($z\lesssim0.7$), at the few-percent level, but becomes more relevant at higher redshift ($z\gtrsim0.7$). Baryonic modifications remain sub-dominant outside the core, at about \(2\,\%\) beyond \(r\gtrsim0.3\,h^{-1}\,\mathrm{Mpc}\). The framework delivers radial profile corrections with uncertainties, combining projection-induced selection bias, baryonic physics, and miscentring, to control systematics in Euclid DR1 cluster cosmology. (abridged)

### [15] [Tracing Primordial Gravitational Waves via non-Gaussian Signatures of Halo Bias](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02882)
*Mariam Abdelaziz,Pritha Bari,Sabino Matarrese,Angelo Ricciardone*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper explores the impact of primordial gravitational waves (PGWs) on the large-scale clustering of dark matter halos, focusing on the non-Gaussianity induced by these waves. It derives a scale-dependent bias correction for halos, which can be significant for rare, high-redshift halos. This effect offers a new way to probe PGWs and provides additional insights into the inflationary epoch.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to investigate the influence of primordial gravitational waves (PGWs) on the large-scale structure, particularly through their generation of scalar density perturbations at second order. The study aims to understand how this tensor-induced non-Gaussianity (NG) affects the clustering of dark matter halos, especially in scenarios with a peaked primordial tensor spectrum. The goal is to use halo bias as a novel probe of PGWs, offering a complementary method to study the inflationary period. \n\n研究的动机是探讨原初引力波（PGWs）对大尺度结构的影响，特别是通过它们在二阶产生的标量密度扰动。该研究旨在理解这种张量诱导的非高斯性（NG）如何影响暗物质晕的聚集，特别是在具有尖峰原初张量谱的情况下。目标是利用晕偏置作为探测PGWs的新方法，为研究暴胀时期提供补充手段。

Method: The method involves deriving the leading scale-dependent contribution to halo bias from the bispectrum of the induced density field due to PGWs. The analysis focuses on inflationary scenarios with a peaked primordial tensor spectrum. The authors calculate the bias correction for both massive low-redshift halos and rare, high-redshift halos. The calculations are based on the quadratic nature of the induced density contrast in the tensor field, which leads to intrinsic non-Gaussianity. \n\n方法涉及从由于PGWs引起的密度场的双谱中导出晕偏置的主要尺度依赖贡献。分析集中在具有尖峰原初张量谱的暴胀情景上。作者计算了对于大质量低红移晕和罕见高红移晕的偏置修正。计算基于张量场中诱导密度对比度的二次性质，这导致了内在的非高斯性。

Result: The results show that the tensor-induced non-Gaussianity can yield a percent-level bias correction for massive low-redshift halos. For rare, high-redshift halos at $z=7$, the bias correction can reach an $\mathcal{O}(1)$ modulation. The signature of this effect has a distinct scale dependence that is not captured by standard primordial non-Gaussianity (PNG) templates. \n\n结果表明，张量诱导的非高斯性可以为大质量低红移晕产生百分比级别的偏置修正。对于$z=7$的罕见高红移晕，偏置修正可以达到$\mathcal{O}(1)$的调制。这种效应的特征具有独特的尺度依赖性，这是标准原初非高斯性（PNG）模板所无法捕捉到的。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the tensor-induced non-Gaussianity from PGWs can significantly affect the large-scale clustering of dark matter halos, particularly for rare, high-redshift halos. This effect provides a novel probe of PGWs and offers a complementary window into the inflationary epoch. The distinct scale dependence of the bias correction suggests that it can be used to distinguish between different models of inflation. \n\n结论是，来自PGWs的张量诱导非高斯性可以显著影响暗物质晕的大尺度聚集，特别是对于罕见的高红移晕。这种效应提供了探测PGWs的新方法，并为研究暴胀时期提供了补充窗口。偏置修正的独特尺度依赖性表明，它可以用来区分不同的暴胀模型。

Abstract: Primordial gravitational waves (PGWs) generate scalar density perturbations at second order. Since the induced density contrast is quadratic in the tensor field, it is intrinsically non-Gaussian. We study the imprint of this tensor-induced non-Gaussianity (NG) on the large-scale clustering of dark matter halos through its correction to halo bias. Focusing on inflationary scenarios with a peaked primordial tensor spectrum, we derive the leading scale-dependent contribution sourced by the bispectrum of the induced density field. While yielding a percent-level bias correction for massive low-redshift halos, this effect can reach an $\mathcal{O}(1)$ modulation for rare, high-redshift halos at $z=7$. Notably, the resulting signature exhibits a distinct scale dependence that is not captured by standard primordial non-Gaussianity (PNG) templates. Our results establish halo bias as a novel probe of PGWs through their imprint on the large-scale structure, providing a complementary window into the inflationary epoch.

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [16] [Nuclear geometry driven symmetry plane correlations in OO and Ne--Ne collisions at the Large Hadron Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00866)
*Suraj Prasad,Raghunath Sahoo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The study examines symmetry-plane correlations (SPCs) in Oxygen--Oxygen (OO) and Neon--Neon (Ne--Ne) collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}}=5.36$ TeV, using nuclear geometry simulations based on NLEFT and PGCM configurations. The AMPT model is used to investigate specific SPCs, revealing that Ne--Ne collisions have larger $\langle \cos[4(\psi_2 - \psi_4)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ values, while OO collisions exhibit larger $\langle \cos[6(\psi_3 - \psi_6)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ values, indicating the deformed shape of $^{20}$Ne and tetrahedral structure of $^{16}$O. Further analysis of tip-tip and body-body collision configurations supports these findings.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this study is to explore the influence of nuclear geometry on symmetry-plane correlations (SPCs) in small systems, such as Oxygen--Oxygen (OO) and Neon--Neon (Ne--Ne) collisions, which are sensitive indicators of the medium's transport properties. By using advanced nuclear geometry models, the authors aim to understand how the initial state participant-plane correlations (PPCs) translate into observable SPCs, and to identify signatures of nuclear deformation and structure in these collisions.

Method: The method involves the use of Nuclear Lattice Effective Field Theory (NLEFT) and Projected Generator Coordinate Method (PGCM) to simulate the nuclear geometry of the colliding nuclei. The A Multi-Phase Transport (AMPT) model is then employed to calculate the SPCs, specifically $\langle \cos[4(\psi_2 - \psi_4)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ and $\langle \cos[6(\psi_3 - \psi_6)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$, in OO and Ne--Ne collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}}=5.36$ TeV. The analysis also includes a comparison of SPCs for events with different collision configurations, such as tip-tip and body-body, to further elucidate the role of nuclear geometry.

Result: The results show that Ne--Ne collisions exhibit larger $\langle \cos[4(\psi_2 - \psi_4)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ values compared to OO collisions, suggesting a strong deformation in the $^{20}$Ne nucleus. Conversely, OO collisions display larger $\langle \cos[6(\psi_3 - \psi_6)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ values, indicating a more tetrahedral structure for the $^{16}$O nucleus. The analysis of tip-tip and body-body collision configurations provides additional support for these conclusions, highlighting the importance of nuclear geometry in determining SPCs.

Conclusion: The study concludes that the observed differences in SPCs between OO and Ne--Ne collisions can be attributed to the distinct nuclear geometries of the colliding nuclei. The larger $\langle \cos[4(\psi_2 - \psi_4)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ in Ne--Ne collisions and the larger $\langle \cos[6(\psi_3 - \psi_6)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ in OO collisions are indicative of the deformed shape of $^{20}$Ne and the tetrahedral structure of $^{16}$O, respectively. These findings provide valuable insights into the interplay between nuclear geometry and the resulting SPCs, which can be used to better understand the transport properties of the medium created in heavy-ion collisions.

Abstract: Symmetry-plane correlations (SPCs) are key observables sensitive to the medium's transport properties and are driven by participant-plane correlations (PPCs) in the nuclear overlap region. This study explores the possibility of nuclear-geometry-driven SPCs in Oxygen--Oxygen (OO) and Neon--Neon (Ne--Ne) collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}}=5.36$ TeV using nuclear geometry simulations based on Nuclear Lattice Effective Field Theory (NLEFT) and Projected Generator Coordinate Method (PGCM) configurations. We investigate $\langle \cos[4(ψ_2 - ψ_4)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ and $\langle \cos[6(ψ_3 - ψ_6)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ in OO and Ne--Ne collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}}=5.36$ TeV using the A Multi-Phase Transport (AMPT) model. We find that Ne--Ne collisions exhibit larger $\langle \cos[4(ψ_2 - ψ_4)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ values than OO collisions, whereas $\langle \cos[6(ψ_3 - ψ_6)]\rangle_{\rm GE}$ is larger in OO than in Ne--Ne collisions. This behavior indicates a strongly deformed shape of the $^{20}$Ne nucleus and a tetrahedral structure of the $^{16}$O nucleus. We also explore SPCs for events with tip-tip and body-body collision configurations, which further support these findings.

</details>

### [18] [Three-flavor supernova neutrino simulation using a hybrid quantum-classical algorithm with qutrits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01099)
*Daniel J. Heimsoth,A. Baha Balantekin,Pooja Siwach*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper describes a hybrid classical-quantum algorithm for simulating a three-flavor neutrino system in a core-collapse supernova. The method, using a qutrit computer, employs the Dirac-Frenkel evolution equations and quantum-assisted simulator (QAS) to calculate the time evolution operator. The results are comparable to exact numerical integration up to $t \approx 30 \,\omega_0^{-1}$, with a step of $\delta t = 0.005 \,\omega_0^{-1}$. The study also discusses the benefits of this approach over quantum Trotterization.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop and test a novel hybrid classical-quantum algorithm for simulating complex neutrino systems, particularly in the context of core-collapse supernovae. By leveraging the strengths of both classical and quantum computing, the authors aim to accurately model the dynamics of self-interacting three-flavor neutrinos, which is computationally challenging using traditional methods.

动机是开发和测试一种新的混合经典-量子算法，用于模拟复杂的中微子系统，特别是在核心塌缩超新星的背景下。通过利用经典计算和量子计算的优势，作者旨在准确地模拟自相互作用的三味中微子的动力学，这使用传统方法在计算上具有挑战性。

Method: The method involves simulating a self-interacting three-flavor neutrino system within a core-collapse supernova using a hybrid classical-quantum algorithm on a qutrit computer. The simulation is based on the Dirac-Frenkel evolution equations, and a variation of the quantum-assisted simulator (QAS) is used to compute the time evolution operator. Qutrit Hadamard tests are performed to find expectation values of unitary operators in the Hamiltonian, and the time evolution is then simulated classically.

该方法涉及使用qutrit计算机上的混合经典-量子算法来模拟核心塌缩超新星中的自相互作用三味中微子系统。模拟基于Dirac-Frenkel演化方程，并使用量子辅助模拟器（QAS）的一种变体来计算时间演化算符。执行qutrit Hadamard测试以找到哈密顿量中幺正算符的期望值，然后通过经典方法进行时间演化模拟。

Result: The hybrid algorithm produces results that are comparable to those obtained from an exact numerical integration, up to times of $t \approx 30 \,\omega_0^{-1}$, with a time step of $\delta t = 0.005 \,\omega_0^{-1}$, where $\omega_0$ is the energy scale of single neutrino vacuum oscillations. This demonstrates the effectiveness of the hybrid approach in accurately simulating the neutrino system.

混合算法产生的结果与精确数值积分的结果相当，时间达到$t \approx 30 \,\omega_0^{-1}$，时间步长为$\delta t = 0.005 \,\omega_0^{-1}$，其中$\omega_0$是单个中微子真空振荡的能量尺度。这证明了混合方法在准确模拟中微子系统方面的有效性。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the hybrid classical-quantum algorithm is a viable and effective approach for simulating complex neutrino systems, such as those found in core-collapse supernovae. The method offers advantages over quantum Trotterization, including improved accuracy and efficiency, making it a promising tool for future research in neutrino physics.

研究结论是，混合经典-量子算法是一种可行且有效的方法，适用于模拟复杂中微子系统，如核心塌缩超新星中的系统。该方法比量子Trotter化具有优势，包括提高的准确性和效率，使其成为未来中微子物理学研究中有前景的工具。

Abstract: We simulate a self-interacting three-flavor neutrino system within a core-collapse supernova using a hybrid classical-quantum algorithm on a qutrit computer. Based on the Dirac-Frenkel evolution equations, we employ a variation of the quantum-assisted simulator (QAS) to calculate the system's time evolution operator by performing qutrit Hadamard tests to find expectation values of unitary operators in the Hamiltonian. The time evolution simulation is then done classically. We find that the hybrid algorithm produces results comparable to an exact numerical integration out to times of $t \approx 30 \,ω_0^{-1}$ with time step $δt = 0.005 \,ω_0^{-1}$, where $ω_0$ is the energy scale of the single neutrino vacuum oscillations. We discuss the lessons learned in simulating neutrino systems using this hybrid quantum-classical algorithm, along with the advantages it offers over quantum Trotterization.

### [19] [Gravitational waves from CP domain wall collapse and electron EDM in a complex singlet model with dimension-five Yukawa interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01318)
*Hieu The Pham,Eibun Senaha*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores the connection between gravitational waves (GWs) from domain wall collapse and the electron electric dipole moment (EDM) in a complex singlet extension of the Standard Model. The study shows that current and future EDM experiments can probe the parameter space where GW signals are detectable, highlighting the complementary nature of these observables in understanding the singlet scalar sector's vacuum structure and CP properties.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the interplay between gravitational waves (GWs) from domain wall collapse and the electron electric dipole moment (EDM) in a model with a complex singlet extension of the Standard Model. The goal is to determine if EDM experiments can probe the parameter space where GWs from domain wall collapse are detectable, thus providing insights into the CP-violating phases and the vacuum structure of the singlet scalar sector.

动机是理解在具有复单态扩展的标准模型中，由畴壁塌缩产生的引力波（GWs）与电子电偶极矩（EDM）之间的相互作用。目标是确定EDM实验是否可以探测到GWs可检测的参数空间，从而提供关于单态标量部分的CP破坏相位和真空结构的见解。

Method: The method involves a theoretical framework where a complex singlet scalar field is added to the Standard Model, leading to the formation of CP domain walls. The authors calculate the GW signal from the collapse of these domain walls and analyze the constraints on the model parameters from current and future EDM experiments. They use the dimension-five Yukawa interactions to couple the singlet scalar to the Standard Model fermions, which allows for the observation of CP-violating phases through EDMs.

方法涉及一个理论框架，其中向标准模型添加了一个复单态标量场，导致CP畴壁的形成。作者计算了这些畴壁塌缩产生的GW信号，并分析了当前和未来EDM实验对模型参数的约束。他们使用五维Yukawa相互作用将单态标量与标准模型费米子耦合，这使得通过EDM观察CP破坏相位成为可能。

Result: The results show that the current electron EDM bound already constrains part of the parameter space, while future EDM sensitivities at the level of $10^{-31}$--$10^{-32}\,e\,\mathrm{cm}$ can probe regions overlapping with the GW-detectable domain. This indicates that there is a significant overlap between the parameter spaces probed by GWs and EDMs, suggesting that both observables are necessary for a complete understanding of the singlet scalar sector.

结果表明，当前的电子EDM限制已经约束了一部分参数空间，而未来EDM灵敏度在$10^{-31}$--$10^{-32}\,e\,\mathrm{cm}$水平上可以探测到与GW可检测区域重叠的区域。这表明GWs和EDMs所探测的参数空间有显著重叠，暗示为了全面理解单态标量部分，这两种可观测物都是必要的。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the complementarity between GW and EDM observables provides a coherent picture of the vacuum structure and CP properties of the singlet scalar sector. Current and future EDM experiments can effectively probe the parameter region where GW signals from domain wall collapse are detectable, enhancing our understanding of the underlying physics.

结论是，GW和EDM可观测物之间的互补性为单态标量部分的真空结构和CP性质提供了连贯的图景。当前和未来的EDM实验可以有效地探测到畴壁塌缩产生的GW信号可检测的参数区域，从而增强我们对潜在物理的理解。

Abstract: We study the interplay between gravitational waves (GWs) from domain wall collapse and the electron electric dipole moment (EDM) in a complex singlet extension of the standard model with dimension-five Yukawa interactions. In this framework, the scalar potential admits CP-related degenerate vacua, leading to the formation of CP domain walls. While the resulting GW signal provides a probe of the vacuum structure of the singlet scalar sector, it does not by itself constitute a CP-violating observable. Once the singlet scalar is coupled to standard model fermions, CP-violating phases become observable through EDMs. We analyze whether current and future EDM experiments can probe the parameter region where the GW signal is detectable by SKA and THEIA. We find that the current electron EDM bound already constrains part of the parameter space, while future sensitivities at the level of $10^{-31}$--$10^{-32}\,e\,\mathrm{cm}$ can probe regions overlapping with the GW-detectable domain. Our results highlight the complementarity between GW and EDM observables in probing the singlet scalar sector, providing a coherent picture of its vacuum structure and CP properties.

### [20] [Multi-Lepton Probes of the Drell-Yan Production of Triplet Higgses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01488)
*Siddharth P. Maharathy,Srimoy Bhattacharya,Andreas Crivellin,Mukesh Kumar,Rachid Mazini,Bruce Mellado*

TL;DR: The paper discusses the possibility of a new Higgs boson with a mass of $152 \pm 1$ GeV, as indicated by excesses in di-photon, $Zγ$, and $WW$ spectra. The Real Higgs Triplet model ($Δ$SM) is proposed to explain these observations, but it predicts more triboson events than observed, leading to a moderate tension with data. Future LHC runs could clarify this situation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this paper stems from the observation of excesses in di-photon, $Zγ$, and $WW$ spectra, which suggest the existence of a new Higgs boson with a mass of $152 \pm 1$ GeV. The absence of an excess in the $ZZ$ channel aligns with the Real Higgs Triplet model ($Δ$SM) with hypercharge $Y = 0$. This model also predicts the enhancement of triboson cross sections, such as $WWZ$, $WZZ$, and $WWW$, through the Drell--Yan production of scalars. Both ATLAS and CMS have reported higher-than-expected significances for these processes, hinting at the presence of an extended Higgs sector.\n\n本文的动机源于在双光子、$Zγ$ 和 $WW$ 谱中观察到的过量，这表明存在一个质量为 $152 \pm 1$ GeV 的新希格斯玻色子。$ZZ$ 通道中没有过量与超荷 $Y = 0$ 的实希格斯三重态模型（$Δ$SM）一致。该模型还预测通过标量的德雷尔-杨产生过程增强三规范玻色子截面，如 $WWZ$、$WZZ$ 和 $WWW$。ATLAS 和 CMS 都报告了这些过程比预期更高的显著性，暗示了扩展希格斯扇区的存在。

Method: The method involves the investigation of the Real Higgs Triplet model ($Δ$SM) and its predictions for the Drell--Yan production of scalars that decay predominantly into electroweak bosons. The authors analyze the compatibility of the model's predictions with the observed triboson excesses in the $VVZ$ (where $V = W$ or $Z$) and $WWZ$ channels, as reported by ATLAS and CMS. They compare the expected number of events from the $Δ$SM with the observed data to determine if the model can account for the excesses while remaining consistent with other experimental constraints.\n\n方法涉及研究实希格斯三重态模型（$Δ$SM）及其对标量德雷尔-杨产生的预测，这些标量主要衰变为电弱玻色子。作者分析了该模型预测与 ATLAS 和 CMS 报告的 $VVZ$（其中 $V = W$ 或 $Z$）和 $WWZ$ 通道中观测到的三规范玻色子过量的一致性。他们比较了 $Δ$SM 预测的事件数与观测数据，以确定该模型是否能够解释过量同时保持与其他实验约束的一致性。

Result: The results show that while the current data prefers a non-zero new physics signal ($2.6σ$), the $Δ$SM predicts more triboson events than are observed. The model is consistent with the data but not preferred over the Standard Model (SM). The tension between the $Δ$SM and the data could be resolved with future data from Run~3 and the High-Luminosity LHC (HL-LHC).\n\n结果显示，虽然当前数据倾向于非零的新物理信号（$2.6σ$），但 $Δ$SM 预测的三规范玻色子事件数多于观测值。该模型与数据一致，但不优于标准模型（SM）。$Δ$SM 与数据之间的张力可以通过未来的 Run~3 和高亮度 LHC（HL-LHC）数据来解决。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the Real Higgs Triplet model ($Δ$SM) can potentially explain the observed excesses in di-photon, $Zγ$, and $WW$ spectra, as well as the enhanced triboson cross sections. However, the model predicts a higher number of events than currently observed, leading to a moderate tension. Future LHC data will be crucial in determining whether the $Δ$SM is a viable extension of the Higgs sector.\n\n结论是实希格斯三重态模型（$Δ$SM）可能解释观测到的双光子、$Zγ$ 和 $WW$ 谱中的过量以及增强的三规范玻色子截面。然而，该模型预测的事件数高于目前观测到的数量，导致了一定程度的张力。未来的 LHC 数据将对确定 $Δ$SM 是否是希格斯扇区的可行扩展至关重要。

Abstract: Excesses in di-photon, $Zγ$, and $WW$ spectra indicate the existence of a new Higgs boson with mass $152 \pm 1$ GeV. However, no excess is observed in the $ZZ$ channel. This pattern aligns with a Real Higgs Triplet model with hypercharge $Y = 0$ ($Δ$SM). A prediction of this model is the Drell--Yan production of scalars at the LHC, which dominantly decay to electroweak bosons, thus enhancing the cross sections of triboson channels such as $WWZ$, $WZZ$, and $WWW$. Interestingly, both ATLAS and CMS have reported higher-than-expected significances for such processes: $6.4σ$ (observed) vs $4.7σ$ (expected) in the $VVZ$ (where $V = W$ or $Z$) channel and $4.4σ$ vs $3.6σ$ in $WWZ$, suggesting the possibility that these signals may be manifestations of an extended Higgs sector. We investigate whether the $Δ$SM can account for these triboson excesses through electroweak production and decay of triplet scalars. We find that while current data prefers a non-zero new physics signal ($2.6σ$), the $Δ$SM predicts more events than observed, such that it is consistent with data but not preferred over the SM. However, this tension could be clarified with Run~3 and HL-LHC data.
