### [21] [Effects of the magnetic field on $π^0$ production in ultraperipheral Pb-Pb collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01500)
*C. N. Azevedo,R. Fariello,F. C. Sobrinho,F. S. Navarra*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates the impact of magnetic fields on neutral pion production in photon-photon interactions during ultraperipheral Pb-Pb collisions at the LHC, revealing a significant reduction in the production cross section due to the suppression of the two-photon decay width in strong magnetic fields.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this study is to understand how strong magnetic fields, which are present in heavy-ion collisions, affect the production of neutral pions ($π^0$) through photon-photon interactions. The focus is on the modification of the $π^0\toγγ$ decay width and its subsequent influence on the $π^0$ production cross section.

这项研究的动机是理解在重离子碰撞中存在的强磁场如何通过光子-光子相互作用影响中性π介子（$π^0$）的产生。重点在于$π^0\toγγ$衰变宽度的变化及其对$π^0$产生截面的影响。

Method: The authors use the equivalent photon approximation (EPA) to calculate the production cross section of neutral pions in ultraperipheral Pb-Pb collisions. They incorporate a magnetic-field dependence into the $Γ(π^0\toγγ)$ decay width, which is then used to compute the modified production cross section. This approach allows for an analysis of how the presence of a strong magnetic field alters the expected outcomes of these high-energy collisions.

作者使用等效光子近似（EPA）来计算超外周Pb-Pb碰撞中中性π介子的产生截面。他们将磁依赖性纳入$Γ(π^0\toγγ)$衰变宽度中，然后用它来计算修正后的产生截面。这种方法允许分析强磁场的存在如何改变这些高能碰撞的预期结果。

Result: The results show that the inclusion of a strong magnetic field leads to a substantial reduction in the two-photon decay width $Γ(π^0\toγγ)$. Consequently, there is a significant decrease (by a factor of about 2-3) in the $π^0$ production cross section at LHC energies. This finding highlights the importance of considering magnetic field effects in theoretical models of particle production in heavy-ion collisions.

结果显示，引入强磁场会导致两光子衰变宽度$Γ(π^0\toγγ)$显著减少。因此，在LHC能量下，$π^0$产生截面减少了约2-3倍。这一发现强调了在重离子碰撞粒子产生的理论模型中考虑磁场效应的重要性。

Conclusion: In conclusion, the presence of a strong magnetic field in ultraperipheral Pb-Pb collisions significantly reduces the $π^0$ production cross section by suppressing the $π^0\toγγ$ decay width. This effect must be taken into account in future studies of particle production in similar environments, as it can have important implications for our understanding of QCD and the properties of matter under extreme conditions.

总之，在超外周Pb-Pb碰撞中存在强磁场会通过抑制$π^0\toγγ$衰变宽度显著减少$π^0$产生截面。在未来类似环境下的粒子产生研究中必须考虑到这种效应，因为它对于我们理解QCD和极端条件下的物质性质具有重要意义。

Abstract: In this work, we study the effect of the magnetic field on the production of neutral pions in photon-photon interactions in ultraperipheral Pb-Pb collisions at the LHC. The calculation is performed within the equivalent photon approximation, including a magnetic-field dependence in the decay width $Γ(π^0\toγγ)$, from which the corresponding production cross section is computed. We find that the reduction of the two-photon decay width in the presence of a strong magnetic field leads to a substantial reduction (by a factor of about 2-3) of the $π^0$ production cross section at LHC energies.

### [22] [Probing Saturation Effect in Heavy Meson Pair Correlation in Forward $pA$ Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01527)
*Zhan Gao,Cyrille Marquet,Yu Shi,Bo-Wen Xiao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper studies heavy meson pair correlations in forward $pA$ collisions using a unified Sudakov resummation within the Color Glass Condensate (CGC) framework. The results are consistent with LHCb data and predict a mass hierarchy in the nuclear modification factor, $R_{pA}$, indicating stronger saturation effects for heavier quarks.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore gluon saturation effects through the study of two-particle angular correlations in forward $pA$ collisions. Specifically, the work aims to understand the contributions from soft-gluon radiation and saturation effects in the back-to-back regime, and to predict heavy meson pair correlations in the forward rapidity regions at the LHC.

动机是通过研究前向$pA$碰撞中的两粒子角关联来探索胶子饱和效应。具体来说，这项工作旨在理解背对背区域中软胶子辐射和饱和效应的贡献，并预测LHC前向快度区间的重介子对关联。

Method: The method involves incorporating a unified Sudakov resummation for heavy meson pair correlations into the Color Glass Condensate (CGC) effective theory. This approach allows for a comprehensive treatment of both soft-gluon radiation and saturation effects in the context of heavy meson production in $pA$ collisions.

方法是将统一的Sudakov重求和纳入到Color Glass Condensate (CGC) 有效理论中，用于处理重介子对关联。这种方法允许在$pA$碰撞中重介子产生的背景下全面处理软胶子辐射和饱和效应。

Result: The results show good agreement with the $Δφ$ data measured by the LHCb Collaboration for $D^0 ar D^0$ pairs in forward $pp$ and $pA$ collisions, as well as $J/ψ$ pairs from $bar b$ decays in forward $pp$ collisions. The predictions for $Dar D$ and $Bar B$ correlations in the forward rapidity regions at the LHC indicate a pronounced mass hierarchy in the nuclear modification factor, $R_{pA}\big|_{m_b}<R_{pA}\big|_{m_c}$, suggesting stronger sensitivity to saturation effects for heavier quarks.

结果与LHCb合作组测量的前向$pp$和$pA$碰撞中的$D^0 ar D^0$对以及前向$pp$碰撞中$bar b$衰变产生的$J/ψ$对的$Δφ$数据一致。LHC前向快度区间的$Dar D$和$Bar B$关联的预测表明，在核修正因子$R_{pA}\big|_{m_b}<R_{pA}\big|_{m_c}$中存在明显的质量层次，这表明对于更重的夸克，对饱和效应的敏感性更强。

Conclusion: The study provides a new avenue for searching for saturation signals via heavy-meson pair correlations in forward $pA$ collisions. The observed mass hierarchy in $R_{pA}$ suggests that heavier quarks exhibit stronger suppression and greater sensitivity to saturation effects at small $x$. These findings will be valuable for future experimental searches and theoretical developments in the field of high-energy QCD.

该研究为通过前向$pA$碰撞中的重介子对关联寻找饱和信号提供了新的途径。在$R_{pA}$中观察到的质量层次表明，更重的夸克在小$x$处表现出更强的抑制和对饱和效应更大的敏感性。这些发现将对未来实验搜索和高能QCD领域的理论发展具有重要价值。

Abstract: Forward two-particle angular correlations in $pA$ collisions have long been recognized as a particularly sensitive observable for exploring gluon saturation effects. In the back-to-back regime, two-particle correlations receive substantial contributions from both soft-gluon radiation and saturation effects. In this work, we study heavy meson pair correlation in forward proton-nucleus collisions by incorporating a unified Sudakov resummation for heavy meson pair correlations in the Color Glass Condensate effect theory. Our results are in good agreement with the $Δφ$ data measured by the LHCb Collaboration for $D^0 \bar D^0$ pairs in forward $pp$ and $pA$ collisions, as well as $J/ψ$ pairs from $b\bar b$ decays in forward $pp$ collisions. Furthermore, we present predictions for $D\bar D$ and $B\bar B$ correlations in the forward rapidity regions at the Large Hadron Collider. A pronounced mass-hierarchy is observed in the nuclear modification factor, $R_{pA}\big|_{m_b}<R_{pA}\big|_{m_c}$, indicating stronger sensitivity to saturation effects at small $x$. As the rapidity increases, the suppression becomes more pronounced while the mass hierarchy remains robust. This study will help us to search for the saturation signal via heavy-meson pair correlations in forward $pA$ collisions.

### [23] [Multimodal Fragmentation of All-Heavy Pentaquarks: Uncertainty-Aware Predictions for Hadron Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01539)
*Francesco Giovanni Celiberto*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper presents a new set of fragmentation functions, PQ5Q1.1, for all-charm pentaquark states at hadron colliders, incorporating both perturbative and nonperturbative uncertainties. The framework is applied to study semi-inclusive pentaquark-plus-jet production at the HL-LHC and future FCC, providing a flexible and uncertainty-controlled approach for predictions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop an uncertainty-aware description of leading-power fragmentation for all-charm pentaquark states at hadron colliders. This is important for understanding the production mechanisms of these exotic hadrons and for making reliable predictions in high-energy QCD.

Method: The authors construct a multimodal set of collinear fragmentation functions, PQ5Q1.1, which incorporates both perturbative and nonperturbative uncertainties. Perturbative effects are estimated via missing higher-order variations (F-MHOUs), while the nonperturbative wave function is modeled through controlled modifications of its transverse-momentum structure (F-NPWF). These uncertainties are consistently combined within a replica-like framework. The initial-scale input for constituent charm fragmentation is refined to describe both compact multiquark and diquark-driven production mechanisms. The (sym)JETHAD interface is used to study NLL/NLO$^+$ semi-inclusive pentaquark-plus-jet production at the HL-LHC and future FCC.

Result: The results provide a flexible framework for uncertainty-controlled predictions, bridging the gap between exotic-hadron structure, heavy-flavor fragmentation, and high-energy QCD. The new set of fragmentation functions, PQ5Q1.1, allows for a more accurate description of the production of all-charm pentaquark states, taking into account both perturbative and nonperturbative effects.

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the developed framework, including the new set of fragmentation functions, PQ5Q1.1, provides a robust and flexible tool for predicting the production of all-charm pentaquark states at hadron colliders, with a clear quantification of uncertainties. This work sets the stage for future studies, particularly in the bottom sector, where nonperturbative modeling is more sensitive.

Abstract: We present an uncertainty-aware description of leading-power fragmentation for all-charm pentaquark states ($S$-wave $|cccc\bar{c}\rangle$) at hadron colliders. We construct a multimodal set of collinear fragmentation functions, PQ5Q1.1, incorporating both perturbative and nonperturbative uncertainties. Perturbative effects are estimated via missing higher-order variations (F-MHOUs), while the nonperturbative wave function is modeled through controlled modifications of its transverse-momentum structure (F-NPWF), consistently combined within a replica-like framework. The initial-scale input for constituent charm fragmentation is refined to describe both compact multiquark and diquark-driven production mechanisms. We employ the (sym)JETHAD interface to study NLL/NLO$^+$ semi-inclusive pentaquark-plus-jet production at the HL-LHC and future FCC. The bottom sector is left to future dedicated studies due to its enhanced sensitivity to nonperturbative modeling. Our results provide a flexible framework for uncertainty-controlled predictions, bridging exotic-hadron structure, heavy-flavor fragmentation, and high-energy QCD.

### [24] [Equation of State of Dense Matter: Pauli Degeneracy, Pairing Correlations, and Implications for Neutron Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01618)
*Yaroslav D. Krivenko-Emetov,Gleb Shabal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper develops a unified description of dense fermionic matter, incorporating Pauli degeneracy, interaction effects, and pairing correlations, and applies it to the equation of state (EOS) for neutron stars. It shows that Pauli degeneracy provides the dominant pressure, interactions affect the stiffness of the EOS, and pairing correlations give subleading but significant corrections, especially in quark matter.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to create a comprehensive model of dense fermionic matter that includes all relevant physical effects, such as Pauli degeneracy, interaction effects, and pairing correlations, and to understand their roles in the equation of state (EOS). This is crucial for accurately describing the structure of neutron stars and other compact objects, and for interpreting modern observational data.

Method: The method involves developing a theoretical framework that separates the contributions from Sommerfeld, Fermi-liquid, and pairing regimes, based on the condition that the temperature is much smaller than the Fermi energy. The resulting equation of state (EOS) is then applied to the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equations to analyze the structure of neutron stars.

Result: The results show that Pauli degeneracy is the dominant source of pressure in dense fermionic matter, while interactions determine the stiffness of the EOS. Pairing correlations, although subleading, can provide significant corrections, particularly in quark matter. These findings have implications for the mass-radius relations and other observable properties of neutron stars.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the unified description of dense fermionic matter, which includes Pauli degeneracy, interaction effects, and pairing correlations, is essential for understanding the equation of state (EOS) and the structure of neutron stars. The model provides a more accurate and comprehensive picture of these systems, which is important for interpreting observational data.

Abstract: We develop a unified description of dense fermionic matter that consistently incorporates Pauli degeneracy, interaction effects, and pairing correlations. The condition that the temperature is much smaller than the Fermi energy leads to a natural separation between Sommerfeld, Fermi-liquid, and pairing regimes, and how these contributions enter the equation of state. The resulting EOS is applied to the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations to analyze neutron-star structure. We demonstrate that Pauli degeneracy provides the dominant pressure, interactions determine the stiffness of the EOS, and pairing correlations produce subleading but potentially significant corrections, especially in quark matter. Implications for mass--radius constraints and modern observations are discussed.

### [25] [New Directions in Kaon Physics: Interference in $K^0\toμ^+μ^-$ as a New Golden Mode](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01744)

TL;DR: The paper discusses the rare decays $K^0_L \to \mu^+\mu^-$ and $K^0_S \to \mu^+\mu^-$, highlighting the interference between $K_L^0$ and $K_S^0$ which is sensitive to direct $CP$ violation. By considering the interference between $K_L^0$ and $K_S^0$, the authors aim to provide a clean probe of $CP$-violating short-distance physics. [English Text]

Result: The results indicate that the CKM parameter $|A^2\lambda^5\bar{\eta}|$ could be constrained by LHCb to about 35% of its Standard Model (SM) value. Additionally, the discrete ambiguity in $\mathcal{B}(K_L^0 \to \mu^+\mu^-)_{\rm SM}$ could be resolved at more than 3$\sigma$ by the end of the high luminosity LHC. [English Text]

Abstract: The rare decays $K^0_L \toμ^+μ^-$ and $K^0_S \toμ^+μ^-$ have long been regarded as difficult channels to extract short-distance physics because they are dominated by long-distance contributions via two-photon exchanges. A qualitatively new feature arises once the interference between $K_L^0$ and $K_S^0$ is taken into account. The interference term is sensitive to genuine direct $CP$ violation in $s \to d μ^+ μ^-$ processes and turns this channel into a clean probe of the $CP$-violating short-distance physics. In this contribution, I summarize the basic mechanism of the $K_L^0$--$K_S^0$ interference, the flavor-tagging strategy at LHCb-like setup, and the projected sensitivities for a kaon-unitarity-triangle parameter combination $|A^2λ^5\barη|$ and also for the sign ambiguity of the $K_L^0 \to γγ$ three-point amplitude. As a result, it is expected that the CKM parameter $|A^2λ^5\barη|$ could be constrained by LHCb at the level of about $35\%$ of its Standard Model (SM) value, and the discrete ambiguity in $\mathcal{B}(K_L^0 \to μ^+μ^-)_{\rm SM}$ could be resolved at more than $3σ$ by the end of the high luminosity LHC.

### [26] [Production Rate of Glueball-like $X(2370)$ in $J/ψ$ Radiative Decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01757)
*Ying Chen,Long-Cheng Gui,Geng Li,Wei Sun*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper discusses the possibility that $X(2370)$ and $η_c$ are mixtures of the pseudoscalar glueball $G_{0^-}$ and the lowest pseudoscalar charmonium $c\bar{c}(0^-)$. The mixing angle $\sinθ$ is small, but it can significantly enhance the branching ratio $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γX(2370))$ due to kinematic factors and transition form factors. Current BESIII results suggest a small mixing angle, which can be further constrained by more measurements.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the nature of the $X(2370)$ particle, which has a mass in the range predicted for the lowest pseudoscalar glueball by lattice QCD studies. Given its decay properties similar to those of $η_c$, the authors propose that $X(2370)$ and $η_c$ could be admixtures of the pseudoscalar glueball $G_{0^-}$ and the lowest pseudoscalar charmonium $c\bar{c}(0^-)$. This hypothesis is based on the finding from a previous lattice QCD study that these two states can mix with a small mixing angle $\sinθ$. The aim is to understand how the mixing affects the branching ratios of certain decays, particularly $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γX(2370))$.

该论文的动机是探索$X(2370)$粒子的本质，其质量在格点QCD研究预测的最低伪标量胶球的质量范围内。鉴于其衰变性质与$η_c$相似，作者提出$X(2370)$和$η_c$可能是伪标量胶球$G_{0^-}$和最低伪标量粲偶素$c\bar{c}(0^-)$的混合态。这一假设基于先前的格点QCD研究发现，这两个状态可以以一个小的混合角$\sinθ$混合。目的是理解这种混合如何影响某些衰变的分支比，特别是$\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γX(2370))$。

Method: The method involves analyzing the mixing between the pseudoscalar glueball $G_{0^-}$ and the lowest pseudoscalar charmonium $c\bar{c}(0^-)$. The authors use the small mixing angle $\sinθ$ to calculate the effects on the branching ratios of specific decays. They consider the kinematic factors and transition form factors that contribute to the enhancement of $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γX(2370))$. Additionally, they compare their predictions with the current experimental results from BESIII to constrain the value of the mixing angle $\sinθ$.

该方法涉及分析伪标量胶球$G_{0^-}$和最低伪标量粲偶素$c\bar{c}(0^-)$之间的混合。作者使用小的混合角$\sinθ$来计算对特定衰变分支比的影响。他们考虑了导致$\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γX(2370))$增强的运动学因子和跃迁形式因子。此外，他们将他们的预测与BESIII当前的实验结果进行比较，以约束混合角$\sinθ$的值。

Result: The results show that while the branching ratio $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γη_c)$ is insensitive to the small mixing angle $\sinθ$, the branching ratio $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γX(2370))$ can be significantly enhanced due to the larger kinematic factor and transition form factor for $J/ψ→γ(c\bar{c}(0^{-}))$. Depending on the value of $\sinθ$, $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γX(2370))$ can be much larger than the prediction for a pure pseudoscalar glueball, which is $2.3(8)×10^{-4}$. The current BESIII results favor a small mixing angle of $\mathcal{O}(1^\circ)$, which can be further constrained by future measurements of $X(2370)$ decays.

结果显示，虽然分支比$\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γη_c)$对小的混合角$\sinθ$不敏感，但分支比$\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γX(2370))$由于$J/ψ→γ(c\bar{c}(0^{-}))$的更大的运动学因子和跃迁形式因子而显著增强。根据$\sinθ$的值，$\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γX(2370))$可能远大于纯伪标量胶球的预测值，即$2.3(8)×10^{-4}$。当前BESIII的结果支持一个约为$\mathcal{O}(1^\circ)$的小混合角，这可以通过未来对$X(2370)$衰变的测量进一步约束。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the $X(2370)$ and $η_c$ particles can be understood as admixtures of the pseudoscalar glueball $G_{0^-}$ and the lowest pseudoscalar charmonium $c\bar{c}(0^-)$, with a small mixing angle $\sinθ$. The mixing leads to a significant enhancement of the branching ratio $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γX(2370))$ compared to the case of a pure pseudoscalar glueball. The current BESIII data suggests a small mixing angle, and future measurements of $X(2370)$ decays can provide further constraints on the mixing angle.

结论是$X(2370)$和$η_c$粒子可以被理解为伪标量胶球$G_{0^-}$和最低伪标量粲偶素$c\bar{c}(0^-)$的混合态，具有一个小的混合角$\sinθ$。这种混合导致分支比$\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ→γX(2370))$相对于纯伪标量胶球的情况显著增强。当前BESIII数据表明混合角较小，未来对$X(2370)$衰变的测量可以进一步约束混合角。

Abstract: $X(2370)$ falls in the mass region of the lowest pseudoscalar glueball predicted by lattice QCD studies and its decay properties are similar to those of $η_c$. A previous lattice QCD study finds that the pseudoscalar glueball ($G_{0^-}$) and the lowest pseudoscalar charmonium ($c\bar{c}(0^-)$) can mix with a small mixing angle $\sinθ$. It is therefore possible that $X(2370)$ and $η_c$ are admixtures of $G_{0^-}$ and $c\bar{c}(0^-)$. In this picture, although $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ\toγη_c)$ is insensitive to the small $\sinθ$, $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ\to γX(2370))$ can be enlarged drastically by the mixing due to the much larger kinematic factor for $J/ψ\to γX(2370)$ and the much larger transition form factor for $J/ψ\to γ(c\bar{c}(0^{-}))$. Depending on the value of $\sinθ$, $\mathrm{Br}(J/ψ\to γX(2370))$ can be much larger than that of the pure pseudoscalar glueball, namely, $2.3(8)\times 10^{-4}$ that is predicted by a quenched lattice QCD calculation. Present results by BESIII favor a small mixing angle of $\mathcal{O}(1^\circ)$, which can be further constrained by more measurements of $X(2370)$ decays if the mixing picture applies here.

### [27] [Transverse momentum dependence of $Ω/φ$ ratio in high energy collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01762)
*Hai-hong Li,Jun Song,Feng-lan Shao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper uses a constituent quark equal-velocity combination model to study the $p_{T}$ dependence of the $Ω/φ$ ratio in various collisions at LHC energies. The key finding is that the relative change rate of the $Ω/φ$ ratio is governed by the curvature property of the $p_{T}$ spectrum of strange quarks just before hadronization. This curvature property is extracted from experimental data and used to explain the observed $p_{T}$ dependence of the $Ω/φ$ ratio, with the influence of strong collective flow in partonic stage evolution being considered as a possible origin for the changes in the curvature.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to understand the dynamics of strange quark production and hadronization in high-energy collisions. Specifically, the authors aim to investigate the $p_{T}$ dependence of the $Ω/φ$ ratio, which can provide insights into the properties of the quark-gluon plasma (QGP) and the hadronization process. By studying the curvature property of the $p_{T}$ spectrum of strange quarks, the authors seek to explain the observed behavior of the $Ω/φ$ ratio in different collision systems and multiplicities.

本文的动机是理解高能碰撞中奇异夸克的产生和强子化动力学。具体来说，作者旨在研究$Ω/φ$比值的$p_{T}$依赖性，这可以提供关于夸克胶子等离子体（QGP）性质和强子化过程的见解。通过研究奇异夸克的$p_{T}$谱曲率特性，作者试图解释不同碰撞系统和多重数下观测到的$Ω/φ$比值的行为。

Method: The authors employ a constituent quark equal-velocity combination model to analyze the $p_{T}$ dependence of the $Ω/φ$ ratio in $pp$, $p$-Pb, and Pb-Pb collisions at LHC energies. They extract the $p_{T}$ spectrum of strange quarks just before hadronization using experimental data of $φ$ mesons after applying a quark number scaling operation. The curvature property of the $p_{T}$ spectrum of strange quarks is then studied in both high and low multiplicity events across different collision systems. These curvature properties are used to explain the observed $p_{T}$ dependence of the $Ω/φ$ ratio, and the influence of strong collective flow in the partonic stage evolution is considered as a possible origin for the changes in the curvature.

作者使用组分夸克等速组合模型来分析LHC能量下$pp$、$p$-Pb和Pb-Pb碰撞中$Ω/φ$比值的$p_{T}$依赖性。他们通过对实验数据中的$φ$介子应用夸克数缩放操作，提取强子化前奇异夸克的$p_{T}$谱。然后在不同碰撞系统中的高低多重数事件中研究奇异夸克的$p_{T}$谱的曲率特性。这些曲率特性被用来解释观测到的$Ω/φ$比值的$p_{T}$依赖性，并考虑部分子阶段演化中强集体流的影响作为曲率变化的可能来源。

Result: The results show that the relative change rate of the $Ω/φ$ ratio is dominated by the curvature property of the $p_{T}$ spectrum of strange quarks just before hadronization. The extracted $p_{T}$ spectra of strange quarks exhibit distinct curvature properties in high and low multiplicity events across different collision systems. These curvature properties are consistent with the observed $p_{T}$ dependence of the $Ω/φ$ ratio in $pp$, $p$-Pb, and Pb-Pb collisions at LHC energies. The influence of strong collective flow in the partonic stage evolution is proposed as a possible explanation for the changes in the curvature of the $p_{T}$ spectra of strange quarks.

结果显示，$Ω/φ$比值的相对变化率主要由强子化前奇异夸克的$p_{T}$谱的曲率特性主导。提取的奇异夸克的$p_{T}$谱在不同碰撞系统的高低多重数事件中表现出不同的曲率特性。这些曲率特性与LHC能量下$pp$、$p$-Pb和Pb-Pb碰撞中观测到的$Ω/φ$比值的$p_{T}$依赖性一致。部分子阶段演化中的强集体流影响被提出作为奇异夸克的$p_{T}$谱曲率变化的可能解释。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the curvature property of the $p_{T}$ spectrum of strange quarks just before hadronization plays a crucial role in determining the $p_{T}$ dependence of the $Ω/φ$ ratio in high-energy collisions. The extracted curvature properties are consistent with experimental observations and provide a deeper understanding of the hadronization process and the dynamics of strange quark production. The influence of strong collective flow in the partonic stage evolution is suggested as a potential mechanism for the observed changes in the curvature of the $p_{T}$ spectra of strange quarks.

研究表明，强子化前奇异夸克的$p_{T}$谱的曲率特性在确定高能碰撞中$Ω/φ$比值的$p_{T}$依赖性方面起着关键作用。提取的曲率特性与实验观测结果一致，提供了对强子化过程和奇异夸克产生动力学的更深入理解。部分子阶段演化中的强集体流影响被认为是奇异夸克的$p_{T}$谱曲率变化的潜在机制。

Abstract: We apply a constituent quark equal-velocity combination model to study the $p_{T}$ dependence of $Ω/φ$ ratio in $pp$, $p$-Pb and Pb-Pb collisions at LHC energies. We demonstrate that the relative change rate of the $Ω/φ$ ratio is dominated by a discrete curvature property of $p_{T}$ spectrum of strange quarks just before hadronization. Using experimental data of $φ$ mesons after a quark number scaling operation, we extract $p_{T}$ spectrum of strange quarks just before hadronization and study its curvature property in high and low multiplicity events in $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}=$ 7, 13 TeV, $p$-Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}$= 5.02 TeV and Pb-Pb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}$= 2.76 TeV. We apply these curvature properties of $p_{T}$ spectra of strange quarks to explain the observed $p_{T}$ dependence of $Ω/φ$ ratio in those collisions. We discuss the possible origin of the change of curvature property for $p_{T}$ spectra of strange quarks just before hadronization by considering the influence of strong collective flow formed in partonic stage evolution in collisions at LHC energies.

### [28] [Boost-invariant and cylindrically symmetric perfect spin hydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01857)
*Zbigniew Drogosz,Wojciech Florkowski,Jakub Witkowski*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper numerically solves the equations of a boost-invariant and cylindrically symmetric perfect hydrodynamics, inspired by the wounded nucleon model. It finds a coupling between the azimuthal and longitudinal components of the spin polarization tensor, leading to a nonzero total polarization due to the interaction of these components. The results can serve as a reference for more realistic hydrodynamic models.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the dynamics of a relativistic massive gas under boost-invariant and cylindrical symmetry, with a focus on the spin polarization tensor. The study aims to understand the coupling between different components of the spin polarization tensor and its effect on the total polarization, which has implications for the freeze-out hypersurface and the Pauli-Lubański four-vector.

动机是研究在具有推进不变性和圆柱对称性的条件下，相对论性大量气体的动力学，重点是自旋极化张量。研究旨在了解自旋极化张量不同分量之间的耦合及其对总极化的影响，这对冻结超曲面和Pauli-Lubański四矢量有影响。

Method: The method involves solving the equations of perfect hydrodynamics numerically, using the energy-momentum and spin tensors that describe a relativistic massive gas governed by Boltzmann statistics. The initial conditions are inspired by the wounded nucleon model, and the geometry is assumed to be boost-invariant and cylindrically symmetric. The freeze-out hypersurface is defined by a constant temperature condition, and the Pauli-Lubański four-vector is evaluated to determine the total polarization.

方法包括数值求解完美流体动力学方程，使用描述由Boltzmann统计支配的相对论性大量气体的能量动量张量和自旋张量。初始条件受到受伤核子模型的启发，几何形状假设为推进不变和圆柱对称。通过恒定温度条件定义冻结超曲面，并评估Pauli-Lubański四矢量以确定总极化。

Result: The results show a coupling between the azimuthal and longitudinal components of the electric and magnetic parts of the spin polarization tensor, similar to findings in Gubser symmetry. However, this study allows for more general initial conditions and expansion geometries. The only nonzero total polarization is induced by the interaction of the longitudinal component of the magnetic part of the spin polarization tensor with the azimuthal electric component.

结果表明，自旋极化张量的电部分和磁部分的方位角分量和纵向分量之间存在耦合，这与Gubser对称性中的发现相似。然而，本研究允许更一般的初始条件和膨胀几何形状。唯一非零的总极化是由自旋极化张量的磁部分的纵向分量与电部分的方位角分量之间的相互作用引起的。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the coupling between the azimuthal and longitudinal components of the spin polarization tensor leads to a specific pattern of total polarization, which can be used as a reference point for more realistic models of hydrodynamic expansion. This work provides a deeper understanding of the dynamics of relativistic gases under cylindrical symmetry and may have implications for heavy-ion collision experiments.

结论是，自旋极化张量的方位角分量和纵向分量之间的耦合导致了特定的总极化模式，这可以作为更现实的流体动力学膨胀模型的参考点。这项工作提供了对圆柱对称下相对论性气体动力学的更深入理解，并可能对重离子碰撞实验有影响。

Abstract: Equations of a boost-invariant and cylindrically symmetric perfect hydrodynamics are solved numerically for initial conditions inspired by the wounded nucleon model. The energy-momentum and spin tensors are used in the form that describes a relativistic massive gas governed by Boltzmann statistics. In contrast to one dimensional boost-invariant expansion, we find a coupling between the azimuthal and longitudinal components of the electric and magnetic components of the spin polarization tensor. This feature is similar to that found earlier for the Gubser symmetry, however, our treatment allows for a more general form of initial conditions and expansion geometry. Defining the freeze-out hypersurface by the constant temperature condition, we evaluate the Pauli-Lubański four-vector and find that for the assumed geometry the only nonzero total polarization may be induced by the longitudinal component of the magnetic part of the spin polarization tensor coupled with the azimuthal electric component. The obtained results may serve as a reference point for more realistic models of hydrodynamic expansion.

</details>


### [29] [Hunting for $B\bar B$ molecular state $X_{b0}$ via radiative transition of $Υ(10753)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01921)
*Yuan-Jun Gao,Gang Li,Shi-Dong Liu,Qi Wu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the radiative decay $\Upsilon(10753) \to \gamma X_{b0}$ using nonrelativistic effective field theory (NREFT). The $\Upsilon(10753)$ is modeled as an $S$-$D$ mixed state, and $X_{b0}$ as a weakly bound $B\bar{B}$ molecule. The decay is dominated by $B_1^{(\prime)}$ meson loops, with a predicted partial decay width of $0.2-1.5~\mathrm{keV}$, making it a promising channel for searching the $X_{b0}$ state.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to investigate the radiative decay $\Upsilon(10753) \to \gamma X_{b0}$ within the framework of nonrelativistic effective field theory (NREFT). The aim is to understand the nature of the $\Upsilon(10753)$ and $X_{b0}$ states, and to provide a theoretical basis for experimental searches of the $X_{b0}$ state, which is important for testing heavy-quark symmetries and understanding the exotic hadron spectrum in the bottom sector.

本文的动机是在非相对论有效场论（NREFT）框架内研究$\Upsilon(10753) \to \gamma X_{b0}$的辐射衰变。目的是理解$\Upsilon(10753)$和$X_{b0}$态的性质，并为实验搜索$X_{b0}$态提供理论基础，这对于测试重夸克对称性和理解底夸克扇区中的奇异强子谱非常重要。

Method: The method used in this paper involves treating the $\Upsilon(10753)$ as an $S$-$D$ mixed state of the $\Upsilon(4S)$ and $\YD$, while the $X_{b0}$ is interpreted as a weakly bound $B\bar{B}$ molecule with $J^{PC}=0^{++}$. The decay process is assumed to occur via intermediate meson loops involving the $S$-wave $B^{(*)}$ and $P$-wave $B_1^{(\prime)}$ mesons. The calculations are performed using nonrelativistic effective field theory (NREFT) to determine the partial decay width and branching fraction.

本文采用的方法是将$\Upsilon(10753)$视为$\Upsilon(4S)$和$\YD$的$S$-$D$混合态，而$X_{b0}$被解释为具有$J^{PC}=0^{++}$的弱束缚$B\bar{B}$分子。衰变过程假设通过涉及$S$波$B^{(*)}$和$P$波$B_1^{(\prime)}$介子的中间介子环进行。计算使用非相对论有效场论（NREFT）来确定部分衰变宽度和分支比。

Result: The results indicate that the decay $\Upsilon(10753) \to \gamma X_{b0}$ is dominated by the $B_1^{(\prime)}$ meson loops. The partial decay width is predicted to be in the range of $0.2-1.5~\mathrm{keV}$ for a binding energy range of $\varepsilon_X=0-10~\mathrm{MeV}$, corresponding to a branching fraction of $10^{-6}-10^{-5}$. The decay width is found to be insensitive to the full width of the $B_1^{\prime}$ meson.

结果表明，$\Upsilon(10753) \to \gamma X_{b0}$的衰变主要由$B_1^{(\prime)}$介子环主导。对于结合能范围$\varepsilon_X=0-10~\mathrm{MeV}$，预测的部分衰变宽度在$0.2-1.5~\mathrm{keV}$之间，对应的分支比为$10^{-6}-10^{-5}$。发现衰变宽度对$B_1^{\prime}$介子的全宽度不敏感。

Conclusion: The study suggests that the radiative decay of the $\Upsilon(10753)$ is a promising channel to search for the $X_{b0}$ state. This is crucial for testing heavy-quark symmetries and understanding the exotic hadron spectrum in the bottom sector.

研究表明，$\Upsilon(10753)$的辐射衰变是一个寻找$X_{b0}$态的有希望的通道。这对于测试重夸克对称性和理解底夸克扇区中的奇异强子谱至关重要。

Abstract: We investigate the radiative decay $Υ(10753) \to γX_{b0}$ within the framework of nonrelativistic effective field theory (NREFT). The $Υ(10753)$ is treated as an $S$-$D$ mixed state of the $Υ(4S)$ and $\YD$, while the $X_{b0}$ is interpreted as a weakly bound $B\bar{B}$ molecule with $J^{PC}=0^{++}$. The decay process was assumed to occur via the intermediate meson loops involving the $S$-wave $B^{(*)}$ and $P$-wave $B_1^{(\prime)}$ mesons. Our calculated results indicate that the decay $Υ(10753) \to γX_{b0}$ is dominated by the $B_1^{(\prime)}$ meson loops. The partial decay width is predicted to be $0.2-1.5~\mathrm{keV}$ for a binding energy range of $ε_X=0-10~\mathrm{MeV}$, corresponding to a branching fraction of $10^{-6}-10^{-5}$. The decay width is found to be insensitive to the full width of the $B_1^{\prime}$ meson. Our study suggests that the radiative decay of the $Υ(10753)$ is a promising channel to search for the $X_{b0}$ state, which is crucial for testing heavy-quark symmetries and understanding the exotic hadron spectrum in the bottom sector.

### [30] [Twist-3 transverse momentum dependent gluon distributions in a spectator model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01952)
*Xiupeng Xie,Zhun Lu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper examines twist-3 transverse momentum dependent distributions of gluons in a nucleon using a spectator model, where the nucleon emits a virtual gluon and an on-shell spectator particle. The authors parameterize the twist-3 gluon-gluon correlators and verify the equation of motion relation numerically, finding it to hold well in this model.

该论文使用旁观者模型研究了核子中胶子的扭曲-3横向动量依赖分布，其中核子发射一个虚拟胶子和一个在壳旁观者粒子。作者对扭曲-3胶子-胶子关联函数进行了参数化，并通过数值方法验证了运动方程关系，在该模型中发现这一关系成立良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this study is to understand the twist-3 transverse momentum dependent (TMD) distributions of gluons in a nucleon, which are important for understanding the internal structure of the nucleon and its interactions. These TMDs provide information about the partonic structure of the nucleon in both momentum and spin space, and are crucial for describing processes such as semi-inclusive deep inelastic scattering (SIDIS) and Drell-Yan lepton pair production.

本研究的动机是理解核子中胶子的扭曲-3横向动量依赖（TMD）分布，这对于理解核子的内部结构及其相互作用非常重要。这些TMD提供了关于核子在动量空间和自旋空间中的部分子结构的信息，并且对于描述诸如半包含深度非弹性散射（SIDIS）和Drell-Yan轻子对产生等过程至关重要。

Method: The method employed in this study involves the use of a spectator model, where the nucleon is described as emitting a virtual (time-like) gluon and an on-shell spectator particle. The mass of the spectator is treated continuously via a spectral function. The twist-3 gluon-gluon correlators, $\Phi^{+i;+-}$ and $\Phi^{ij;l+}$, are parameterized by a set of complex functions, with the real and imaginary parts corresponding to T-even and T-odd components, respectively. The authors then numerically check the equation of motion (EOM) relation for these distributions.

本研究采用的方法是使用旁观者模型，其中核子被描述为发射一个虚拟（类时）胶子和一个在壳旁观者粒子。旁观者的质量通过谱函数连续处理。扭曲-3胶子-胶子关联函数 $\Phi^{+i;+-}$ 和 $\Phi^{ij;l+}$ 由一组复函数参数化，实部和虚部分别对应于T-偶和T-奇分量。然后作者数值检查了这些分布的运动方程（EOM）关系。

Result: The results of the numerical check show that the equation of motion (EOM) relation holds fairly well within the spectator model. This indicates that the parameterization of the twist-3 gluon-gluon correlators is consistent with the underlying physics of the nucleon and provides a reliable framework for further studies of these distributions.

数值检查的结果表明，运动方程（EOM）关系在旁观者模型中成立良好。这表明扭曲-3胶子-胶子关联函数的参数化与核子的基本物理一致，并为这些分布的进一步研究提供了一个可靠的框架。

Conclusion: The conclusion drawn from this study is that the twist-3 transverse momentum dependent distributions of gluons in a nucleon can be effectively described using a spectator model. The parameterization of the twist-3 gluon-gluon correlators, and the verification of the EOM relation, support the validity of this approach for understanding the internal structure of the nucleon and its interactions.

从这项研究得出的结论是，核子中胶子的扭曲-3横向动量依赖分布可以通过旁观者模型有效地描述。扭曲-3胶子-胶子关联函数的参数化以及EOM关系的验证支持了这种方法在理解核子内部结构及其相互作用方面的有效性。

Abstract: We study the twist-3 transverse momentum dependent distributions of gluons in a nucleon within a spectator model framework. In this model, the nucleon is described as emitting a virtual (time-like) gluon and an on-shell spectator particle, with the spectator mass treated continuously via a spectral function. The twist-3 gluon-gluon correlators, $Φ^{+i;+-}$ and $Φ^{ij;l+}$, are parameterized by a set of complex functions, whose real and imaginary parts correspond to T-even and T-odd components, respectively. We numerically check the equation of motion relation for these distributions and find that relation holds fairly well in the spectator model.

### [31] [Non-Holomorphic Impact on $t-b-τ$ Yukawa Unification in minimal GMSB](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01980)
*Ali Çiçi,Büşra Niş,Cem Salih Ün*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores the low-scale implications of Yukawa unification in minimal gauge-mediated supersymmetry breaking models, incorporating non-holomorphic terms. It finds solutions consistent with the Higgs boson mass, leading to heavy strongly interacting SUSY particles and lighter electroweak sector particles. Charginos and staus are found to be as light as 120 GeV and 600 GeV, respectively, and can be tested soon via lifetime analyses and heavy Higgs boson searches.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the low scale implications of Yukawa unification (YU) within the context of minimal gauge-mediated supersymmetry breaking (GMSB) models, particularly by including non-holomorphic terms that allow for YU solutions with $\mu > 0$. The goal is to identify testable predictions at low scales that are compatible with YU and current experimental constraints, such as the Higgs boson mass.

动机是探索在最小规范介导的超对称破缺（GMSB）模型中，尤卡瓦统一（YU）在低尺度上的含义，特别是通过包括非全纯项，这些项允许在$\mu > 0$的情况下实现YU解。目标是识别与YU兼容且符合当前实验约束（如希格斯玻色子质量）的可测试的低尺度预测。

Method: The method involves a detailed analysis of the low-scale phenomenology of GMSB models with Yukawa unification, incorporating non-holomorphic terms. The authors consider the impact of these terms on the spectrum of supersymmetric (SUSY) particles, particularly focusing on the Higgs boson mass, chargino, neutralino, and stau masses. They also perform lifetime analyses for the light charginos and staus, and evaluate the compatibility of their findings with current and future experimental searches.

方法涉及详细分析具有尤卡瓦统一的GMSB模型的低尺度现象学，包括非全纯项。作者考虑了这些项对超对称（SUSY）粒子谱的影响，特别关注希格斯玻色子质量、带电轻子、最轻中性子和stau的质量。他们还对轻带电轻子和stau进行了寿命分析，并评估了他们的发现与当前和未来实验搜索的兼容性。

Result: The results show that the inclusion of non-holomorphic terms allows for a wide range of solutions consistent with the Higgs boson mass. These solutions predict heavy strongly interacting SUSY particles, while the electroweak sector can be relatively lighter. Notably, charginos can be as light as about 120 GeV and degenerate with the lightest neutralino, and staus can be as light as about 600 GeV. The lifetime analyses indicate that light charginos decay in about $10^{-2}$ ns, and staus have lifetimes that make them testable in the near future. The solutions are also compatible with heavy Higgs boson searches.

结果显示，包含非全纯项可以得到与希格斯玻色子质量一致的广泛解。这些解预测强相互作用的SUSY粒子较重，而电弱部门可以相对较轻。值得注意的是，带电轻子可以轻至约120 GeV，并且与最轻的中性子简并，stau可以轻至约600 GeV。寿命分析表明，轻带电轻子的衰变时间约为$10^{-2}$ ns，而stau的寿命使其在未来不久即可进行测试。这些解也与重希格斯玻色子搜索兼容。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the incorporation of non-holomorphic terms in GMSB models with Yukawa unification leads to a rich set of low-scale implications, including the possibility of light charginos and staus. These particles can be probed in the near future through lifetime analyses and heavy Higgs boson searches. The benchmark scenarios provided in the paper offer concrete examples of how these solutions can be tested experimentally.

结论是，在具有尤卡瓦统一的GMSB模型中引入非全纯项会导致丰富的低尺度含义，包括轻带电轻子和stau的可能性。这些粒子可以通过寿命分析和重希格斯玻色子搜索在不久的将来进行探测。论文中提供的基准情景提供了如何实验测试这些解的具体示例。

Abstract: We study and explore the low scale implications of Yukawa unification in the minimal gauge mediated supersymmetry breaking models. We also assume non-zero non-holomorphic terms, with which the YU solutions can be accommodated in the cases with $μ> 0$. These results can be considered a direct effect from the non-holomorphic terms, but they also lead to testable low scale implications compatible with YU. We observe abundant solutions consistent with the Higgs boson mass. This constraint leads to heavy strongly interacting supersymmetric particles, while the electroweak sector can be realized relatively lighter and they can be probed by several experiments. We find that the chargino can be lighter than 1 TeV and it is degenerate with the lightest neutralino in most of such solutions. Consistent solutions in this region can accommodate charginos as light as about 120 GeV, and they will be tested more likely soon by the analyses over the compressed spectra. These solutions are also be subjected in the lifetime analyses. Our analyses identify such light charginos decaying in about $10^{-2}$ ns. Probing such points may need a slight improvement in sensitivity of the analyses, and one can expect them to be tested very soon. In the same region, stau is realized to be another light supersymmetric particle, and some of the solutions can be inconsistently lighter. We find that it can weigh as light as about 600 GeV consistently, and it can be tested also soon over its lifetime. We summarize and also exemplify our findings with five benchmark scenarios. Most of the benchmark solutions also reveal that the solutions can be tested in heavy Higgs boson searches, which shape the whole Higgs boson spectrum in models.

### [32] [Pair creation via Amplitude-Modulated Periodic and Quasiperiodic Pulse Sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02515)
*Deepak Sah*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores nonperturbative pair production in alternating-sign electric field pulse trains, using a quantum kinetic approach. It compares the effects of periodic and quasiperiodic (Fibonacci-ordered) pulse sequences on the longitudinal momentum spectrum and particle yield. Periodic sequences lead to regular interference patterns, while quasiperiodic ones cause spectral fragmentation and localization. The study shows that temporal ordering mainly redistributes spectral weight, with the total yield primarily determined by the effective field strength.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the impact of different temporal orderings (periodic vs. quasiperiodic) in electric field pulse trains on the nonperturbative pair production. The authors aim to establish long-range temporal ordering as an effective control parameter for multipulse Schwinger pair production, which can guide the design of tailored pulse sequences in high-intensity laser experiments.

动机是理解不同时间顺序（周期性与准周期性）的电场脉冲序列对非微扰粒子产生过程的影响。作者旨在将长程时间顺序确立为多脉冲施温格粒子产生过程中的有效控制参数，这可以指导高强度激光实验中定制脉冲序列的设计。

Method: The method involves a quantum kinetic approach to analyze the longitudinal momentum spectrum and particle yield for pulse sequences with either strictly periodic or quasiperiodic (Fibonacci-ordered) temporal structure. The study considers pulse trains with N=12 and N=20 pulses, varying the field-strength ratio to observe the effects on the spectra and yields.

方法涉及使用量子动力学方法来分析具有严格周期或准周期（斐波那契序）时间结构的脉冲序列的纵向动量谱和粒子产额。研究考虑了N=12和N=20脉冲的脉冲序列，并改变场强比以观察其对光谱和产额的影响。

Result: For N=12 pulses, periodic trains generate regularly modulated spectra characteristic of multi-slit (Ramsey-type) interference, whereas Fibonacci sequences produce fragmented structures and partial momentum-space localization. Increasing the pulse number to N=20 enhances these effects: periodic driving yields sharper and higher-contrast interference fringes, while quasiperiodic ordering leads to stronger localization and increasingly irregular spectral features. The particle yield exhibits a strongly nonlinear dependence on the field-strength ratio, with quasiperiodic sequences yielding slightly larger values than the periodic case for stronger fields.

对于N=12个脉冲，周期性序列产生具有多缝（拉姆齐型）干涉特征的规则调制光谱，而斐波那契序列则产生碎片化结构和部分动量空间局域化。增加脉冲数量到N=20会增强这些效应：周期性驱动产生更尖锐和对比度更高的干涉条纹，而准周期排序导致更强的局域化和越来越不规则的光谱特征。粒子产额对场强比表现出强烈的非线性依赖，在较强场下，准周期序列产生的值略大于周期性情况。

Conclusion: The results show that temporal ordering primarily redistributes spectral weight in momentum space, while the integrated yield is governed predominantly by the effective field strength. Long-range temporal ordering is established as an effective control parameter in multipulse Schwinger pair production, providing guidance for designing tailored pulse sequences in future high-intensity laser experiments.

结果表明，时间顺序主要在动量空间中重新分配光谱权重，而总产额主要由有效场强决定。长程时间顺序被确立为多脉冲施温格粒子产生过程中的有效控制参数，为未来高强度激光实验中设计定制脉冲序列提供了指导。

Abstract: We study nonperturbative pair production driven by alternating-sign electric field pulse trains. Using a quantum kinetic approach, we analyze both the longitudinal momentum spectrum and the particle yield for pulse sequences with either strictly periodic temporal structure, in which the pulse amplitudes alternate in a regular and repeating (E_1, E_2) pattern, or quasiperiodic (Fibonacci-ordered) structure, where the amplitudes follow a deterministic but aperiodic sequence generated by the Fibonacci substitution rule, exhibiting long-range order without exact repetition. For N=12 pulses, periodic trains generate regularly modulated spectra characteristic of multi-slit (Ramsey-type) interference, whereas Fibonacci sequences produce fragmented structures and partial momentum-space localization. Increasing the pulse number to N=20 further enhances these effects: periodic driving yields sharper and higher-contrast interference fringes, while quasiperiodic ordering leads to stronger localization and increasingly irregular spectral features.The particle yield exhibits a strongly nonlinear dependence on the field-strength ratio. For weak modulation , both temporal orderings produce nearly identical yields. For stronger fields, a modest crossover behavior is observed, with quasiperiodic sequences yielding slightly larger values than the periodic case. Overall, temporal ordering primarily redistributes spectral weight in momentum space, while the integrated yield is governed predominantly by the effective field strength. These results establish long-range temporal ordering as an effective control parameter in multipulse Schwinger pair production and provide guidance for designing tailored pulse sequences in future high-intensity laser experiments.

</details>


### [33] [Detectability of Magnetar-Induced Vacuum Birefringence with IXPE and eXTP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02541)
*Fayez Abu-Ajamieh*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper evaluates the potential for detecting vacuum birefringence from magnetars using IXPE and eXTP, with a more realistic magnetic field model leading to larger time delays. The Stokes parameters are calculated, and 1RXS J170849.0-400910 is identified as the best candidate for detection.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the feasibility of quantitatively detecting vacuum birefringence from magnetars using the upcoming IXPE and eXTP experiments. Previous studies have estimated the time delay and phase difference in polarization eigenmodes, but this work aims to refine these estimates by adopting a more realistic magnetic field profile of magnetars.

本文的动机是探讨使用即将进行的IXPE和eXTP实验定量检测磁星真空双折射效应的可行性。先前的研究已经估计了偏振本征模式中的时间延迟和相位差，但本文旨在通过采用更现实的磁星磁场轮廓来改进这些估计。

Method: The authors use a realistic profile to model the magnetic field of magnetars, which is then used to calculate the time delay and phase difference in the parallel and perpendicular components of polarization eigenmodes. Adler's integral formula is applied to perform these calculations. Additionally, the Stokes parameters for all known magnetars are computed to assess the detectability with IXPE and eXTP.

作者使用一个现实的模型来模拟磁星的磁场，然后利用该模型计算偏振本征模式中平行和垂直分量的时间延迟和相位差。应用Adler积分公式来进行这些计算。此外，还计算了所有已知磁星的Stokes参数，以评估IXPE和eXTP的可检测性。

Result: The results show that the time delay could be an order of magnitude larger than previous estimates in the literature. Furthermore, the calculations of the Stokes parameters indicate that both IXPE and eXTP are capable of quantitatively measuring birefringence from magnetars, with the magnetar 1RXS J170849.0-400910 being the most promising candidate for detection.

结果表明，时间延迟可能比文献中先前的估计大一个数量级。此外，Stokes参数的计算表明，IXPE和eXTP都能够定量测量来自磁星的双折射效应，其中磁星1RXS J170849.0-400910是最有希望的探测候选者。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the use of a realistic magnetic field profile for magnetars leads to a significant increase in the estimated time delay for vacuum birefringence. This, combined with the capability of IXPE and eXTP to measure the Stokes parameters, suggests that 1RXS J170849.0-400910 is the best candidate for the detection of vacuum birefringence, providing a strong case for future observational efforts.

研究表明，使用现实的磁星磁场轮廓会导致真空双折射估计的时间延迟显著增加。结合IXPE和eXTP测量Stokes参数的能力，这表明1RXS J170849.0-400910是检测真空双折射的最佳候选者，为未来的观测努力提供了有力的支持。

Abstract: We analyze the prospects of quantitatively detecting vacuum birefringence from magnetars using the IXPE and eXTP experiments. We adopt a realistic profile to model the magnetic field of magnetars, and use it to calculate the time delay and phase difference in the parallel and perpendicular components of polarization eigenmodes using Adler's integral formula. We find that the time delay could be an order of magnitude larger than previous estimates in the literature. We also calculate the Stokes parameters for all known magnetars and show that both IXPE and eXTP are capable of quantitatively measuring birefringence from magnetars, with the magnetar dubbed 1RXS J170849.0-400910 being the best candidate for detection.

### [34] [How neutrinos could help solving cosmological anomalies and tensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02547)
*Pasquale Di Bari*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper discusses how neutrinos might help resolve cosmological anomalies and tensions, including the neutrino mass tension and the excess radio background. A boomerang mechanism is proposed, where dark neutrinos are transferred to the dark sector and later return as photons, potentially explaining these phenomena and predicting an effective neutrino magnetic moment within experimental reach.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the potential role of neutrinos in resolving several anomalies and tensions in cosmology. Specifically, it aims to address the discrepancy between the cosmological observations and neutrino oscillation experiments regarding neutrino masses, and the unexplained excess in the cosmic radio background. The paper also seeks to propose a novel mechanism that could explain these phenomena while being consistent with current experimental constraints on the neutrino magnetic moment.

本文的动机是探讨中微子在解决宇宙学中若干异常和张力中的潜在作用。具体来说，它旨在解决宇宙学观测与中微子振荡实验之间关于中微子质量的差异，以及无法解释的宇宙射电背景过剩问题。文章还试图提出一种新的机制，该机制能够解释这些现象，同时符合当前对中微子磁矩的实验限制。

Method: The method employed in this paper involves the theoretical exploration of a boomerang mechanism. This mechanism proposes that at $t \sim 100\,{\rm s}$ and $T \sim 100\,{\rm keV}$, the visible sector transfers dark neutrinos into the dark sector. Later, at approximately the present time, the dark sector returns photons back to the visible sector. This process is designed to circumvent the upper bound on the neutrino effective magnetic moment and to provide a plausible explanation for the observed anomalies and tensions in cosmology.

本文采用的方法是对回旋镖机制进行理论探索。该机制提出，在$t \sim 100\,{\rm s}$ 和 $T \sim 100\,{\rm keV}$时，可见部门将暗中微子转移到暗部门。然后，在大约现在的时间，暗部门将光子返回到可见部门。这个过程旨在规避中微子有效磁矩的上限，并为宇宙学中观察到的异常和张力提供一个合理的解释。

Result: The proposed boomerang mechanism predicts an effective neutrino magnetic moment that could be within the reach of future experiments. Additionally, it suggests a possible contribution to the 21 cm cosmological signal. The mechanism offers a potential solution to both the neutrino mass tension and the excess radio background mystery, making it a promising avenue for further research into beyond-the-standard-model (BSM) physics.

所提出的回旋镖机制预测了一个可能在未来实验中达到的有效中微子磁矩。此外，它还暗示了对21厘米宇宙信号的可能贡献。该机制为中微子质量张力和射电背景过剩之谜提供了潜在的解决方案，使其成为进一步研究超出标准模型（BSM）物理的一个有希望的方向。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the boomerang mechanism, involving the transfer of dark neutrinos to the dark sector and their eventual return as photons, is a promising approach to resolving the neutrino mass tension and the excess radio background. It opens up new possibilities for detecting BSM physics through upcoming experiments and observations, particularly in the context of the 21 cm cosmological signal and the measurement of the neutrino magnetic moment.

本文得出结论，涉及将暗中微子转移到暗部门并最终以光子形式返回的回旋镖机制，是解决中微子质量张力和射电背景过剩的一种有前景的方法。它为通过即将进行的实验和观测来探测超出标准模型（BSM）物理开辟了新的可能性，特别是在21厘米宇宙信号和中微子磁矩测量的背景下。

Abstract: In this talk I discuss how neutrinos might help solving or alleviating different anomalies and tensions in cosmology. Invisible decays of the heaviest relic neutrinos might provide a way to solve the neutrino mass tension between cosmological observations and neutrino oscillation experiments. The excess radio background mystery could be explained by radiative decays of relic neutrinos. However, the upper bound on the neutrino effective magnetic moment requires some trick to be circumvented. To this extent, I discuss a recently proposed boomerang mechanism in which the visible sector throws dark neutrinos into the dark sector at $t \sim 100\,{\rm s}$ and $T \sim 100\,{\rm keV}$, and much later (basically at the present time) the dark sector throws back photons into the visible sector. The mechanism predicts an effective neutrino magnetic moment that might be within the reach of next experiments. Some contribution to the 21 cm cosmological signal is also expected. These are exciting times for cosmological searches of BSM physics.

</details>


### [35] [Studying the Infrared Behaviour of Improved Logarithmic Accuracy Parton Showers with Herwig](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02622)
*Jack Holguin,Simon Plätzer,Michael H. Seymour,Siddharth Sule*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper implements and studies two next-to-leading-logarithmic (NLL) dipole shower algorithms in the Herwig event generator, comparing them with existing algorithms. The study highlights the importance of the infrared cutoff and its impact on hadronization, proposing it as a starting point for further research. Finally, the tunability of the models is assessed, and best-fit parameters are identified.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to improve the accuracy and physical realism of parton shower simulations in the Herwig event generator by implementing and studying two new NLL dipole shower algorithms. The focus is on their performance in different regimes, including the logarithmic, hard, and infrared, and their interplay with the hadronization model.

动机是通过在Herwig事件生成器中实现和研究两种新的NLL偶极子淋浴算法来提高部分子淋浴模拟的准确性和物理现实性。重点在于它们在对数、硬和红外不同区域的表现，以及与强子化模型的相互作用。

Method: The method involves implementing the two NLL dipole shower algorithms into the Herwig event generator, comparing their properties with the existing dipole and angular ordered parton shower algorithms. The study includes NLO matching in the hard regime and cluster hadronization in the infrared regime. The infrared cutoff used by each shower is precisely defined and its impact on the hadronization process is analyzed.

方法包括将两种NLL偶极子淋浴算法实现到Herwig事件生成器中，并将其特性与现有的偶极子和角序部分子淋浴算法进行比较。该研究包括在硬区域中的NLO匹配和在红外区域中的簇强子化。精确定义每个淋浴使用的红外截止点，并分析其对强子化过程的影响。

Result: The results show that the new NLL dipole shower algorithms have improved properties in the logarithmic regime and play important roles in the hard and infrared regimes. The differences in the infrared cutoffs between the showers lead to significant consequences at the hadron level, suggesting a need for further investigation into the interplay between parton showers and hadronization models.

结果表明，新的NLL偶极子淋浴算法在对数区域具有改进的特性，并在硬和红外区域发挥重要作用。淋浴之间的红外截止点差异导致了强子水平上的显著后果，这表明需要进一步研究部分子淋浴和强子化模型之间的相互作用。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the new NLL dipole shower algorithms provide a more accurate and physically realistic description of parton showers, especially in the infrared regime. The study emphasizes the importance of the infrared cutoff and its role in the initial state for hadronization. The tunability of the models is also assessed, and best-fit parameters are identified for each algorithm.

结论是，新的NLL偶极子淋浴算法提供了更准确和物理上更现实的部分子淋浴描述，特别是在红外区域。研究强调了红外截止点的重要性及其作为强子化初始状态的作用。还评估了模型的可调性，并为每种算法确定了最佳拟合参数。

Abstract: We have implemented two recently proposed dipole shower algorithms that have next-to-leading-logarithmic accuracy at leading colour in the Herwig event generator. We study their properties and compare them to Herwig's existing dipole and angular ordered parton shower algorithms. In addition to their improved properties in the logarithmic regime, we find important roles for their extrapolations into the hard regime, where we perform NLO matching, and into the infrared regime, where we perform cluster hadronization. We emphasise the importance of this infrared regime and the precise definition of the infrared cutoff used by each shower as the initial state for Herwig's hadronization model. Studying the results at the hadron level, we find important consequences of this infrared cutoff difference and propose it as a starting point for further study of the interplay between parton showers and hadronization models. We conclude by studying the models' tunability and identifying the best-fit parameters for each.

</details>


### [36] [Axion electron-electron interaction in the RaOH molecule to search for Dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02775)
*Mikhail Reiter,Anna Zakharova*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper explores the potential of using the RaOH molecule for detecting axion-mediated electron-electron interactions, employing a combination of Generalized relativistic effective core potential and One-center restoration technique to account for molecular rotations and vibrations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Axions are considered promising candidates for dark matter. The motivation of this paper is to investigate the feasibility of using the RaOH molecule as a means to experimentally detect axion-mediated electron-electron interactions, which could provide evidence for the existence of axions and their role in dark matter.

轴子被认为是暗物质的有力候选者。本文的动机是研究使用RaOH分子作为实验检测轴子介导的电子-电子相互作用的方法的可行性，这可以为轴子的存在及其在暗物质中的作用提供证据。

Method: The authors employ a combination of the Generalized relativistic effective core potential (GRECP) and the One-center restoration technique to accurately model the RaOH molecule under various rotational and vibrational states. This approach allows for the consideration of the complex electronic structure of the molecule, including relativistic effects, and the restoration of the correct four-component spinors, which are essential for the accurate description of the electron-electron interactions mediated by axions.

作者结合广义相对论有效芯势（GRECP）和单中心恢复技术来准确建模处于各种旋转和振动状态下的RaOH分子。这种方法能够考虑包括相对论效应在内的分子复杂的电子结构，并恢复正确的四分量旋量，这对于准确描述由轴子介导的电子-电子相互作用至关重要。

Result: The results of the study demonstrate that the RaOH molecule can be effectively used for the detection of axion-mediated electron-electron interactions, with the computational methods employed providing a reliable framework for accounting for the molecular dynamics and electronic structure. The use of GRECP and the One-center restoration technique ensures that the calculations are both accurate and comprehensive, allowing for a detailed analysis of the potential signal from axion exchange.

研究表明，RaOH分子可以有效地用于检测轴子介导的电子-电子相互作用，所采用的计算方法为考虑分子动力学和电子结构提供了可靠的框架。GRECP和单中心恢复技术的使用确保了计算既准确又全面，从而能够对轴子交换的潜在信号进行详细分析。

Conclusion: The conclusion of the paper is that the RaOH molecule, when analyzed using advanced computational techniques such as GRECP and the One-center restoration technique, shows promise as a tool for the experimental detection of axion-mediated electron-electron interactions. This work provides a foundation for future experimental efforts to search for axions, contributing to the broader understanding of dark matter.

论文的结论是，通过使用如广义相对论有效芯势（GRECP）和单中心恢复技术等先进的计算技术分析，RaOH分子作为实验检测轴子介导的电子-电子相互作用的工具显示出潜力。这项工作为未来寻找轴子的实验努力奠定了基础，有助于更广泛地理解暗物质。

Abstract: Axions are promising candidates for the role of Dark matter particles. In this paper, the question of the suitability of the RaOH molecule for the experimental detection of electron-electron interactions through the exchange of axions is studied. To take into account an impact of the rotations and vibrations a computation must be performed for a large number of molecular configurations. In this work we study this problem using a combination of the Generalized relativistic effective core potential and One-center restoration technique of the correct four-component spinors.

### [37] [Collins asymmetries for pion-in-jet production in polarized $\ell p$ collisions at the EIC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02890)
*Umberto D'Alesio,Carlo Flore,Marco Zaccheddu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates Collins azimuthal asymmetries in pion-in-jet production during polarized lepton-proton collisions, using a simplified TMD approach and transversity and Collins fragmentation functions. The study includes both leading order calculations and the Weizsäcker-Williams approximation for quasireal photon exchange, showing that quark-initiated channels dominate over gluon ones. This research aims to provide a clearer understanding of the transversity distribution, including its sea-quark component, and to test the universality of the Collins function and TMD factorization.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to extend the analysis of Collins azimuthal asymmetries from polarized $pp$ scattering to polarized lepton-proton collisions, which is theoretically simpler and complementary. The goal is to gain a clearer access to the transversity distribution, including the sea-quark component, and to test the hypothesis of the universality of the Collins function and TMD factorization.

动机是将Collins方位角不对称性的分析从极化$pp$散射扩展到极化轻子-质子碰撞，这在理论上更简单且具有互补性。目标是更清楚地了解横向度分布，包括海夸克成分，并检验Collins函数和TMD因子化的普遍性假设。

Method: The method involves adopting a simplified transverse momentum dependent (TMD) approach with a collinear configuration for the initial state. The transversity and Collins fragmentation functions are used as extracted from semi-inclusive deep inelastic scattering and $e^+ e^-$ annihilation processes. Azimuthal asymmetries are computed for EIC kinematics at leading order (LO) and by including quasireal photon exchange in the Weizsäcker-Williams approximation.

该方法采用简化的横向动量依赖（TMD）方法，初始状态为共线构型。使用从半包容深度非弹性散射和$e^+ e^-$湮灭过程中提取的横向度和Collins碎片函数。计算了EIC动力学下的方位角不对称性，包括在Weizsäcker-Williams近似下考虑准实光子交换的领头阶（LO）计算。

Result: The results show that the contribution from quasireal photon exchange is significant throughout the kinematic range but does not affect the dominance of quark-initiated channels. The role of gluon-initiated channels remains marginal. This allows for a clearer access to the transversity distribution, particularly the sea-quark component.

结果表明，准实光子交换在整个动力学范围内都有显著贡献，但不影响夸克引发通道的主导地位。胶子引发通道的作用仍然很小。这使得对横向度分布的访问更加清晰，特别是对于海夸克成分。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that Collins azimuthal asymmetries in lepton-proton processes provide a clearer access to the transversity distribution, including its sea-quark component. Future EIC data could further test the universality of the Collins function and TMD factorization for this class of processes.

结论是，在轻子-质子过程中，Collins方位角不对称性提供了对横向度分布更清晰的访问，包括其海夸克成分。未来的EIC数据可以进一步测试Collins函数和这类过程的TMD因子化的普遍性。

Abstract: We study Collins azimuthal asymmetries in pion-in-jet production in polarized lepton-proton collisions, extending previous analyses of polarized $pp$ scattering to a complementary and theoretically simpler process. We keep adopting a simplified transverse momentum dependent (TMD) approach, with a collinear configuration for the initial state, and employ the transversity and Collins fragmentation functions as extracted from semi-inclusive deep inelastic scattering and $e^+ e^-$ annihilation processes. We then compute azimuthal asymmetries for the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC) kinematics, both within a leading order (LO) approach and by including quasireal photon exchange in the Weizsäcker-Williams approximation. Although this contribution is relevant in the whole kinematical range explored, it does not spoil the dominance of quark-initiated channels, leaving only a marginal role to their gluon counterparts. In this respect, Collins asymmetries in lepton-proton processes allow for a much clearer access to the transversity distribution, including its sea-quark component. As we will argue, a comparison with future EIC data could represent a further step in testing the hypothesis of the universality of the Collins function as well as of the TMD factorization for this class of processes.

</details>

### [38] [A gravity interpretation for the complex Euclidean saddles of the ABJM index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00987)
*Minwoo Suh*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper resolves the puzzle of divergent contributions in the superconformal index of ABJM theory by showing the instability of wrapped M5-branes, analogous to the resolution for $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand and resolve the issue of divergent contributions in the superconformal index of ABJM theory, similar to the resolved problem in $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory. The authors aim to show that the divergence can be attributed to the instability of wrapped M5-branes, providing a consistent explanation with the gravitational on-shell action.

Method: The method involves studying the superconformal index of ABJM theory, which is a grand-canonical partition function counting 1/16-BPS states. The authors analyze the Legendre transform of the index with respect to reduced chemical potentials and examine the contributions from shifted terms. They then investigate the corresponding gravitational system, focusing on the instability of wrapped M5-branes as a criterion for the divergence.

Result: The result is the identification of the instability of wrapped M5-branes as the cause of the divergent contributions in the superconformal index of ABJM theory. This finding parallels the resolution for $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory, where the divergence was linked to the instability of wrapped D3-branes.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the divergence in the superconformal index of ABJM theory can be explained by the instability of wrapped M5-branes, providing a consistent analogy with the previously resolved case in $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory. This work strengthens the understanding of the connection between the superconformal index and the gravitational on-shell action.

Abstract: The superconformal index is a grand-canonical partition function that counts the 1/16-BPS states in the theory, and its Legendre transform with respect to reduced chemical potentials accounts for the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy of electrically charged rotating black holes in anti-de Sitter spacetime. However, the superconformal index of $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory appears to allow shifts in chemical potentials, and the contributions of the shifted terms diverge exponentially. This puzzle was resolved by showing the instability of wrapped D3-branes corresponding to the shifts in the gravitational on-shell action. Analogously, we study the ABJM index and the M5-brane instability criterion.

### [39] [Reconstructing conformal field theoretical compositions with Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01072)
*Haotian Cao,Garrett Merz,Kyle Cranmer,Gary Shiu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates the use of transformers to accurately reconstruct the compositions of tensor products of 2D rational conformal field theories (RCFTs) from their low-energy spectra, achieving 98% accuracy and showing potential for application in AdS/CFT bulk reconstruction.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a new method using transformers for reconstructing the compositions of tensor product RCFTs based on their low-energy spectra. This task is inherently challenging due to its combinatorial nature, and the goal is to provide a tool that can generalize to CFTs with larger central charges and unseen classes of RCFTs.

动机是开发一种使用transformers的新方法，根据低能谱重构张量积RCFT的组成。由于其组合性质，这项任务本身具有挑战性，目标是提供一种可以推广到具有更大中心电荷和未见过的RCFT类别的工具。

Method: The authors employ transformers, a type of deep learning model, to analyze and reconstruct the compositions of tensor products of two-dimensional rational conformal field theories (RCFTs). The models are trained on data sets characterized by central charges and affine Lie algebra labels, and they demonstrate high accuracy in recovering the constituents of tensor products constructed from Wess-Zumino-Witten (WZW) models. Additionally, the method shows generalizability to CFTs with larger central charges and unseen RCFT classes by incorporating a small number of out-of-domain examples.

作者使用一种深度学习模型——transformers，来分析和重构二维有理共形场论（RCFT）的张量积组成。这些模型在由中心电荷和仿射李代数标签表征的数据集上进行训练，并展示了从Wess-Zumino-Witten (WZW) 模型构建的张量积成分恢复的高准确性。此外，通过引入少量域外示例，该方法显示出对具有更大中心电荷和未见过的RCFT类别的泛化能力。

Result: The results show that the transformers achieve 98% accuracy in reconstructing the compositions of tensor product RCFTs from their low-energy spectra. Furthermore, the method generalizes well to CFTs with larger central charges and unseen classes of RCFTs, even when only a small number of out-of-domain examples are added to the training set.

结果表明，transformers在从低能谱重构张量积RCFT的组成方面达到了98%的准确性。此外，即使只向训练集中添加少量域外示例，该方法也能很好地推广到具有更大中心电荷和未见过的RCFT类别。

Conclusion: The study concludes that transformers are an effective tool for reconstructing the compositions of tensor product RCFTs based on their low-energy spectra. The high accuracy and generalizability of the method suggest that it has the potential to be a valuable tool for bulk reconstruction in the context of AdS/CFT.

研究得出结论，transformers是根据低能谱重构张量积RCFT组成的有效工具。该方法的高准确性和泛化能力表明，它有可能成为AdS/CFT背景下体重构的有价值的工具。

Abstract: We study the use of transformers to reconstruct the compositions of tensor products of two-dimensional rational conformal field theories (RCFTs) based on their low-energy spectra. The task is challenging due to its combinatorial nature. The constituent theories are characterized by their central charges and affine Lie algebra labels. We achieve 98% accuracy in recovering the constituents of tensor products theories constructed from Wess-Zumino-Witten models. We further demonstrate that our method generalizes to CFTs with larger central charge and unseen classes of RCFTs by adding a small number of out-of-domain examples. Our results show that transformers are effective at this task and point towards a new tool for bulk reconstruction in AdS/CFT.

### [40] [Twist Operator BOPE and Entanglement Entropy in 2D Interface CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01150)
*Mianqi Wang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper explores the entanglement entropy in 2D interface CFTs using the replica method and introduces the boundary OPE (BOPE) of the R\u00e9nyi twist operator, leading to a new way to calculate the $O(1)$ contribution to the entanglement entropy. The results are consistent with previous holographic studies.

本文使用复制法探讨了2D界面CFTs中的纠缠熵，并引入了R\u00e9nyi扭曲算子的边界OPE（BOPE），提出了一种计算纠缠熵$O(1)$贡献的新方法。结果与之前的全息研究一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of the paper is to explore the entanglement entropy in 2D interface conformal field theories (CFTs) using a more refined approach than what has been previously applied to boundary CFTs. By considering the boundary OPE (BOPE) of the R\u00e9nyi twist operator, the authors aim to provide a deeper understanding of the $O(1)$ contribution to the entanglement entropy, which is not captured by standard methods.

本文的动机是探索2D界面共形场论（CFTs）中的纠缠熵，采用比之前应用于边界CFTs更精细的方法。通过考虑R\u00e9nyi扭曲算子的边界OPE（BOPE），作者旨在更深入地理解标准方法无法捕捉到的纠缠熵的$O(1)$贡献。

Method: The authors use the replica method to address the entanglement entropy of 2D interface CFT. They introduce the boundary OPE (BOPE) of the R\u00e9nyi twist operator, which leads to the identification of a boundary twist operator anchored on the interface. This novel approach allows them to express the $O(1)$ contribution to the entanglement entropy in terms of the BOPE coefficients of the twist operator.

作者使用复制法处理2D界面CFT的纠缠熵。他们引入了R\u00e9nyi扭曲算子的边界OPE（BOPE），这导致识别出一个锚定在界面上的边界扭曲算子。这种新颖的方法使他们能够用扭曲算子的BOPE系数来表示纠缠熵的$O(1)$贡献。

Result: The key result of the paper is the derivation of the $O(1)$ contribution to the entanglement entropy using the BOPE coefficients of the R\u00e9nyi twist operator. The authors also analyze the entanglement entropy for different intervals and find consistency with previous holographic calculations, thus validating their approach.

论文的关键结果是利用R\u00e9nyi扭曲算子的BOPE系数推导出纠缠熵的$O(1)$贡献。作者还分析了不同区间的纠缠熵，并发现与之前的全息计算一致，从而验证了他们的方法。

Conclusion: The paper concludes by comparing the entanglement entropy of different intervals with previous holographic results, validating the BOPE approach and providing a new method for calculating the $O(1)$ contribution to the entanglement entropy in 2D interface CFTs.

该论文通过将不同区间内的纠缠熵与先前的全息结果进行比较，验证了BOPE方法的有效性，并为计算2D界面CFT中$O(1)$贡献的纠缠熵提供了一种新方法。

Abstract: We address several aspects of entanglement entropy of 2D interface CFT using the replica method. Unlike the case of boundary CFT, we consider the boundary OPE (BOPE) of the Rényi twist operator and find a boundary twist operator anchored on the interface. This approach gives the $O(1)$ contribution to the entanglement entropy in terms of the BOPE coefficients of the twist operator. We further analyze entanglement entropy of different intervals and compare our findings with previous holographic results.

### [41] [Exact WKB and Quantum Periods for Extremal Black Hole Quasinormal Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01321)
*Yasuyuki Hatsuda,Tomohito Shiga*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper applies exact WKB analysis to the spectral problem in black hole perturbation theory, leading to quantization conditions for quasinormal modes. By computing quantum periods (Voros symbols) and using Borel--Padé resummation, it reproduces quasinormal mode frequencies with high precision for extremal Reissner--Nordström and Kerr black holes.

该论文将精确WKB分析应用于黑洞微扰理论中的谱问题，从而得到准正模的量子化条件。通过计算量子周期（Voros符号）并使用Borel--Padé重求和方法，它以高精度重现了极端Reissner--Nordström和Kerr黑洞的准正模频率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a more accurate and systematic approach to determine the quasinormal mode frequencies of black holes, which are crucial for understanding the dynamics and stability of black holes. The exact WKB method provides a powerful tool for solving the quantization conditions arising from the boundary conditions of quasinormal modes.

动机是开发一种更准确和系统的方法来确定黑洞的准正模频率，这对于理解黑洞的动力学和稳定性至关重要。精确WKB方法为解决由准正模边界条件引起的量子化条件提供了一个强大的工具。

Method: The authors apply the exact WKB analysis to the spectral problem in black hole perturbation theory. They derive exact quantization conditions for the complex frequencies of quasinormal modes. To solve these conditions, they compute the quantum periods, or Voros symbols, up to very high orders in the WKB expansion. They then use Borel--Padé resummation to obtain the resummed quantization conditions.

作者将精确WKB分析应用于黑洞微扰理论中的谱问题。他们推导出准正模复频率的精确量子化条件。为了解决这些条件，他们计算了WKB展开中非常高阶的量子周期（即Voros符号）。然后，他们使用Borel--Padé重求和方法来获得重求和后的量子化条件。

Result: The resummed quantization conditions successfully reproduce the correct quasinormal mode frequencies with high precision for scalar perturbations of extremal Reissner--Nordström and Kerr black holes. This demonstrates the effectiveness of the exact WKB method combined with Borel--Padé resummation in solving the spectral problem of black hole perturbations.

重求和后的量子化条件成功地以高精度重现了极端Reissner--Nordström和Kerr黑洞标量微扰的准正模频率。这证明了结合Borel--Padé重求和方法的精确WKB方法在解决黑洞微扰的谱问题方面的有效性。

Conclusion: The paper shows that the exact WKB method, combined with Borel--Padé resummation, is a powerful and accurate tool for determining the quasinormal mode frequencies of black holes. This method can be applied to a wide range of black hole perturbation problems, providing a systematic and precise approach to studying the dynamics and stability of black holes.

该论文表明，结合Borel--Padé重求和方法的精确WKB方法是确定黑洞准正模频率的强大且准确的工具。这种方法可以应用于广泛的黑洞微扰问题，为研究黑洞的动力学和稳定性提供了一种系统而精确的方法。

Abstract: We apply exact WKB analysis to the spectral problem arising in black hole perturbation theory. The boundary conditions for quasinormal modes lead to exact quantization conditions for the complex frequencies. To solve these conditions, one needs to evaluate the so-called quantum periods, or Voros symbols. For scalar perturbations of extremal Reissner--Nordström and Kerr black holes, we compute these quantities up to very high orders in the WKB expansion and perform Borel--Padé resummation. The resulting resummed quantization conditions successfully reproduce the correct quasinormal mode frequencies with high precision.

</details>


### [42] [Hidden gauge invariance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01453)
*Karl-Henning Rehren*
