TL;DR: The paper reconsiders the role of gauge invariance by deriving it from quantum principles without assuming it. It shows that most interactions fulfilling these constraints have a hidden, exact, and unbroken gauge invariance, even with massive vector bosons. This is achieved using string-localized interactions, which ensure S-matrices are string-independent and consistent with local interactions in gauge theory, thus eliminating the need for indefinite state spaces or ghosts.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand gauge invariance in an autonomous way, derived from quantum principles rather than assumed. The aim is to show that gauge invariance can emerge naturally from the constraints imposed by the representation on a Hilbert space, leading to a deeper understanding of particle physics without the need for additional constructs like indefinite state spaces or ghosts.

Method: The method involves an autonomous approach to interactions of Standard Model particles, where renormalizable interactions are constrained by quantum principles, specifically the representation on a Hilbert space. The key technique is the use of string-localized interactions, which secure that S-matrices are independent of the string and coincide with those from gauge theories on indefinite state spaces. This approach reveals a hidden, exact, and unbroken gauge invariance in the interactions, even when massive vector bosons are present.

Result: The result is the discovery of a hidden, exact, and unbroken gauge invariance in most interactions that fulfill the quantum principle constraints. This gauge invariance is shown to be present even in the presence of massive vector bosons. Furthermore, the S-matrices derived from string-localized interactions are found to be string-independent and consistent with those from gauge theories on indefinite state spaces, but without the need for such spaces or ghosts.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that particle physics, including the interactions of massless and massive vector bosons, can be understood through an autonomous approach based on quantum principles, leading to the emergence of gauge invariance. This approach eliminates the need for indefinite state spaces and ghosts, providing a more fundamental and coherent framework for the Standard Model.

Abstract: The role of gauge invariance is reconsidered by "deriving it without assuming it" within an autonomous approach to interactions of Standard Model particles. In this approach, the renormalizable interactions are purely constrained by quantum principles, notably the representation on a Hilbert space. It is shown that - surprisingly - most interactions fulfilling the constraints enjoy a "hidden" gauge invariance (uncovered via redefinitions of quantum fields). The hidden gauge invariance is exact and unbroken even in the presence of massive vector bosons. While the Hilbert space formulation requires the use of "string-localized interactions", its role is to secure that S-matrices are string-independent, and in fact coincide with S-matrices with local interactions from the gauge theory approach on indefinite state spaces. Thus, particle physics with massless and massive vector bosons can be understood without neither indefinite state spaces nor ghosts.

### [43] [Reductions in Khovanov-Rozansky operator formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01584)
*D. Galakhov,E. Lanina,A. Morozov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper reformulates the Khovanov-Rozansky (KhR) description of knot invariants using a bicomplex with simple operators $D$ and conjugations $\chi^{(\pm)}$. The process is split into two steps: defining 'vertical' cohomologies and 'horizontal' cohomologies, which are combined to form the KhR polynomial. This construction is global but built from local components, allowing for local reductions and simplifications, especially in bipartite cases.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation behind this work is to provide a more intuitive and physically meaningful formulation of the Khovanov-Rozansky (KhR) description of knot invariants. By substituting the counterintuitive matrix factorization with simpler, locally defined operators and conjugations, the authors aim to make the KhR procedure more accessible and easier to handle, particularly for complex link diagrams. 

这项工作的动机是提供一种更直观且具有物理意义的Khovanov-Rozansky (KhR) 描述结不变量的方法。通过用更简单、局部定义的算子和共轭取代反直觉的矩阵因子化，作者旨在使KhR过程更容易理解和处理，特别是对于复杂的链图。

Method: The method involves constructing a bicomplex where the operators $D$ are defined for every MOY resolution of a link diagram, and these operators become nilpotent when the diagram has no external lines. Conjugations $\chi^{(\pm)}$ relate operators for different resolutions. The KhR procedure is then divided into two steps: first, defining 'vertical' cohomologies associated with particular resolutions, and second, defining 'horizontal' cohomologies by combining standard nilpotent morphisms. The resulting cohomologies depend on the entire link diagram, but the building blocks are local, allowing for local reductions and simplifications.

该方法包括构建一个双复形，在每个MOY分解的链图上定义算子$D$，当图没有外部线时，这些算子成为幂零的。共轭$\chi^{(\pm)}$关联了不同分解的算子。然后，KhR过程被分为两个步骤：首先，定义与特定分解相关的“垂直”上同调；其次，通过组合标准幂零态射来定义“水平”上同调。结果的上同调依赖于整个链图，但其构建块是局部的，允许进行局部简化和简化。

Result: The result is a new, more intuitive, and physically meaningful formulation of the Khovanov-Rozansky (KhR) description of knot invariants. The use of simple operators $D$ and conjugations $\chi^{(\pm)}$ allows for a clearer understanding of the KhR procedure, and the local nature of the building blocks enables local reductions and simplifications. In particular, the bipartite calculus is simplified, and in the $N=2$ and arbitrary $N$ bipartite cases, global reductions can be applied to transfer the local construction of the KhR double-complex to the global construction of the Khovanov-like single-complex.

结果是一种新的、更直观且具有物理意义的Khovanov-Rozansky (KhR) 描述结不变量的方法。使用简单的算子$D$和共轭$\chi^{(\pm)}$使得KhR过程更容易理解，而构建块的局部性质允许进行局部简化和简化。特别是在二分法的情况下，计算得到了简化，并且在$N=2$和任意$N$的二分情况下，可以应用全局简化，将KhR双复形的局部构造转换为类似Khovanov单复形的全局构造。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the reformulation of the Khovanov-Rozansky (KhR) description of knot invariants in terms of a bicomplex with simple operators and conjugations provides a more intuitive and physically meaningful framework. This new approach not only simplifies the understanding of the KhR procedure but also allows for local reductions and simplifications, making it a valuable tool for studying complex link diagrams, especially in bipartite cases.

论文得出结论，通过使用简单算子和共轭的双复形来重新表述Khovanov-Rozansky (KhR) 描述结不变量的方法，提供了一个更直观且具有物理意义的框架。这种新方法不仅简化了对KhR过程的理解，还允许进行局部简化和简化，使其成为研究复杂链图（尤其是在二分情况）的有价值的工具。

Abstract: Sophisticated Khovanov-Rozansky (KhR) description of knot invariants in the fundamental representation can be reformulated in terms of bicomplex with a simple physical meaning. Namely, the counterintuitive matrix factorization is substituted by simple operators $D$, locally constructed for every MOY resolution of a link diagram, which becomes nilpotent when the diagram has no external lines. Operators for different resolutions are related by equally simple conjugations $χ^{(\pm)}$. The KhR procedure then splits in two steps - defining ``vertical'' cohomologies of $D$, which are associated with particular resolutions and will be put at vertices of the hypercube, and conjugations $χ^{(\pm)}$, that define morphisms along its edges. As usual, standard combinations of morphisms are nilpotent, and one can define ``horizontal'' cohomologies - which are then combined into Poincaré polynomial, called KhR polynomial in application to links. This construction remains global in the sense that resulting cohomologies depend on the entire link diagram, but all its building blocks, including the operators and morphisms are local in the sense that they are defined for its particular vertices. Sometimes, this allows simple local reductions, allowing to eliminate or change particular vertices or sets of those. Along with the obvious case of Reidemeister equivalencies this happens also for antiparallel-lock tangles, what is responsible for simplification of bipartite calculus. In the $N=2$ and arbitrary $N$ bipartite cases, one can also provide global reductions transferring the local construction of the KhR double-complex to the global construction of the Khovanov(-like) single-complex.

</details>

Result: The main result is the explicit computation of the one-loop quantum corrections to the superfield effective potential for the higher-derivative Maxwell-Chern-Simons theories. The effective potential is obtained in closed form and is expressed in terms of the roots of the polynomial functions, which allows for a detailed analysis of the quantum corrections.

主要结果是显式地计算了高阶导数Maxwell-Chern-Simons理论中超场有效势的一圈量子修正。有效势以闭合形式获得，并用多项式函数的根来表示，这允许对量子修正进行详细分析。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the one-loop quantum corrections to the superfield effective potential for the higher-derivative Maxwell-Chern-Simons theories can be computed explicitly and are expressed in terms of the roots of polynomial functions. This provides a new perspective on the quantum behavior of these theories and their renormalization properties.

论文得出结论，高阶导数Maxwell-Chern-Simons理论中超场有效势的一圈量子修正可以显式计算，并且用多项式函数的根来表示。这为这些理论的量子行为及其重整化性质提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We define a higher-derivative generalization of Maxwell-Chern-Simons theory in $\mathcal{N}=1$ and $\mathcal{N}=2$ superspaces. In particular, the chosen higher-derivative operator is a polynomial function of the d'Alembertian of arbitrary degree, and it is introduced exclusively in the gauge sector. The main goal is to explicitly compute the one-loop quantum corrections to the superfield effective potential for these theories. This is carried out by means of background field quantization in a higher-derivative $R_ξ$ gauge. ### [45] [A Non-local "Boundary'' Term for Two-Point Amplitudes in String Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01784)

TL;DR: A new boundary term in free bosonic string field theory is proposed, which restores cyclicity broken by the insertion of a step-function operator. The term is constructed as a bilinear form involving the commutator of the BRST operator with the step-function operator. It ensures a well-defined variational principle and reproduces the correct tree-level two-point amplitudes for both open and closed strings, verified in the tachyon and massless sectors.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

This is important for maintaining a consistent and well-defined variational principle in the theory, especially when dealing with on-shell string fields.

Method: The method involves constructing a new boundary term as a bilinear form. This term includes the commutator of the BRST operator with the step-function operator. The construction aims to ensure that the resulting action has a well-defined variational principle and correctly reproduces the tree-level two-point amplitudes for both open and closed strings.

Result: The result is a new boundary term in the free bosonic string field theory that successfully restores the cyclicity and maintains a well-defined variational principle. When evaluated on on-shell string fields, this term reproduces the correct tree-level two-point amplitudes for both open and closed strings, as explicitly verified in the tachyon and massless sectors.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the proposed boundary term effectively restores the cyclicity in the free bosonic string field theory and ensures a well-defined variational principle. It correctly reproduces the tree-level two-point amplitudes for both open and closed strings, thereby providing a consistent framework for further theoretical developments.

Abstract: We propose a new ``boundary'' term in free bosonic string field theory. Here, the term ``boundary'' refers to a contribution introduced to restore the cyclicity broken by the insertion of a stringy step-function operator, although it is not strictly localized as it involves an operator that selects positive-energy modes. We construct this term as a bilinear form involving the commutator of the BRST operator with the step-function operator. The resulting action has a well-defined variational principle. When evaluated on on-shell string fields, the proposed term reproduces the correct tree-level two-point amplitude for both open and closed strings. We verify this explicitly in the tachyon and massless sectors.

### [46] [Confinement of Massive Ghost in Quadratic Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01966)
*Ichiro Oda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper discusses the confinement of a massive ghost in quadratic gravity, using the BRST quartet mechanism to restore unitarity. The asymptotic field of the massive ghost is identified as a massive dipole, while the bound state obeys a massive Klein-Gordon equation, drawing a parallel to color confinement in QCD.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In the covariant canonical formalism of quadratic gravity, the presence of a massive ghost poses a problem by violating the unitarity of the physical S-matrix. The motivation is to address this issue and propose a mechanism for confining the massive ghost, thereby restoring unitarity.

在协变正则形式的二次引力框架中，存在一个具有质量的鬼场破坏了物理S-矩阵的幺正性。动机是解决这个问题，并提出一种机制来约束具有质量的鬼场，从而恢复幺正性。

Method: The method involves the use of the BRST quartet mechanism, which suggests that if there is a bound state between the massive ghost and the Faddeev-Popov ghost, the massive ghost can be confined in zero-norm states. This confinement restores the unitarity of the S-matrix. Additionally, the superfield formulation by Bonora and Tonin is used to show that the asymptotic field of the massive ghost must be a massive dipole, while the bound state follows a massive Klein-Gordon equation.

该方法使用BRST四元机制，该机制表明，如果具有质量的鬼场和Faddeev-Popov鬼场之间存在束缚态，则具有质量的鬼场可以被约束在零范数态中。这种约束恢复了S-矩阵的幺正性。此外，还使用了Bonora和Tonin的超场表述来表明，具有质量的鬼场的渐近场必须是一个具有质量的偶极子，而束缚态遵循具有质量的Klein-Gordon方程。

Result: The result shows that the massive ghost can indeed be confined through the BRST quartet mechanism, leading to the restoration of unitarity. The asymptotic field of the massive ghost is identified as a massive dipole, and the bound state is found to obey a massive Klein-Gordon equation. This situation draws a parallel to the conjecture in QCD where a massive gluon, rather than a massless one, is confined.

结果表明，通过BRST四元机制，确实可以约束具有质量的鬼场，从而恢复幺正性。具有质量的鬼场的渐近场被确定为具有质量的偶极子，而束缚态被发现遵循具有质量的Klein-Gordon方程。这种情况与QCD中的猜想相似，即被约束的是具有质量的胶子，而不是无质量的胶子。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the confinement of the massive ghost through the BRST quartet mechanism effectively restores the unitarity of the S-matrix in the context of quadratic gravity. The identification of the massive ghost's asymptotic field as a massive dipole and the bound state's behavior as governed by a massive Klein-Gordon equation provide a novel perspective on the nature of confinement, potentially analogous to the confinement of massive gluons in QCD.

结论是，通过BRST四元机制约束具有质量的鬼场有效地恢复了二次引力背景下S-矩阵的幺正性。将具有质量的鬼场的渐近场识别为具有质量的偶极子，以及束缚态的行为受具有质量的Klein-Gordon方程支配，为约束的本质提供了新的视角，可能类似于QCD中具有质量的胶子的约束。

Abstract: In the framework of the covariant canonical formalism of quadratic gravity, we consider the problem of confinement of massive ghost which violates the unitarity of the physical S-matrix. It is shown that if there is a bound state between the massive ghost and Faddeev-Popov ghost the massive ghost is confined in the zero-norm states through the BRST quartet mechanism, thereby the unitarity being restored. Based on the superfield formulation by Bonora and Tonin, we show that the asymptotic field of the massive ghost must be a massive dipole whereas that of the bound state obeys a massive Klein-Gordon equation. This situation may be of some similarity to color confinement in quantum chromodynamics (QCD) where it is conjectured that not a massless but a massive gluon is in fact confined.

### [47] [All DDF/lightcone two-particle decay widths up to level $8$ in open bosonic string in critical dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02013)
*Samuele Critelli,Igor Pesando*

TL;DR: The paper performs an extensive analysis of Abelian two-particle decay channels for open bosonic string states up to level 8, excluding tachyons. It identifies the most stable states and dominant decay channels, with a focus on the role of photons and the influence of tachyonic decays in the lightcone computation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop intuition about the stability of open bosonic string states and to identify the dominant decay channels by explicitly computing all possible Abelian two-particle decay channels (excluding the tachyon) up to level 8. The aim is to understand which states are the most stable and to characterize the typical decay patterns, especially the role of photons and tachyons in these decays.

动机是通过显式计算所有可能的阿贝尔两粒子衰变通道（不包括快子）直到第8级，来发展对开弦玻色态稳定性的直觉，并确定主要的衰变通道。目的是理解哪些状态是最稳定的，并表征这些衰变的典型模式，特别是光子和快子在这些衰变中的作用。

Method: The method involves an experimental analysis where all possible Abelian two-particle decay channels (excluding the tachyon) of open bosonic massive states up to level 8 are computed. This amounts to approximately 2,000,000 cases. The authors also compare the lightcone and equal-time computations, noting the effects of ``surges'' due to decays into a tachyon and a higher-mass state.

该方法涉及一种实验分析，其中计算了直到第8级的所有可能的阿贝尔两粒子衰变通道（不包括快子）的开弦玻色质量态。这大约涉及到2,000,000个案例。作者还比较了光锥和等时计算，注意到了由于衰变成快子和高质态而引起的“激增”效应。

Result: The results show that the ratio of decay widths between the slowest- and fastest-decaying states is of order one. The dominant polarized decay channel, which typically involves at least one photon, accounts for at least $10\%$ of the total decay width, while the first five channels together contribute roughly 60%. Even when summing about 10,000 polarized channels, the dominant channels always involve at least one photon. The most stable states are those made using the DDF/lightcone oscillators $A_{-1}$ and some $A_{-2}$, which are close relatives of the states on the leading Regge trajectory. Additionally, it is hypothesized that decays into tachyons may constitute the dominant decay channels in bosonic string theory.

结果显示，最慢和最快衰减状态之间的衰变宽度比值为数量级一。主要的极化衰变通道，通常至少涉及一个光子，占总衰变宽度的至少$10\%$，而前五个通道合计贡献约60%。即使在总计约10,000个极化通道时，主要通道也总是至少涉及一个光子。最稳定的状态是使用DDF/光锥振荡器$A_{-1}$和一些$A_{-2}$构建的状态，这些状态与主导Regge轨迹上的状态密切相关。此外，假设在玻色弦理论中，衰变成快子可能是主要的衰变通道。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the most stable open bosonic string states are those constructed using the DDF/lightcone oscillators $A_{-1}$ and some $A_{-2}$. The dominant decay channels almost always involve at least one photon, and the hypothesis is put forward that, in bosonic string theory, decays into tachyons may be the dominant decay channels. The lightcone computation differs from the equal-time computation due to surges, i.e., decays into a tachyon and a higher-mass state.

研究得出结论，最稳定的开弦玻色态是使用DDF/光锥振荡器$A_{-1}$和一些$A_{-2}$构建的状态。主要的衰变通道几乎总是至少涉及一个光子，并且提出了一个假设，在玻色弦理论中，衰变成快子可能是主要的衰变通道。由于“激增”，即衰变成快子和高质态，光锥计算与等时计算不同。

Abstract: We carry out an ``experimental analysis'' in which we explicitly compute all possible Abelian two-particle decay channels (excluding the tachyon) of open bosonic massive states up to level (8), amounting to approximately 2,000,000 cases. The aim is to develop intuition about which states are the most stable and to identify the dominant decay channels. Our results show that, for all levels considered, the ratio of decay widths between the slowest- and fastest-decaying states is of order one. In most cases, the dominant polarized decay channel accounts for at least $10\%$ of the total decay width, while the first five channels together contribute roughly 60%. Even when we sum about $10000$ polarized channels. Dominant polarized channels always involve at least one photon and all strings ultimately decay into a photon carrying energy at the string scale. The most stable states are made using the DDF/lightcone oscillators $A_{-1}$ and some $A_{-2}$ and are close relatives of the states on the leading Regge trajectory. Finally, we discuss how the computation on the lightcone differs from the equal-time computation due to ``surges'', i.e., decays into a tachyon and a higher-mass state, and we hypothesize that, in bosonic string theory, decays into tachyons constitute the dominant decay channels.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a comprehensive understanding of the planar Makeenko--Migdal loop equations in the continuum limit, to determine the quantum fluctuation determinant, and to explore the implications for the mass spectrum and transition amplitudes of open- and closed-string sectors in Yang--Mills theory.

动机是全面理解连续极限下的平面Makeenko--Migdal环方程，确定量子涨落行列式，并探索其对Yang--Mills理论中开弦和闭弦部分的质量谱和跃迁幅度的影响。

Method: The method involves using the confining twistor-string representation to compute the quantum fluctuation determinant, reducing it to a discrete product of finite-dimensional matrix quadratures in Minkowski space. The path integral localizes on the classical trajectory, and the holonomy shift dictates exact geometric degeneracies. For the pure Yang--Mills closed string, the conformal Liouville anomaly drives the string to a trigonometric minimum, and the zero-mode measure nullifies the transition amplitude of the massless scalar ghost.

方法包括使用约束twistor-string表示来计算量子涨落行列式，在Minkowski空间中将其简化为有限维矩阵求积的离散乘积。路径积分集中在经典轨迹上，而holonomy移位决定了精确的几何简并。对于纯Yang--Mills闭弦，共形Liouville异常驱动弦到三角最小值，零模测度使无质量标量鬼的跃迁幅度消失。

Result: The results show that the $ζ$-regularized weight is independent of winding number $w$, and near the mass shell, the pole singularity is generated by $w \to \infty$. The path integral localizes on the classical trajectory, and the pole spectrum and transition residues are parametrically exact in the large-$w$ WKB limit. The holonomy shift dictates exact geometric degeneracies between parity families, and the conformal Liouville anomaly drives the pure-gauge minimal surface to the trigonometric minimum, yielding linear Regge trajectories. The mass gap for purely gluonic states is explicitly demonstrated, and the Lüscher intercept is recovered.

结果表明，$ζ$-正则化权重与缠绕数$w$无关，而在质量壳附近，极点奇异性由$w \to \infty$生成。路径积分集中在经典轨迹上，在大$w$ WKB极限下，极点谱和跃迁残差在参数上是精确的。Holonomy移位决定了宇称家族之间的精确几何简并，共形Liouville异常将纯规范极小曲面驱动到三角最小值，产生线性Regge轨迹。明确展示了纯胶子态的质量间隙，并恢复了Lüscher截距。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the analysis provides a detailed understanding of the planar Makeenko--Migdal loop equations and their implications for the mass spectrum and transition amplitudes in Yang--Mills theory. The results demonstrate the dynamical stability of the pure-gauge minimal surface and provide a mechanism for a purely gluonic mass gap, with the Lüscher intercept being recovered as a macroscopic spectrum baseline for unassigned isoscalar candidates.

结论是该分析提供了对平面Makeenko--Migdal环方程及其对Yang--Mills理论中质量谱和跃迁幅度影响的详细理解。结果表明纯规范极小曲面的动力学稳定性，并提供了一种纯胶子质量间隙的机制，Lüscher截距被恢复为未分配的同标量候选物的宏观谱基线。

Abstract: We complete the analysis of planar Makeenko--Migdal loop equations in the continuum limit. Using the confining twistor-string representation, we compute the quantum fluctuation determinant. In Minkowski space, this reduces to a discrete product of finite-dimensional matrix quadratures. The $ζ$-regularized weight is independent of winding number $w$. Near the mass shell, the pole singularity is generated by $w \to \infty$, suppressing fluctuation variance as $1/w$. The path integral localizes on the classical trajectory, rendering the pole spectrum and transition residues parametrically exact in the large-$w$ WKB limit.For the open-string meson sector, we fit 40 states across five topological sectors ($h=0, \pm 1, \pm 2$). The holonomy shift $h$ dictates exact geometric degeneracies between parity families, reproducing mass splittings without phenomenological spin-orbit parameters. Evaluated one-loop residues yield relative transition cross-sections, demonstrating nontrivial topology- and flavor-dependent scaling that captures heavy-mass quenching and phase-space enhancement for high-spin light states.For the pure Yang--Mills closed string, we demonstrate dynamical stability of the pure-gauge minimal surface in the planar limit: the conformal Liouville anomaly drives the string strictly to the trigonometric minimum ($q=0$). The complex elliptic geometry analytically collapses, yielding linear Regge trajectories. The translation zero-mode measure dynamically nullifies the transition amplitude of the massless scalar ghost, providing an explicit analytic mechanism for a purely gluonic mass gap. Anchoring parameter-free glueball trajectories to the string tension natively recovers the L"uscher intercept $α(0)=1/12$, yielding a macroscopic spectrum that provides a suggestive baseline for established PDG unassigned isoscalar candidates.

### [49] [Functional Renormalization Group for a Rank-4 Renormalizable Tensorial Group Field Theory with Derivative Necklace Couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02422)
*Seke Fawaaz Zime Yerima,Vincent Lahoche,Dine Ousmane Samary*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper applies the functional renormalization group to an Abelian Group Field Theory, including subdominant but derivative-enhanced interactions. It identifies a nontrivial ultraviolet fixed point in a rank-4 model with necklace-structured non-melonic interactions, similar to large-N random matrix models. The fixed point's robustness is further investigated using modified Ward identities.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to explore the application of the functional renormalization group (FRG) to an extended Abelian Group Field Theory (AGFT). This extension includes interactions that, while subdominant from a power-counting perspective, are enhanced by derivative couplings. The aim is to understand the behavior of such theories beyond the well-studied branched-polymer (melonic) sector and to identify new nontrivial ultraviolet (UV) fixed points.

本文的动机是探索泛函重整化群（FRG）在扩展的阿贝尔群场论（AGFT）中的应用。这种扩展包括虽然从幂次计数的角度来看是次主导的，但通过导数耦合增强的相互作用。目的是理解这些理论在已研究得很好的分支聚合物（melon）部门之外的行为，并识别新的非平凡紫外（UV）固定点。

Method: The method employed in this paper involves the use of the functional renormalization group (FRG) applied to a rank-4 Abelian Group Field Theory (AGFT) model. The model is extended to include non-melonic interactions with a necklace structure, which, due to their index contraction pattern, exhibit leading-order behavior analogous to large-N random matrix models. The analysis focuses on identifying the emergence of a nontrivial ultraviolet (UV) fixed point and its reliability within the current truncation. Additionally, the robustness of this fixed point is further investigated through the use of modified Ward identities.

本文采用的方法是将泛函重整化群（FRG）应用于一个四阶阿贝尔群场论（AGFT）模型。该模型被扩展以包括具有项链结构的非melon相互作用，由于它们的指标收缩模式，表现出类似于大N随机矩阵模型的领先阶行为。分析的重点在于识别非平凡紫外（UV）固定点的出现及其在当前截断下的可靠性。此外，通过使用修改后的Ward恒等式进一步调查了这个固定点的鲁棒性。

Result: The result of this study is the identification of a nontrivial ultraviolet (UV) fixed point in the extended AGFT model. This fixed point is reminiscent of mechanisms previously observed in large-N random matrix models, suggesting a deeper connection between the two frameworks. The analysis also suggests that the UV fixed point is reliable within the present truncation scheme, and the robustness of this fixed point is further supported by the examination using modified Ward identities.

本研究的结果是在扩展的AGFT模型中识别出一个非平凡的紫外（UV）固定点。这个固定点让人想起在大N随机矩阵模型中先前观察到的机制，这表明两者框架之间存在更深层次的联系。分析还表明，UV固定点在当前的截断方案下是可靠的，并且通过使用修改后的Ward恒等式的检查进一步支持了这一固定点的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: The conclusion drawn from this work is that the inclusion of non-melonic, derivative-enhanced interactions in an Abelian Group Field Theory can lead to the emergence of a nontrivial ultraviolet fixed point. This finding, along with the robustness of the fixed point as examined through modified Ward identities, opens up new avenues for understanding the ultraviolet behavior of such field theories beyond the melonic sector. It also highlights the potential for discovering new universality classes in the context of Group Field Theories.

从这项工作中得出的结论是，在阿贝尔群场论中包含非melon、导数增强的相互作用可以导致非平凡紫外固定点的出现。这一发现，以及通过修改后的Ward恒等式检查到的固定点的鲁棒性，为理解此类场论在melon部门之外的紫外行为开辟了新途径。它还突出了在群场论背景下发现新的普适类的可能性。

Abstract: We apply the functional renormalization group to an Abelian Group Field Theory extended beyond the branched-polymer (melonic) sector by including interactions that are subdominant from a power-counting perspective but enhanced by derivative couplings. Focusing on a rank-4 model, we consider a class of non-melonic interactions with a necklace structure. Due to their index contraction pattern, their leading-order behavior is analogous to that of large-N random matrix models and is associated with a planar graph structure. Within this setting, we identify the emergence of a nontrivial ultraviolet fixed point, reminiscent of mechanisms previously observed in matrix models, and discuss its reliability within the present truncation. The robustness of this fixed point will be further investigated through modified Ward identities, following strategies previously developed in the melonic sector.

### [50] [Quantum scars from holographic boson stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02446)
*Yan Liu,Ya-Wen Sun,Yuan-Tai Wang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates that asymptotically AdS mini-boson stars can serve as a holographic realization of quantum many-body scars, which are nonthermal states embedded in a chaotic spectrum. These boson stars exhibit random-matrix signatures of chaos while supporting integrable spectral branches, and show lower entanglement and robust revivals in Krylov complexity compared to black holes, indicating nonergodic dynamics.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this work is to explore the connection between quantum many-body scars, quantum chaos, and horizonless gravitational dynamics within a self-gravitating system. The authors aim to provide a holographic realization of scar-like states and to understand how these states can coexist with chaotic behavior in the same spectrum, while also exhibiting nonergodic dynamics and low entanglement.

这项工作的动机是探索在一个自引力系统中量子多体疤痕、量子混沌和无视界引力动力学之间的联系。作者旨在提供一个类似疤痕状态的全息实现，并理解这些状态如何与同一谱中的混沌行为共存，同时表现出非遍历动力学和低纠缠。

Method: The authors use holographic duality to study the properties of asymptotically AdS mini-boson stars, which are considered as a realization of scar-like states. They analyze the spectrum of these boson stars, comparing it with the chaotic spectrum of black holes, and investigate the entanglement entropy and Krylov complexity to identify the nonergodic dynamics and low entanglement characteristics of the boson stars.

作者使用全息对偶来研究渐近AdS小型玻色星的性质，将其视为类似疤痕状态的一种实现。他们分析了这些玻色星的谱，将其与黑洞的混沌谱进行比较，并研究了纠缠熵和Krylov复杂性，以识别玻色星的非遍历动力学和低纠缠特性。

Result: The results show that asymptotically AdS mini-boson stars exhibit random-matrix signatures of chaos, but also support embedded integrable spectral branches, indicating the presence of scar-like states. Additionally, the boson stars have anomalously low entanglement and display robust revivals in Krylov complexity, distinguishing them from typical black hole states.

结果表明，渐近AdS小型玻色星表现出混沌的随机矩阵特征，但也支持嵌入的可积谱分支，表明存在类似疤痕的状态。此外，玻色星具有异常低的纠缠，并在Krylov复杂性中显示出稳健的恢复，这将它们与典型的黑洞状态区分开来。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that asymptotically AdS mini-boson stars provide a holographic realization of quantum many-body scars, which are nonthermal states embedded in a chaotic spectrum. These states exhibit nonergodic dynamics, low entanglement, and robust revivals, providing evidence for the existence of holographic quantum scars in a self-gravitating system. This work suggests a new connection between many-body scar physics, quantum chaos, and horizonless gravitational dynamics.

论文得出结论，渐近AdS小型玻色星提供了量子多体疤痕的全息实现，这是嵌入混沌谱中的非热态。这些状态表现出非遍历动力学、低纠缠和稳健的恢复，为自引力系统中全息量子疤痕的存在提供了证据。这项工作提出了多体疤痕物理、量子混沌和无视界引力动力学之间的一个新联系。

Abstract: Quantum many-body scars are atypical nonthermal states embedded in the chaotic spectrum that evade conventional ergodicity. We show that asymptotically AdS mini-boson stars provide a holographic realization of scar-like states. Their spectrum exhibits random-matrix signatures of chaos while supporting embedded integrable spectral branches. The full holographic system, including black holes, is generically chaotic with most eigenstates satisfying the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis; in contrast, the boson star macrostate probes an approximately integrable subsector within this chaotic spectrum, signaling scarred spectral structures. Boson stars further display anomalously low entanglement relative to black holes at the same energy density, and also robust revivals in Krylov complexity, revealing nonergodic dynamics. These spectral, entanglement, and dynamical diagnostics provide unified evidence for holographic quantum scars in a self-gravitating system. Our work suggests a new connection between many-body scar physics, quantum chaos, and horizonless gravitational dynamics.

### [51] [Kerr-de Sitter Black Holes: Quantum Aspects and Cosmic Censorship Conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02523)
*Ankit Anand,Ankur Dey*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper tests the weak cosmic censorship conjecture (wCCC) in a quantum Kerr-de Sitter (qKdS) black hole, including exact backreaction from quantum matter fields. The results show that the black hole remains stable against horizon-destroying processes, and quantum corrections strengthen the horizon's robustness, supporting the preservation of wCCC in the presence of quantum effects.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this paper is to explore the validity of the weak cosmic censorship conjecture (wCCC) in the context of a quantum Kerr-de Sitter (qKdS) black hole, where the backreaction from quantum matter fields is taken into account. The aim is to determine whether an extremal qKdS black hole can be over-extremized to expose a naked singularity, and to understand the role of quantum corrections in the stability of the black hole's horizon.

本文的动机是探索在考虑量子物质场反作用的情况下，弱宇宙审查猜想 (wCCC) 在量子Kerr-de Sitter (qKdS) 黑洞背景下的有效性。目的是确定一个极端的qKdS黑洞是否可以通过过度极化暴露出裸奇点，并理解量子修正对黑洞视界稳定性的作用。

Method: The method used in this paper involves a test particle approach to analyze the stability of the horizon of an extremal qKdS black hole. The authors incorporate exact backreaction from quantum matter fields to study how infalling matter affects the black hole's horizon. By considering the dynamics of the test particles, they assess the potential for the black hole to be over-extremized and the impact of quantum corrections on the horizon's robustness.

本文采用试探粒子方法来分析极端qKdS黑洞视界的稳定性。作者结合了来自量子物质场的精确反作用，研究入射物质如何影响黑洞的视界。通过考虑试探粒子的动力学，他们评估了黑洞被过度极化的可能性以及量子修正对视界鲁棒性的影响。

Result: The results of the analysis indicate that the black hole remains stable against horizon-destroying processes induced by infalling matter. Quantum corrections are found to enhance the robustness of the horizon rather than destabilize it. This finding supports the preservation of the weak cosmic censorship conjecture (wCCC) in the presence of quantum effects.

分析结果表明，黑洞在入射物质引起的视界破坏过程中保持稳定。量子修正被发现增强了视界的鲁棒性，而不是使其不稳定。这一发现支持了在量子效应存在下弱宇宙审查猜想 (wCCC) 的保持。

Conclusion: The conclusion drawn from this work is that the weak cosmic censorship conjecture (wCCC) remains valid in the background of a quantum Kerr-de Sitter (qKdS) black hole, even when exact backreaction from quantum matter fields is considered. The enhanced robustness of the horizon due to quantum corrections suggests that the conjecture is preserved in the presence of quantum effects, providing further evidence for the stability of black hole horizons in a quantum context.

从这项工作中得出的结论是，即使考虑到来自量子物质场的精确反作用，弱宇宙审查猜想 (wCCC) 在量子Kerr-de Sitter (qKdS) 黑洞背景下仍然有效。由于量子修正增强的视界鲁棒性表明，在量子效应存在下该猜想得以保持，为量子背景下黑洞视界的稳定性提供了进一步的证据。

Abstract: In this article, we test the validity of the weak cosmic censorship conjecture (wCCC) in the background of a quantum Kerr-de Sitter (qKdS) black hole, incorporating exact backreaction from quantum matter fields. Using a test particle approach, we analyze whether an extremal qKdS black hole can be over-extremized to expose a naked singularity. Our results indicate that the black hole remains stable against horizon-destroying processes induced by infalling matter. Quantum corrections enhance the horizon's robustness rather than destabilize it, offering further evidence that wCCC remains preserved in the presence of quantum effects.

### [53] [Albertian Channel Memory in Black-Hole Evaporation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02792)
*Rafael B. Frigori*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores the AMPS paradox using an octonionic magical supergravity framework, leading to a description where the emitted radiation carries exceptional memory, rather than a restored tensor factorization. This is achieved through an Albertian algebraic-quantum description and Peirce theory, which divides horizon data into distinct components. The analysis in real and Euclidean time reveals a spectral-overlap coherence and a transfer kernel with specific statistical limits, ultimately reconstructing the Page-curve envelope.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of the paper is to address the AMPS paradox by employing a novel theoretical framework based on octonionic magical supergravity. The goal is to provide an alternative perspective on the nature of the information carried by the emitted radiation from a black hole, specifically focusing on the concept of exceptional memory as opposed to the traditional tensor-product structure assumed in the AMPS paradox.

本文的动机是通过采用基于八元数魔幻超引力的新理论框架来解决AMPS悖论。目标是提供关于黑洞发射辐射所携带信息性质的另一种视角，特别关注异常记忆的概念，而不是AMPS悖论中假设的传统张量积结构。

Method: The method involves studying a retained attractor sector of octonionic magical supergravity, where the horizon symbols form the Albert algebra J3(O). This leads to an Albertian algebraic-quantum description, wherein states are represented as positive normalized functionals, events as Jordan idempotents, and reversible motions as algebra automorphisms. The application of Peirce theory further decomposes the horizon data into a hidden exceptional complement, an interface relay, and a two-helicity exterior detector. By eliminating the relay, a Volterra memory law is derived for a neutral-source fixed-charge Reissner--Nordstrom evaporation trajectory. In both real and Euclidean time, the behavior of the system is analyzed, revealing specific statistical properties and coherence patterns.

该方法涉及研究八元数魔幻超引力的一个保留吸引子部分，其中视界符号形成Albert代数J3(O)。这导致了一个Albertian代数量子描述，其中状态表示为正归一化泛函，事件表示为Jordan幂等元，可逆运动表示为代数自同构。应用Peirce理论进一步将视界数据分解为隐藏的异常补集、接口中继和双螺旋外检测器。通过消除中继，推导出一个针对中性源固定电荷Reissner--Nordstrom蒸发轨迹的Volterra记忆定律。在实时间和欧几里得时间中，分析了系统的性质，揭示了特定的统计特性和相干模式。

Result: The result shows that the emitted radiation carries exceptional memory, manifested as a spectral-overlap connected two-time coherence of windowed helicity/Stokes observables in the emitted history. In Euclidean time, the Peirce--Volterra kernel becomes a transfer kernel with two branchwise superstatistical limits, leading to a regular-opening Tsallis/Lomax onset and a near-extremal shifted-Levy residence branch. The reconstruction of the Page-curve envelope is achieved through the lower admissible envelope of the endpoint actions.

结果表明，发射的辐射携带着异常记忆，表现为发射历史中窗口化的螺旋度/斯托克斯可观测量的光谱重叠连接的两时相干性。在欧几里得时间中，Peirce-Volterra核成为一个具有两个分支超级统计极限的转移核，导致一个规则开启的Tsallis/Lomax起始点和一个近极值位移的Levy驻留分支。通过对端点作用的下可接受包络的重建，实现了Page曲线包络的重建。

Conclusion: The conclusion drawn from this study is that the emitted radiation from a black hole can be described as carrying exceptional memory, rather than conforming to the tensor-product structure assumed in the AMPS paradox. This finding provides a new perspective on the information content of the emitted radiation, suggesting that it retains a form of memory that is not captured by traditional quantum mechanical descriptions. The work thus contributes to the ongoing debate on black hole information and the nature of quantum gravity.

从这项研究得出的结论是，从黑洞发射的辐射可以被描述为携带异常记忆，而不是符合AMPS悖论中假设的张量积结构。这一发现为发射辐射的信息内容提供了新的视角，表明它保留了一种传统量子力学描述无法捕捉的记忆形式。因此，这项工作为正在进行的关于黑洞信息和量子引力性质的辩论做出了贡献。

Abstract: The AMPS paradox assumes a globally associative tensor-product stage for the early radiation, the exterior Hawking mode, and the interior partner. We study a retained attractor sector of octonionic magical supergravity whose horizon symbols form the Albert algebra J3(O). This induces an Albertian algebraic-quantum description: states are positive normalized functionals, events are Jordan idempotents, reversible motions are algebra automorphisms, and ordinary quantum mechanics is recovered on associative readout blocks. Peirce theory then splits the horizon data into a hidden exceptional complement, an interface relay, and a two-helicity exterior detector. Eliminating the relay gives a source-fixed Volterra memory law on a neutral-source fixed-charge Reissner--Nordstrom evaporation trajectory. In real time, the leading one-time occupation follows the sourced evaporation clock, while the retained-memory imprint appears as a spectral-overlap connected two-time coherence of windowed helicity/Stokes observables in the emitted history. In Euclidean time, the Peirce--Volterra kernel becomes a transfer kernel with two branchwise superstatistical limits: a regular-opening Tsallis/Lomax onset and a near-extremal shifted-Levy residence branch. The lower admissible envelope of the endpoint actions then reconstructs the Page-curve envelope. The result is an ordinary emitted readout with exceptional memory, not a restored AMPS tensor factorization.

</details>


### [54] [Landau levels via Jordan superalgebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02847)
*Alessio Marrani,Todor Popov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates that Jordan algebras and superalgebras offer a concise and elegant language for formulating quantum mechanical problems with (super)conformal symmetry, using the example of the quantum MICZ-Kepler model and its dual oscillator realization in ${\mathbb R}^2$.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide an alternative and more natural framework for reconstructing (super)conformal algebras in quantum mechanical systems, specifically in the context of the quantum MICZ-Kepler model and its dual oscillator realization. The authors aim to show that Jordan algebras and superalgebras can elegantly encapsulate the (super)conformal symmetries inherent in these systems.

动机是为量子力学系统中的(超)共形代数重构提供一个替代且更自然的框架，特别是在量子MICZ-Kepler模型及其对偶振子实现的背景下。作者旨在展示Jordan代数和超代数可以优雅地封装这些系统中固有的(超)共形对称性。

Method: The method involves the use of Kaplansky ${\mathfrak J} {\mathbb R}^{1|2}$ and Exceptional ${\mathfrak J} F^{6|4}$ Jordan superalgebras, which are applied through the Tits-Kantor-Koecher correspondence to reconstruct (super)conformal algebras hidden in the Landau levels of an electron in an external magnetic field. This approach leverages the mathematical structure of Jordan (super)algebras to uncover the underlying (super)conformal symmetries.

该方法涉及使用Kaplansky ${\mathfrak J} {\mathbb R}^{1|2}$ 和Exceptional ${\mathfrak J} F^{6|4}$ Jordan超代数，通过Tits-Kantor-Koecher对应关系来重构隐藏在外部磁场中电子的Landau能级中的(超)共形代数。这种方法利用了Jordan（超）代数的数学结构来揭示其潜在的(超)共形对称性。

Result: The result is that the (super)conformal symmetries of the quantum MICZ-Kepler model and its dual oscillator realization in ${\mathbb R}^2$ are effectively captured by the Jordan superalgebraic framework. This provides a new perspective on the (super)conformal structures in these systems, highlighting the role of Jordan (super)algebras in their formulation.

结果是量子MICZ-Kepler模型及其在${\mathbb R}^2$中的对偶振子实现的(超)共形对称性被Jordan超代数框架有效地捕捉到。这为这些系统中的(超)共形结构提供了新的视角，突出了Jordan（超）代数在其表述中的作用。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that Jordan algebras and superalgebras serve as a powerful and elegant tool for formulating and understanding (super)conformal symmetries in quantum mechanical systems. The use of specific Jordan superalgebras, such as Kaplansky ${\mathfrak J} {\mathbb R}^{1|2}$ and Exceptional ${\mathfrak J} F^{6|4}$, provides a natural and concise way to reconstruct (super)conformal algebras in the context of the quantum MICZ-Kepler model and its dual oscillator realization.

结论是Jordan代数和超代数作为强有力的工具，在表述和理解量子力学系统中的(超)共形对称性方面起到了优雅的作用。使用特定的Jordan超代数，如Kaplansky ${\mathfrak J} {\mathbb R}^{1|2}$ 和Exceptional ${\mathfrak J} F^{6|4}$，为在量子MICZ-Kepler模型及其对偶振子实现的背景下重构(超)共形代数提供了一种自然且简洁的方法。

Abstract: The goal of this note is to show that Jordan algebras and superalgebras provide an elegant and concise language for formulating quantum mechanical problems with inherent (super)conformal symmetry. The superconformal symmetries of the quantum MICZ-Kepler model and its dual oscillator realization in ${\mathbb R}^2$ are reviewed through the lens of the Tits-Kantor-Koecher correspondence:
  Kaplansky ${\mathfrak J} {\mathbb R}^{1|2}$ and Exceptional ${\mathfrak J} F^{6|4}$ Jordan superalgebras provide a natural framework for reconstructing (variously extended) superconformal algebras hidden in the Landau levels of an electron in an external magnetic field.

### [55] [Finite-temperature operator basis on $\mathbb{R}^3 \times S^1$ for SMEFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02878)
*Joydeep Chakrabortty,Bruno Siqueira Eduardo,Siddhartha Karmakar,Philipp Schicho*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper presents the first complete non-redundant operator basis for the SMEFT at finite temperature, using the imaginary-time formalism. The authors classify all effective operators up to dimension-six and impose various constraints, including integration-by-parts and equations-of-motion. They also identify intrinsically thermal operators that vanish at zero temperature.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this work is to construct a complete and non-redundant operator basis for the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) at finite temperature, which is essential for understanding the behavior of the Standard Model in high-temperature environments, such as those encountered in the early universe or in heavy-ion collisions. 

这项工作的动机是构建一个完整且无冗余的有限温度标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）算符基，这对于理解标准模型在高温环境下的行为至关重要，例如在早期宇宙或重离子碰撞中遇到的情况。

Method: The method used in this paper involves the application of the Hilbert series method on the space-time manifold $\mathbb{R}^3 \times S^1$ to classify all effective operators up to dimension-six. The authors consistently impose integration-by-parts (IBP) and equations-of-motion (EOM) constraints along spatial directions. Additionally, they analyze the impact of further constraints, such as the vanishing of the curl of the electric and magnetic fields and gauge choices for the temporal components. The operators are also expressed in terms of static three-dimensional spatial and zero-temperature SMEFT operators.

本文使用的方法是在时空流形$\mathbb{R}^3 \times S^1$上应用Hilbert级数方法，以分类所有达到六维的有效算符。作者一致地沿着空间方向施加了部分积分（IBP）和运动方程（EOM）约束。此外，他们还分析了进一步约束的影响，例如电场和磁场旋度的消失以及时间分量的规范选择。这些算符还用静态三维空间和零温SMEFT算符表示。

Result: The main result of this paper is the construction of the first complete non-redundant operator basis for the SMEFT at finite temperature. The authors have classified all effective operators up to dimension-six and identified intrinsically thermal operators that vanish at zero temperature. These results provide a comprehensive framework for studying the SMEFT in high-temperature environments.

本文的主要结果是构建了第一个完整的有限温度SMEFT非冗余算符基。作者已经分类了所有达到六维的有效算符，并识别出内在热算符，这些算符在零温下消失。这些结果为研究高温环境下的SMEFT提供了一个全面的框架。

Conclusion: The conclusion of this work is that a fully general and consistent framework has been established for constructing the SMEFT operator basis at finite temperature. This framework can be extended to arbitrary mass dimensions and compact connected internal symmetry groups, providing a powerful tool for analyzing the SMEFT in high-temperature regimes.

这项工作的结论是，已经建立了一个完全通用且一致的框架来构建有限温度下的SMEFT算符基。该框架可以扩展到任意质量维度和紧致连通内部对称群，为分析高温状态下的SMEFT提供了一个强大的工具。

Abstract: We present the first complete non-redundant operator basis for the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) at finite temperature, using the imaginary-time formalism. By employing the Hilbert series method on the space-time manifold $\mathbb{R}^3 \times S^1$, we classify all effective operators up to dimension-six. In constructing the basis, we consistently impose integration-by-parts and equations-of-motion constraints along spatial directions. We further analyze the impact of additional constraints, including the vanishing of the curl of the electric and magnetic fields and gauge choices for the temporal components on an operator basis. We also express them in terms of static three-dimensional spatial and zero-temperature SMEFT operators. At dimension five and six, we identify intrinsically thermal operators that vanish in zero temperature. Our framework is fully general and extends to arbitrary mass dimension and compact connected internal symmetry groups.

### [56] [de Sitter Vacua & pUniverses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02883)
*Jeremias Aguilera-Damia,Dionysios Anninos,Tarek Anous,Johnny Gleeson,Alan Rios Fukelman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the $p$-Schwinger model on a de Sitter background, showing that discrete global symmetries can be spontaneously broken in de Sitter space, leading to $p$ degenerate ground states. The model with ${\rm N}_{\rm f}$ flavors is coupled to quantum gravity, and a semiclassical de Sitter saddle is found at large ${\rm N}_{\rm f}$. The $p$ de Sitter invariant vacua are interpreted as microstates of the de Sitter horizon.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the behavior of discrete global symmetries in quantum field theories on a de Sitter background and their implications for the structure of the vacuum states. By extending the Schwinger model to include fermions with non-unit integer charge $p$, the authors aim to understand how these symmetries can be spontaneously broken and how this affects the number of de Sitter invariant vacua. Additionally, the coupling of the model to quantum gravity provides a framework to interpret these vacua in the context of the de Sitter horizon.

Method: The method involves analyzing the $p$-Schwinger model, which is an extension of the Schwinger model where charged massless fermions have a non-unit integer charge $p$. The analysis is performed on a de Sitter background, and the spontaneous breaking of discrete zero- and one-form global symmetries is demonstrated. The model is then coupled to quantum gravity with a positive cosmological constant $\Lambda > 0$, and the existence of a semiclassical de Sitter saddle is shown at large ${\rm N}_{\rm f}$.

Result: The results show that the $p$-Schwinger model on a de Sitter background has $p$ distinct, but locally indistinguishable, de Sitter invariant states, or vacua, satisfying the Hadamard property. When coupled to quantum gravity, the theory exhibits a semiclassical de Sitter saddle at large ${\rm N}_{\rm f}$. These $p$ de Sitter invariant vacua are interpreted as possible microstates of the de Sitter horizon in the low-energy effective field theory.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the $p$-Schwinger model on a de Sitter background can exhibit spontaneously broken discrete global symmetries, leading to $p$ degenerate ground states. The coupling to quantum gravity suggests that these vacua could represent microstates of the de Sitter horizon, providing a new perspective on the structure of de Sitter space and its potential connection to the concept of microstates in black hole physics.

Abstract: We analyze a simple extension of the Schwinger model, which we refer to as the $p$-Schwinger model, on a de Sitter background. In this theory, the charged massless fermions carry non-unit integer charge $p$. In Minkowski space, the $p$-Schwinger model has discrete zero- and one-form global symmetries that are spontaneously broken, yielding $p$ degenerate ground states. We demonstrate that these features persist upon placing the $p$-Schwinger model on a global de Sitter background, establishing that such discrete global symmetries can be spontaneously broken for quantum field theories in de Sitter space. In particular, the theory is endowed with $p$ distinct, but locally-indistinguishable, de Sitter invariant states, the de Sitter vacua, satisfying the Hadamard property. We couple a variant of the $p$-Schwinger model with ${\rm N}_{\rm f}$ flavors to quantum gravity with $Λ>0$, and demonstrate the existence of a semiclassical de Sitter saddle at large ${\rm N}_{\rm f}$. In the gravitational theory, the $p$ de Sitter invariant vacua are speculatively interpreted as microstates of the de Sitter horizon in the low-energy effective field theory.

### [57] [Open-Closed-Open Triality Beyond Matrix Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02885)
*Edward A. Mazenc,Debmalya Sarkar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper explores the open-closed-open triality in twisted holography, showing that the effective potential from integrating out open strings on one stack of branes captures their backreaction on the geometry. This is matched with the action of giant gravitons in the deformed conifold, indicating the emergence of bulk spacetime.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the open-closed-open triality within the framework of twisted holography and to demonstrate how the backreaction of open strings on the geometry can be captured by an effective potential. The goal is also to show that this potential matches the action of giant gravitons in the deformed conifold, thereby providing a direct diagnosis of the emergent bulk spacetime.

动机是理解扭曲全息图框架内的开闭合三重性，并展示如何通过有效势来捕捉开弦对几何的反作用。目标还在于表明，该势与变形锥形中的巨引力子的作用相匹配，从而直接诊断出涌现的体空间。

Method: The method involves starting from two transverse stacks of branes in the B-model on the resolved conifold, leading to two equivalent open string descriptions. These are analyzed as full-fledged field theories, which simplify to gauged $\beta\gamma$-systems with determinant insertions. The $\rho$-matrix models are derived from an on-shell analysis of the field-theory actions. The key step is to integrate out the open strings on one stack of branes to generate an effective potential that captures their backreaction on the geometry, matching it with the action of giant gravitons in the deformed conifold.

方法涉及从解析锥形上的B模型中两个横向堆叠的膜开始，导致两个等效的开弦描述。这些被分析为完整的场论，简化为带有行列式插入的规范$\beta\gamma$系统。$\rho$矩阵模型是从场论作用的在壳分析中得出的。关键步骤是积分掉一个膜堆叠上的开弦以生成有效势，该势捕获了它们对几何的反作用，并将其与变形锥形中巨引力子的作用相匹配。

Result: The results show that the effective potential generated by integrating out the open strings on one stack of branes exactly captures their backreaction on the geometry. This effective potential matches the action of giant gravitons in the deformed conifold, directly diagnosing the emergent bulk spacetime.

结果表明，通过积分掉一个膜堆叠上的开弦所生成的有效势准确地捕捉到了它们对几何的反作用。这个有效势与变形锥形中巨引力子的作用相匹配，直接诊断出涌现的体空间。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the open-closed-open triality in twisted holography provides a clear understanding of the backreaction of open strings on the geometry through the effective potential. This potential's agreement with the action of giant gravitons in the deformed conifold confirms the emergent nature of the bulk spacetime, offering a new perspective on the interplay between open strings and the bulk geometry in the context of holography.

结论是，在扭曲全息图中，开闭合三重性通过有效势提供了对开弦对几何反作用的清晰理解。这种势与变形锥形中巨引力子的作用一致，确认了体空间的涌现性质，为全息背景下开弦与体几何之间的相互作用提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We explore the ideas of open-closed-open triality within twisted holography. Starting from two transverse stacks of branes in the B-model on the resolved conifold, we obtain two equivalent open string descriptions. Both are full-fledged field theories. In the appropriate limit, they simplify to gauged $βγ$-systems with determinant insertions, as expected from open string field theory. The $ρ$-matrix models that have appeared previously in the literature appear from an on-shell analysis of the field-theory actions. Most importantly, we show that the effective potential generated by integrating out the open strings on the other stack of branes exactly captures their backreaction on the geometry. In particular, we match the action of the probe branes to that of giant gravitons in the $\textit{deformed}$ conifold. The second open string description of the triality thus directly diagnoses the emergent bulk spacetime.

### [58] [Full spacetime inversion generated by electromagnetic Abelian gauge transformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00867)
*Alcides Garat*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores the possibility of reversing the flow of time within a spacetime region inside a null surface using electromagnetic gauge transformations. It introduces new tetrads and demonstrates how to create a field configuration that can turn a future-directed timelike vector into a past-directed one, achieving time reversal by physical means.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to investigate whether it is possible to achieve full inversions or time reversal in a specific spacetime region under electromagnetic gauge transformations. The authors aim to build on previous work that showed the kinematic nature of spacetime can be altered with such transformations, and they seek to devise a method for reversing the direction of time through physical means, which has not been discussed before in the literature.

动机是研究在电磁规范变换下，在特定时空区域内是否可能实现完全反转或时间反演。作者旨在基于先前的研究，即通过这样的变换可以改变时空的动力学性质，并寻求通过物理手段逆转时间方向的方法，这在文献中尚未被讨论过。

Method: The method involves introducing new tetrads that depend on electromagnetic gauge and constructing a field configuration that can reverse the flow of time. The authors use these tetrads to demonstrate how a future-directed timelike vector can be transformed into a past-directed timelike vector, thereby achieving time reversal. This is done by manipulating the electromagnetic gauge and observing the resulting changes in the kinematic properties of the spacetime region inside the null surface.

方法涉及引入依赖于电磁规范的新四维基，并构建能够逆转时间流动的场构型。作者使用这些四维基来展示如何将一个未来指向的时间类矢量转换为过去指向的时间类矢量，从而实现时间反演。这是通过操控电磁规范并观察零表面内部时空区域的动力学性质变化来完成的。

Result: The result is a theoretical demonstration that it is possible to physically reverse the flow of time within a spacetime region inside a null surface. 结果是理论上证明了在零表面内的时空区域内物理地逆转时间流动是可能的。作者展示了通过使用引入的四维基和适当的场构型，确实可以将未来指向的时间类矢量转换为过去指向的时间类矢量，从而实现时间反演。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the authors have successfully demonstrated a method for creating a field configuration that can reverse the flow of time within a spacetime region inside a null surface. This is achieved by transforming a future-directed timelike vector into a past-directed one, using new tetrads and electromagnetic gauge transformations. The findings open up new possibilities for further research into the manipulation of spacetime and the potential for time reversal experiments.

结论是作者成功地展示了一种方法，可以在零表面内的时空区域内创建一种能够逆转时间流动的场构型。这是通过使用新的四维基和电磁规范变换将未来指向的时间类矢量转换为过去指向的时间类矢量来实现的。这些发现为操纵时空和进行时间反演实验提供了新的可能性。

In this manuscript we will deal with the possibility of full inversions in a region of spacetime inside a null surface under electromagnetic gauge transformations. Since new tetrads whose construction depends on electromagnetic gauge were introduced it has been proved that the physical kinematic nature of spacetime can be altered as proved previously. In this case we will see how to create a field configuration that will reverse the flow of time. We will prove that we can turn a future directed timelike vector into a past directed timelike vector by physical means. Experiments devised in order to achieve time reversal or full inversion have been never discussed before.

### [59] [Oscillon Formation in Palatini Modified Gravity Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00945)
*Shreyas Upadhye,Sukanta Panda*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores the formation and properties of Oscillons, non-topological solitonic energy configurations, during the preheating phase after Inflation. It uses a modified gravity model with a non-minimal coupling between the scalar field and the Ricci Scalar in the Palatini Formalism. The study reveals that Oscillons dominate for an extended period and generate Ultra-High Frequency Gravitational Waves, detectable by future experiments.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the formation and evolution of Oscillons, which are localized, oscillatory, and quasi-stable energy configurations, during the preheating phase following Inflation. Previous studies have been conducted within the framework of General Relativity using the Metric Formalism. This work aims to explore the dynamics of Oscillons in a modified gravity setting, specifically through a non-minimal coupling with the Ricci Scalar in the context of the Palatini Formalism. The goal is to investigate how these modifications affect the formation and stability of Oscillons and their impact on the early universe's dynamics, including the generation of Gravitational Waves.

动机是理解在通货膨胀之后的预热阶段，Oscillons（局部化、振荡且准稳定的能量构型）的形成和演化。之前的研究是在广义相对论框架下使用度规形式进行的。本工作旨在探索在修改引力设置下的Oscillons动力学，特别是通过标量场与Ricci标量之间的非最小耦合在Palatini形式下的影响。目标是研究这些修改如何影响Oscillons的形成和稳定性及其对早期宇宙动力学的影响，包括引力波的产生。

Method: The method involves modifying the Einstein-Hilbert action by introducing a non-minimal coupling between the scalar field and the Ricci Scalar, $R$. The analysis is performed in the Palatini Formalism, which treats the metric and connection as independent variables. The potential for the scalar field is assumed to be polynomial. Numerical simulations are carried out using CosmoLattice, a lattice-based numerical code, to solve the equations of motion for the scalar field. These simulations help in understanding the dynamics of the Inflaton field, the formation of Oscillons, and the power spectrum of perturbations. Additionally, the equation of state and the primordial Gravitational Wave spectrum due to the asymmetric distribution of Oscillons are studied.

方法涉及通过引入标量场与Ricci标量$R$之间的非最小耦合来修改Einstein-Hilbert作用量。分析在Palatini形式下进行，该形式将度规和联络视为独立变量。假设标量场的势为多项式形式。数值模拟使用基于晶格的数值代码CosmoLattice进行，以求解标量场的运动方程。这些模拟有助于理解Inflaton场的动力学、Oscillons的形成以及扰动的功率谱。此外，还研究了由于Oscillons的不对称分布引起的方程状态和原初引力波谱。

Result: The results show that the scalar field dynamics governed by the modified gravity model lead to the formation of Oscillons, which exhibit oscillatory and decaying behavior. The power spectrum of perturbations shows growth in $k$ modes, consistent with the expected behavior of Oscillons. The equation of state indicates an extended period of Oscillon domination in the early universe. Furthermore, the study reveals that the asymmetric distribution of Oscillons generates Ultra-High Frequency Gravitational Waves, which lie in the range of planned future detectors and experiments.

结果表明，由修改后的引力模型控制的标量场动力学导致Oscillons的形成，这些Oscillons表现出振荡和衰减行为。扰动的功率谱显示$k$模式的增长，与预期的Oscillons行为一致。方程状态表明，在早期宇宙中存在一个延长的Oscillons主导时期。此外，研究揭示了Oscillons的不对称分布产生了超高频引力波，这些引力波位于计划中的未来探测器和实验的范围内。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the modified gravity model with a non-minimal coupling between the scalar field and the Ricci Scalar in the Palatini Formalism supports the formation and long-term stability of Oscillons. These Oscillons dominate the early universe for an extended period and generate Ultra-High Frequency Gravitational Waves, which could be detected by future gravitational wave observatories. This work provides new insights into the role of modified gravity in the dynamics of the early universe and the potential for observing the effects of such modifications through gravitational waves.

结论是，在Palatini形式下标量场与Ricci标量之间具有非最小耦合的修改引力模型支持Oscillons的形成和长期稳定性。这些Oscillons在早期宇宙中占据主导地位，并产生超高频引力波，这些引力波可能被未来的引力波天文台探测到。这项工作为修改引力在早期宇宙动力学中的作用提供了新的见解，并展示了通过引力波观测这种修改效应的可能性。

Abstract: We investigate the formation of spatially localized, oscillatory in time and non topological solitonic, quasi-stable energy configurations, Oscillons, which are formed at the end of Inflationary epoch, during the preheating phase and decay over long periods of time. Oscillons have been previously studied in literature in the regime of General Relativity using Metric Formalism. In this paper we look for formation of these energy lumps by modifying the gravity part of the Einstein Hilbert Action, considering a non minimal coupling of the scalar field with Ricci Scalar,$R$, and working in an alternative formulation of General Relativity known as Palatini Formalism. The potential we consider is of polynomial form. We demonstrate numerically, using CosmoLattice, that the equation governing the dynamics of the Inflaton scalar field give oscillatory and decaying solutions as it is expected in the case of Oscillons, with power spectrum governing the growth of perturbations of $k$ modes. The equation of state reveals an extended period of Oscillon domination in the early universe. Along with this, the Primordial Gravitational Wave spectrum due to asymmetric distribution of these energy configurations have also been studied. We observe that these generate Ultra-High Frequency regime Gravitational Waves, which lie in the range of the planned future detectors and experiments.

### [60] [Nonperturbative Danielson-Satishchandran-Wald Decoherence with Unruh-DeWitt detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00956)
*Levy B. N. Batista,André G. S. Landulfo,Robert B. Mann,George E. A. Matsas*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the DSW mechanism of decoherence for uniformly accelerated charges and masses in superposition, using a gapless finite-time detector interacting with a massive scalar field. The study is nonperturbative and aims to provide a controlled analysis of the decoherence process.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the DSW mechanism, which proposes that decoherence of spatial superpositions of uniformly accelerated charges and masses can occur due to the emission and absorption of soft photons and gravitons. This effect is significant because it suggests a novel source of decoherence in spacetimes with bifurcating Killing horizons, and the authors aim to understand this mechanism in a more controlled setting.

Method: The method involves using a gapless finite-time detector that is prepared in a spatial superposition of uniformly accelerated paths in Minkowski spacetime. The detector interacts with a massive scalar field, and the calculations are performed nonperturbatively to analyze the decoherence process.

Result: The results of the study highlight the main factors contributing to the decoherence process under the DSW mechanism. By using a gapless finite-time detector and a massive scalar field, the authors are able to provide a detailed and controlled analysis of how the interaction leads to decoherence in a finite proper time.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the DSW mechanism of decoherence for uniformly accelerated charges and masses in superposition is effectively analyzed using a gapless finite-time detector and a massive scalar field. The nonperturbative approach allows for a deeper understanding of the factors that contribute to this interesting decoherence process.

Abstract: Recently, Danielson, Satishchandran, and Wald (DSW) have proposed a novel source of decoherence for uniformly accelerated charges and masses in spatial superposition in spacetimes containing a bifurcating Killing horizon. Such an effect can be traced back to the emission and absorption of soft photons and gravitons, which effectively act as "which-path'' information probes. This results in the decoherence of any such superposition in a finite proper time. With this in mind, we study the DSW mechanism using a gapless finite-time detector prepared in a spatial superposition of uniformly accelerated paths in Minkowski spacetime that interacts with a massive scalar field. The calculation is nonperturbative. Such a model will enable us to analyze the decoherence process in a more controlled manner, highlighting the main factors that give rise to this interesting mechanism.

</details>

*Paulo Luz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper presents a general series solution to the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equations for compact stellar objects, using an algorithm to compute power series coefficients based on the equation of state and its derivatives. The solutions are used to derive closed-form expressions for the radius and mass of stellar objects, and the formalism is extended to piecewise equations of state.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to provide a more systematic and analytical approach to solving the TOV equations, which describe the structure of compact stellar objects. By developing a general series solution, the authors aim to gain deeper insights into the properties of analytic solutions and their relation to the regularity of the equation of state. This approach allows for the derivation of closed-form expressions for the radius and mass of stellar objects, which can be compared with numerical results and applied to different models, including fluids with affine and polytropic equations of state, as well as piecewise equations of state.

Method: The method involves developing a general series solution to the TOV equations. The authors create an algorithm to compute the coefficients of the power series in terms of the equation of state and its derivatives with respect to thermodynamic variables. They then use the theory of Padé approximants to derive series representations for meromorphic functions, which can have domains of convergence that include isolated poles. These series solutions are applied to specific models, such as fluids with affine and polytropic equations of state, and the results are compared with those from numerical integration. The formalism is also extended to piecewise equations of state, allowing for the matching of series solutions across transition hypersurfaces.

Result: The results of the paper include the derivation of general series solutions to the TOV equations, which are used to establish the properties of analytic solutions and their relation to the regularity of the equation of state. Closed-form expressions for the radius and mass of stellar objects are obtained, and the formalism is successfully applied to specific models, including fluids with affine and polytropic equations of state. The comparison with numerical integration shows good agreement, and the extension to piecewise equations of state allows for the matching of series solutions across transition hypersurfaces.

Conclusion: The conclusion of the paper is that the general series solutions to the TOV equations provide a powerful and flexible tool for analyzing the structure of compact stellar objects. The derived closed-form expressions for the radius and mass of stellar objects offer a valuable alternative to numerical methods, and the extension to piecewise equations of state demonstrates the versatility of the approach. The results highlight the importance of the regularity of the equation of state in determining the properties of analytic solutions.

Abstract: We present general series solutions to the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations for compact stellar objects. We develop an algorithm to compute the coefficients of the power series in terms of the equation of state and its derivatives with respect to the thermodynamic variables. Using these results, we establish general properties of analytic solutions and their relation to the regularity of the equation of state. Applying the theory of Padé approximants, we derive series representations for meromorphic functions whose domains of convergence may include isolated poles. These analytic solutions are then used to obtain closed-form expressions to approximate the radius and mass of stellar objects. We apply the formalism to specific models, namely fluids with affine equations of state and polytropic fluids, and compare the results with those obtained from numerical integration. Lastly, we extend the formalism to piecewise equations of state, deriving series solutions that can be matched across transition hypersurfaces.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the potential observational signatures of traversable wormholes through the analysis of the gravitational-wave signals produced when a stellar-mass black hole falls into such a wormhole. 动机是通过分析恒星级黑洞落入这种虫洞时产生的引力波信号，来探索可穿越虫洞的潜在观测特征。该研究旨在提供一个理论框架，以便在未来引力波观测中识别这些奇异天体。

Method: The method involves modeling the infalling black hole as a test particle and deriving analytic expressions for the emitted gravitational waveform, including contributions from the mass quadrupole and higher-order multipoles. The authors also compute the amplitude spectral density and compare it with the sensitivities of representative ground-based gravitational-wave detectors.

方法包括将落下的黑洞建模为试探粒子，并推导出所发射引力波形的解析表达式，其中包括质量四极矩和更高阶多极矩的贡献。作者还计算了振幅谱密度，并将其与代表性的地面引力波探测器的灵敏度进行了比较。

Result: The results show that the gravitational-wave signal has a characteristic pulse-gap structure due to repeated throat crossings of the traversable wormhole. The signal's amplitude spectral density suggests that such signals could be within the sensitivity range of current ground-based detectors for optimally oriented sources at distances up to ~500 Mpc.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the gravitational-wave signal from a stellar-mass black hole falling into a traversable wormhole could serve as a potential observational signature for these exotic spacetime structures. The detection of such signals would provide strong evidence for the existence of traversable wormholes and open new avenues for testing fundamental physics.

结论是，恒星级黑洞落入可穿越虫洞所产生的引力波信号可以作为这些奇异时空结构的潜在观测特征。此类信号的检测将为可穿越虫洞的存在提供强有力的证据，并为检验基本物理开辟新的途径。

Abstract: We compute the gravitational-wave signal generated by the radial infall of a stellar-mass black hole into a thin-shell Schwarzschild traversable wormhole. Modeling the black hole as a test particle, we derive analytic expressions for the emitted waveform, including contributions from the mass quadrupole and higher-order multipoles. The resulting signal exhibits a characteristic pulse-gap structure associated with repeated throat crossings. We further compute the amplitude spectral density and compare it with representative ground-based detector sensitivities, finding that such signals could lie within the sensitivity range for optimally oriented sources at distances of order ~500 Mpc. These results provide a potential observational signature of traversable wormholes in gravitational-wave data.

Method: The authors start from the first law of black hole thermodynamics, establishing a correspondence between the corrected entropy and the metric function under fixed black hole energy and horizon position. They then use the corrected metric to compute the photon sphere radius and shadow size, and compare these results with Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) observations of Sgr A* to constrain the parameters.

作者从黑洞热力学第一定律出发，在固定黑洞能量和视界位置的条件下，建立了修正熵和度规函数之间的对应关系。然后，他们使用修正后的度规计算光子球半径和阴影大小，并将这些结果与Sgr A*的事件视界望远镜（EHT）观测结果进行比较，以限制参数范围。

Conclusion: The study provides a feasible approach for testing generalized entropy frameworks and probing deviations from the Bekenstein-Hawking area law by constraining the parameter range introduced in the corrected entropy through comparisons with EHT observations of Sgr A*.

该研究通过与Sgr A*的EHT观测结果进行比较，限制了修正熵中引入的参数范围，从而提供了一种测试广义熵框架和探测偏离Bekenstein-Hawking面积定律的方法。

Abstract: Starting from the first law of black hole thermodynamics, we establish an explicit correspondence between the corrected entropy and the metric function under the condition of fixed black hole energy and horizon position. Using the corrected metric, we further compute the photon sphere radius and shadow size, demonstrating that different entropy corrections lead to characteristic optical shifts. By comparing with the Event Horizon Telescope observations of Sgr A*, we constrain the parameter range introduced in the corrected entropy. Method: The study employs a particular functional form of $f(Q, L_m)$ gravity to derive explicit field equations. The static spherically symmetric structures are analyzed using two innovative non-singular solutions. Smooth matching conditions are used to determine the values of unknown constants in the metric coefficients. Conclusion: The considered anisotropic compact objects in the $f(Q, L_m)$ gravity framework are found to be viable and stable, as all the required physical conditions are satisfied. 在$f(Q, L_m)$引力框架下考虑的各向异性致密天体被发现是可行且稳定的，因为所有必要的物理条件都得到了满足。通过声速方法确认了稳定性，并通过各种重要物理特性的图形分析评估了可行性。

Abstract: This manuscript examines viability and stability of anisotropic compact objects in the framework of $f(Q,L_m)$ gravity ($Q$ is the non-metricity and $L_m$ is the matter Lagrangian). We assume a particular functional form of this theory to get explicit expressions for the field equations which govern the behavior of matter and geometry in this context. The configuration of static spherically symmetric structures is evaluated using the two innovative non-singular solutions. We use smooth matching conditions to evaluate the values of unknown constants in the metric coefficients. The viability of considered compact stars is assessed using a graphic analysis of various important physical characteristics. We also investigate stability of the considered stellar objects through sound speed method. It is found that these stellar objects are viable and stable, as all the required conditions are satisfied.
