### [65] [Acausal exact vacuum solutions in nonlocal gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01413)
*Zhe Zhao,Leonardo Modesto,Cosimo Bambi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that a specific subclass of Gödel-type Universes, which allow closed time-like curves, is an exact solution in nonlocal gravity. This finding is consistent with a well-defined quantum theory but requires a particular class of nonlocal form factors. The causality violation occurs from the nonlocal fundamental scale to macroscopic scales, and the presence of matter breaks the degeneracy between Minkowski and Gödel Universes. At the non-perturbative quantum level, the transition from a flat to a Gödel Universe is extremely small.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the classical equations of motion in nonlocal gravity, specifically focusing on whether Gödel-type Universes, which allow for closed time-like curves, can be exact solutions. The aim is to understand the implications of such solutions on the renormalizability and causality of the theory.

动机是探索非局部引力中的经典运动方程，特别是关注允许闭合类时曲线的哥德尔型宇宙是否可以成为精确解。目的是理解这些解对理论的重整化性和因果性的影响。

Method: The authors use the classical equations of motion in nonlocal gravity and analyze a specific subclass of Gödel-type Universes. They explicitly show that these Universes are exact solutions in vacuum. The analysis also involves examining the role of nonlocal form factors and their impact on the consistency of the theory at the quantum level.

作者使用非局部引力的经典运动方程，分析了哥德尔型宇宙的一个特定子类。他们明确地展示了这些宇宙在真空中是精确解。分析还涉及研究非局部形式因子的作用及其对量子水平上理论一致性的影响。

Result: The result is that a particular subclass of Gödel-type Universes, allowing for closed time-like curves, is an exact solution in nonlocal gravity. This solution is consistent with a well-defined quantum theory, but it requires a special class of nonlocal form factors. The causality violation is observed from the nonlocal fundamental scale to macroscopic scales, and the presence of matter breaks the degeneracy between Minkowski and Gödel Universes. At the non-perturbative quantum level, the transition probability from a flat to a Gödel Universe is extremely small.

结果是，允许闭合类时曲线的哥德尔型宇宙的一个特定子类是非局部引力的精确解。这个解与一个定义良好的量子理论一致，但它需要一类特殊的非局部形式因子。从非局部基本尺度到宏观尺度都观察到了因果性的违反，物质的存在打破了闵可夫斯基宇宙和哥德尔宇宙之间的简并。在非微扰量子水平上，从平坦宇宙到哥德尔宇宙的跃迁概率极小。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that while nonlocal gravity allows for Gödel-type Universes as exact solutions, the causality violation associated with these solutions is significant. The presence of matter plays a crucial role in breaking the degeneracy between Minkowski and Gödel Universes. The renormalizability requirement alone is not sufficient to avoid causality violation in vacuum. The transition from a flat to a Gödel Universe at the non-perturbative quantum level is negligibly small, indicating that such transitions are highly unlikely.

结论是，虽然非局部引力允许哥德尔型宇宙作为精确解，但与这些解相关的因果性违反是显著的。物质的存在在打破闵可夫斯基宇宙和哥德尔宇宙之间的简并中起着关键作用。仅靠重整化要求不足以避免真空中的因果性违反。在非微扰量子水平上，从平坦宇宙到哥德尔宇宙的跃迁极小，表明这种跃迁极不可能发生。

Abstract: Nonlocal gravity is a promising super-renormalizable or finite quantum gravity theory consistent with unitarity. In this paper, we focus on the classical equations of motion and explicitly show that a particular subclass of Gödel-type Universes, where closed time-like curves are allowed, is an exact solution of nonlocal gravity in vacuum. The result is consistent with a well defined theory at quantum level, but it is realized only with a special, although large, class of nonlocal form factors. Therefore, by itself the renormalizability requirement is not a sufficient guiding principle in vacuum whether we want to avoid the causality violation. From the physical point of view, the causality violation takes place from the non locality fundamental scale to macroscopic scales. Therefore, it is the presence of matter to break the classical degeneracy between the Minkowski and the Gödel Universe. Finally, we have shown that at the non-perturbative quantum level the transition from a flat to a Gödel Universe is ridiculously small.

### [66] [A note on methods for computing the critical curve of Kerr-like black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01426)
*Siddharth Kumar Sahoo,Indrani Banerjee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This study compares three definitions of the critical curve (shadow) of Kerr-like black holes and finds that they agree in vacuum or inhomogeneous plasma at large distances, but diverge for finite-distance observers. In homogeneous plasma, Bardeen's definition contracts with increasing density, contradicting other definitions. The effect of tetrad changes on the critical curve is also explored, showing only a horizontal shift.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to systematically compare and analyze the different celestial coordinate definitions of the critical curve (or shadow) of Kerr-like blackholes, as proposed by Bardeen, de Vries, and Grenzebach et al. The aim is to understand the behavior of these definitions under various conditions, such as the presence of plasma and the location of the observer.

本文的动机是系统地比较和分析Bardeen、de Vries 和 Grenzebach等人提出的Kerr类黑洞临界曲线（或阴影）的不同天球坐标定义。目的是了解这些定义在各种条件下的行为，例如等离子体的存在和观察者的位置。

Method: The method involves a systematic comparison of the three definitions of the critical curve: Bardeen's, de Vries's, and Grenzebach et al.'s. The study considers black holes in vacuum, surrounded by inhomogeneous and homogeneous plasma, and examines the impact of the observer's distance. Additionally, the effect of changing tetrads (Bardeen and Carter tetrads) on the critical curve is analyzed, particularly in the presence of plasma.

该方法涉及对临界曲线的三种定义进行系统的比较：Bardeen 的、de Vries 的和 Grenzebach 等人的定义。研究考虑了真空中的黑洞、被不均匀和均匀等离子体包围的黑洞，并检查了观察者距离的影响。此外，还分析了改变四元数（Bardeen 和 Carter 四元数）对临界曲线的影响，特别是在存在等离子体的情况下。

Result: The results show that all three definitions of the critical curve agree for black holes in vacuum or surrounded by inhomogeneous plasma when observed from large distances. However, for finite-distance observers, the definitions diverge, with Bardeen's yielding the smallest critical curve and de Vries's the largest. In the case of homogeneous plasma, Bardeen's definition deviates and contracts compared to the vacuum case, which contradicts the predictions of de Vries's and Grenzebach et al.'s definitions. The change of tetrads introduces only a horizontal shift in the critical curve.

结果表明，当从远距离观察时，这三种临界曲线定义在真空或被不均匀等离子体包围的黑洞中是一致的。然而，对于有限距离的观察者，这些定义出现分歧，Bardeen 的定义产生最小的临界曲线，而 de Vries 的定义产生最大的临界曲线。在均匀等离子体的情况下，Bardeen 的定义偏离并收缩，与真空情况相比，这与 de Vries 和 Grenzebach 等人的定义预测相矛盾。四元数的变化仅在临界曲线上引入水平偏移。

Conclusion: The study concludes that while the three definitions of the critical curve agree in certain conditions, they significantly differ in others, particularly for finite-distance observers and in the presence of homogeneous plasma. This highlights the importance of carefully choosing the appropriate definition depending on the physical context. The horizontal shift introduced by the change of tetrads suggests that the choice of tetrad can affect the apparent position of the critical curve.

研究得出结论，在某些条件下，三种临界曲线定义是一致的，但在其他情况下显著不同，特别是对于有限距离的观察者和存在均匀等离子体的情况。这强调了根据物理背景仔细选择适当定义的重要性。四元数变化引入的水平偏移表明，四元数的选择可能会影响临界曲线的表观位置。

Abstract: This study systematically compares Bardeen's, de Vries's, and Grenzebach et al.'s celestial coordinate definitions of the critical curve ("shadow") of Kerr-like black holes. We find that all three definitions agree for black holes in vacuum or surrounded by inhomogeneous plasma observed from large distances. However, they diverge for observers located at a finite distance: Bardeen's definition yields the smallest critical curve, while de Vries's yields the largest. When homogeneous plasma is considered, critical curve computed using Bardeen's definition deviates from the other two even at large distances and contracts compared to the vacuum case with increasing plasma density. This is in clear contradiction with the behaviour predicted by de Vries's, Grenzebach et al.'s definitions, and previous gravitational lensing studies. We derive de Vries's definition assuming a critical curve on the observer's sky plane and explain its discrepancy with Grenzebach et al.'s definition. We further explore the effect of the change of tetrad on the critical curve. Using Bardeen and Carter tetrads, we plot the critical curve for Schwarzschild and Kerr black holes in the presence of plasma, highlighting that tetrad changes introduce only a horizontal shift in the critical curve.

### [67] [Constraints on Einstein-aether gravity from the precision timing of PSR J1738+0333](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01436)
*Massimo Vaglio,Amodio Carleo,Abhimanyu Susobhanan,Enrico Barausse,Bilel Ben Salem,Alessandro Corongiu,Paulo C. C. Freire,Delphine Perrodin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper uses high-precision pulsar timing data to constrain the parameters of Einstein-aether gravity, a Lorentz-violating extension of General Relativity. The authors apply Bayesian methods to obtain stringent constraints on the theory's coupling constants, providing the strongest bounds from a single binary pulsar system.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to test and constrain the parameters of Einstein-aether gravity, a Lorentz-violating modification of General Relativity, using precise pulsar timing data. This is important for understanding fundamental physics and testing the limits of general relativity in strong gravitational fields.

动机是使用精确的脉冲星计时数据来测试和约束爱因斯坦以太引力的参数，这是一种洛伦兹违反的广义相对论修正。这对于理解基础物理并在强引力场中检验广义相对论的极限非常重要。

Method: The method involves using updated high-precision pulsar timing observations from multiple observatories, including EPTA and NANOGrav, to analyze the first post-Newtonian (1PN) corrections arising from Lorentz violation. The authors use the Bayesian timing pipeline Vela to process the full dataset of times of arrival (ToAs) and sample the joint posterior over binary component masses, post-Keplerian parameters, and center-of-mass velocity components. A resampling scheme is then applied to derive robust constraints on the fundamental theory parameters.

方法涉及使用来自多个天文台（包括EPTA和NANOGrav）的更新高精度脉冲星计时观测数据，分析由洛伦兹违反引起的一阶后牛顿（1PN）修正。作者使用贝叶斯计时管道Vela处理完整的到达时间（ToAs）数据集，并对双星组分质量、后开普勒参数和质心速度分量的联合后验进行采样。然后应用重采样方案来推导对基本理论参数的稳健约束。

Result: The results include the most stringent strong-field bounds on the Einstein-aether coupling constants obtained from a single binary pulsar system, PSR J1738+0333. These constraints are derived from the combined analysis of conservative and dissipative 1PN corrections, and they provide significant improvements over previous bounds.

结果包括从单个双星脉冲星系统PSR J1738+0333获得的对爱因斯坦以太耦合常数的最严格的强场约束。这些约束是从保守和耗散1PN修正的综合分析中得出的，并且相比之前的约束有了显著改进。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the updated high-precision pulsar timing data, combined with advanced Bayesian analysis techniques, have provided the most stringent constraints on the Einstein-aether coupling constants to date. This work advances our understanding of Lorentz-violating theories and their implications for gravitational physics.

结论是，结合先进的贝叶斯分析技术，更新的高精度脉冲星计时数据提供了迄今为止对爱因斯坦以太耦合常数最严格的约束。这项工作推进了我们对洛伦兹违反理论及其对引力物理影响的理解。

Abstract: We constrain Einstein-aether gravity -- a Lorentz-violating extension of General Relativity in which a dynamical, unit timelike vector field selects a preferred frame -- using updated high-precision pulsar timing observations of PSR J1738+0333 from EPTA second Data Release and the NANOGrav 9-year release, in combination with ToAs from Arecibo, Green Bank, Nancay, Parkes, and Westerbork. Our method accounts for both conservative and dissipative first post-Newtonian corrections arising from Lorentz violation; here we apply it to PSR J1738+0333 using the Bayesian timing pipeline Vela to process the full ToA dataset. We sample the joint posterior over binary component masses, post-Keplerian parameters and center-of-mass velocity components, and then apply a resampling scheme to propagate posteriors into robust constraints on the fundamental theory parameters, obtaining the most stringent strong-field bounds on the Einstein-aether coupling constants from a single binary pulsar system to date.

### [68] [On the formulations of the Fermat principle in general relativity and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01532)
*Erasmo Caponio,Miguel Angel Javaloyes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper surveys the Fermat principle in general relativity, from classical optics to modern variational formulations, addressing mathematical difficulties and exploring extensions to various scenarios including extended sources, Finsler spacetimes, and non-continuous interfaces.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to provide a comprehensive overview of the Fermat principle within the context of general relativity. It aims to bridge the gap between the historical development of the principle in classical optics and its contemporary applications in Lorentzian geometry, while also addressing the inherent mathematical challenges and presenting possible solutions.

本文的动机是全面概述广义相对论框架下的费马原理。它旨在弥合该原理在经典光学中的历史发展与其在洛伦兹几何中的当代应用之间的差距，同时解决内在的数学挑战并提出可能的解决方案。

Method: The authors present a proof of the Fermat principle using smooth lightlike curves in the framework of general relativity. They analyze the mathematical difficulties, particularly the non-smooth manifold structure of the space of lightlike curves in the Sobolev topology due to the null condition. To overcome these issues, they discuss alternative frameworks that utilize the quadratic arrival time functional to establish multiplicity results for light rays. Additionally, they explore extensions of the principle to various settings, such as extended sources and receivers, arbitrary arrival curves, timelike geodesics with prescribed proper time, Finsler spacetimes, and scenarios with a non-continuous interface leading to a Snell law.

作者使用光滑类光曲线在广义相对论框架下证明了费马原理。他们分析了数学上的困难，特别是由于零条件导致Sobolev拓扑中类光曲线空间的非光滑流形结构。为了解决这些问题，他们讨论了利用二次到达时间泛函来建立光线多重性结果的替代框架。此外，他们还探讨了将该原理扩展到各种场景，例如扩展源和接收器、任意到达曲线、具有规定固有时的类时测地线、芬斯勒时空以及导致斯涅尔定律的非连续界面场景。

Result: The paper demonstrates that the space of lightlike curves in the Sobolev topology does not admit a smooth manifold structure, which poses a significant challenge for the variational formulation of the Fermat principle. The authors propose alternative frameworks, such as the use of the quadratic arrival time functional, to address these challenges. They also show how the Fermat principle can be extended to various physical scenarios, providing a more robust and versatile understanding of the principle.

论文表明，在Sobolev拓扑中类光曲线的空间不具有光滑流形结构，这对费马原理的变分公式提出了重大挑战。作者提出了替代框架，如使用二次到达时间泛函来解决这些挑战。他们还展示了如何将费马原理扩展到各种物理场景，提供了对该原理更稳健和多样的理解。

Conclusion: The paper concludes by emphasizing the importance of the Fermat principle in general relativity and its applicability to a wide range of physical scenarios. Despite the mathematical difficulties, the authors provide a rigorous and detailed analysis, offering new insights and potential solutions. The work highlights the need for further research into the variational principles and their applications in general relativity.

论文总结强调了费马原理在广义相对论中的重要性及其在广泛物理场景中的适用性。尽管存在数学上的困难，作者提供了严谨和详细的分析，提供了新的见解和潜在的解决方案。这项工作突显了进一步研究变分原理及其在广义相对论中应用的必要性。

Abstract: This paper presents a survey of the Fermat principle within the framework of general relativity, tracing its evolution from classical optics to its modern variational formulation in Lorentzian geometry. In particular, we provide its proof in the framework of smooth lightlike curves. We also analyze the mathematical difficulties inherent in the relativistic setting, specifically demonstrating that the space of lightlike curves in the Sobolev topology does not admit a smooth manifold structure due to the cone nature of the null condition. To address these variational obstacles, we discuss alternative frameworks highlighting the role of the quadratic arrival time functional in establishing multiplicity results for light rays. Furthermore, we explore significant extensions of the principle, such as its application to extended sources and receivers, arbitrary arrival curves, timelike geodesics with prescribed proper time, Finsler spacetimes, or settings with a non-continuous interface giving rise to a Snell law.

### [69] [Relational quantum dynamics of the black hole interior: singularity resolution and quantum bounce](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01576)
*Paolo Fragolino,Saeed Rastgoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the interior of a Schwarzschild black hole using a relational and gauge-invariant quantization framework. It constructs the physical Hilbert space via refined algebraic quantization and uses the Page-Wootters formalism with a covariant POVM clock for quantum dynamics. The study finds that the Kretschmann and expansion scalars remain finite, and the area of 2-spheres is bounded below by a minimum value, indicating a black-hole-to-white-hole transition at the quantum bounce.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the quantum nature of the interior of a Schwarzschild black hole, specifically focusing on resolving the classical singularity and understanding the behavior of key observables such as the area of 2-spheres, the Kretschmann scalar, and the expansion scalar of null geodesics. The authors aim to use a fully relational and gauge-invariant quantization framework to achieve this.

动机是探索史瓦西黑洞内部的量子性质，特别是解决经典奇点问题，并理解关键可观测量（如2-球面面积、Kretschmann标量和零测地线的膨胀标量）的行为。作者旨在使用完全关系性和规范不变的量子化框架来实现这一目标。

Method: The method involves constructing the physical Hilbert space via refined algebraic quantization and employing the Page-Wootters formalism with a covariant POVM clock. The clock is built from one of the two configuration variables, and its Hamiltonian is proportional to the momentum of that variable. Gauge-invariant relational observables are constructed using group averaging (G-twirl) and evaluated on physical states. The study is carried out in a way that is independent of any specific quantization scheme other than the Schrodinger representation.

方法涉及通过精细代数量化构造物理希尔伯特空间，并使用带有协变POVM时钟的Page-Wootters形式。时钟由两个配置变量中的一个构建，其哈密顿量与该变量的动量成正比。使用群平均（G-twirl）构造规范不变的关系可观测量，并在物理态上进行评估。研究以独立于任何特定量化方案的方式进行，除了薛定谔表示法。

Result: The results show that the Kretschmann and expansion scalars remain finite throughout the black hole, while the area of 2-spheres is bounded below by a minimum value, which is proportional to the uncertainty in the system variable. The expansion scalar vanishes and changes sign at the quantum bounce, indicating a black-hole-to-white-hole transition. These findings hold for any general clock whose operator forms a canonical pair with the clock Hamiltonian.

结果表明，Kretschmann标量和膨胀标量在整个黑洞中保持有限，而2-球面的面积有一个最小值下界，该下界与系统变量的不确定性成正比。膨胀标量在量子反弹处消失并改变符号，表明从黑洞到白洞的转变。这些发现适用于任何与时钟哈密顿量形成正则对的一般时钟算符。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the singularity resolution in the interior of the Schwarzschild black hole emerges directly from the principles of relationality, the Heisenberg uncertainty principle, and the structure of the physical Hilbert space. The study provides a clear picture of the quantum behavior of the black hole interior, including the boundedness of the 2-sphere area and the transition from a black hole to a white hole.

结论是，史瓦西黑洞内部的奇点解析直接源于关系性原理、海森堡不确定性原理以及物理希尔伯特空间的结构。研究提供了黑洞内部量子行为的清晰图景，包括2-球面面积的有界性和从黑洞到白洞的转变。

Abstract: We study the interior of the Schwarzschild black hole which is isometric to the Kantowski-Sachs cosmological model, using a fully relational and gauge-invariant quantization framework. The physical Hilbert space is constructed via refined algebraic quantization, and quantum dynamics is recovered through the Page-Wootters formalism with a covariant POVM clock built from one of the two configuration variables, whose Hamiltonian is proportional to the momentum of the said variable. Gauge-invariant relational observables for the area of 2-spheres, the Kretschmann scalar, and the expansion scalar of null geodesic are constructed via group averaging (G-twirl) and evaluated on physical states. We find that the Kretschmann and expansion scalars remain finite throughout the black hole, while the area of 2-spheres is bounded below by a minimum value proportional to the uncertainty in the system variable, which is the other configuration variable distinct from the clock variable. In particular, the expansion scalar vanishes and changes sign at the quantum bounce, establishing a black-hole-to-white-hole transition. These results hold for any general clock whose operator forms a canonical pair with the clock Hamiltonian, and require no specific quantization scheme other than the Schrodinger representation. The singularity resolution emerges directly from relationality, the Heisenberg uncertainty principle, and the structure of the physical Hilbert space.

</details>


### [70] [Dyonic Ellis-Bronnikov wormholes from warped extra dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01602)
*Francisco S. N. Lobo,Miguel A. S. Pinto,Manuel E. Rodrigues*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper explores traversable wormhole solutions in a 4D effective theory derived from a 5D Einstein-Maxwell-Chern-Simons action with a non-minimally coupled scalar field. The authors classify various configurations, including pure phantom-supported and fully coupled dilaton-axion-gauge configurations, demonstrating that regular, asymptotically flat, traversable 4D wormholes can emerge naturally from higher-dimensional scalar-tensor theories.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to investigate the existence of traversable wormholes within a 4D effective theory derived from a 5D Einstein-Maxwell-Chern-Simons (EMCS) action. The authors aim to explore how such wormholes, which are supported by various fields, can arise from higher-dimensional scalar-tensor theories.

动机是研究在由五维Einstein-Maxwell-Chern-Simons（EMCS）作用导出的四维有效理论中可穿越虫洞的存在。作者旨在探索这些由各种场支持的虫洞如何从高维标量-张量理论中自然产生。

Method: The method involves using a warped Kaluza-Klein compactification to derive an Einstein-frame theory in four dimensions. This theory includes a phantom dilaton, a canonical axion, a Maxwell field, and a Kaluza-Klein vector. The authors focus on the Ellis-Bronnikov geometry and construct solutions that incorporate both dyonic Maxwell and Kaluza-Klein fields. For exponential gauge couplings, the Einstein equations determine the scalar kinetic term and the combined potentials, while the remaining field equations reduce to algebraic relations fixing the individual potentials and the radial behavior of the electric charges.

方法包括使用翘曲Kaluza-Klein紧致化来导出四维的Einstein框架理论。该理论包括一个phantom dilaton、一个canonical axion、一个Maxwell场和一个Kaluza-Klein矢量。作者专注于Ellis-Bronnikov几何，并构建包含dyonic Maxwell和Kaluza-Klein场的解。对于指数型规范耦合，Einstein方程确定了标量动能项和组合势能，而其余的场方程则简化为代数关系，固定了各个势能和电荷的径向行为。

Result: The results show a systematic classification of configurations, ranging from pure phantom-supported wormholes to fully coupled dilaton-axion-gauge configurations. The Kaluza-Klein sector enriches the solution space with additional structure while preserving analytic tractability. These findings demonstrate that regular, asymptotically flat, traversable 4D wormholes can naturally arise from higher-dimensional scalar-tensor theories.

结果表明，从纯phantom支持的虫洞到完全耦合的dilaton-axion-gauge配置，系统地分类了各种配置。Kaluza-Klein部门通过增加额外的结构丰富了解空间，同时保持了分析的可处理性。这些发现表明，规则的、渐近平坦的、可穿越的四维虫洞可以自然地从高维标量-张量理论中产生。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that regular, asymptotically flat, traversable 4D wormholes can naturally arise from higher-dimensional scalar-tensor theories. The inclusion of the Kaluza-Klein sector provides additional structure and complexity to the solutions, while maintaining their analytic tractability. This work opens up new avenues for understanding the nature of wormholes in higher-dimensional theories.

结论是，规则的、渐近平坦的、可穿越的四维虫洞可以自然地从高维标量-张量理论中产生。引入Kaluza-Klein部门为解提供了额外的结构和复杂性，同时保持了解的分析可处理性。这项工作为理解高维理论中的虫洞性质开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: We investigate traversable wormhole solutions within a four-dimensional effective theory derived from a five-dimensional Einstein-Maxwell-Chern-Simons action with a non-minimally coupled scalar field. A warped Kaluza-Klein compactification yields an Einstein-frame theory containing a phantom dilaton, a canonical axion, a Maxwell field, and a Kaluza-Klein vector, with the couplings fixed by the higher-dimensional origin. Focusing on the Ellis-Bronnikov geometry, we construct solutions that incorporate both dyonic Maxwell and Kaluza-Klein fields. For exponential gauge couplings, the Einstein equations determine the scalar kinetic term and the combined potentials, while the remaining field equations reduce to algebraic relations fixing the individual potentials and the radial behaviour of the electric charges. We obtain a systematic classification of configurations, ranging from the pure phantom-supported wormhole to fully coupled dilaton-axion-gauge configurations. The Kaluza-Klein sector enriches the solution space with additional structure while preserving analytic tractability. These results show that regular, asymptotically flat traversable four-dimensional wormholes arise naturally from higher-dimensional scalar-tensor theories.

### [71] [Reevaluation of Inflationary Dynamics in Extended General Relativity with Perturbatively and Tensorially Structured Conformal Metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01619)
*Swapnil K. Singh,Saleh O. Allehabi,Azzah A. Alshehri,Mahmoud Nasar,Abdel Nasser Tawfik*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper reexamines the dynamics of cosmic inflation using a quantum-deformed conformal metric, providing analytical formulas for inflationary observables with quantum corrections. These corrections offer a physical interpretation and modify the observables while maintaining classical limits, suggesting potential quantum-gravitational structures in the early Universe.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cosmic inflation, an accelerated expansion phase in the early Universe, is driven by a nearly constant energy density, typically modeled through a slow-rolling scalar field. This model addresses several cosmological issues and generates primordial perturbations. However, significant questions remain about the nature of the inflaton, the origin of the potential, and the role of quantum gravity. The motivation is to address these questions by incorporating quantum-induced corrections into the inflationary dynamics.

宇宙膨胀是早期宇宙中一个加速扩张的阶段，由几乎恒定的能量密度驱动，通常通过缓慢滚动的标量场建模。该模型解决了几个宇宙学问题并产生了原初扰动。然而，关于膨胀子的本质、势能的起源以及量子引力的作用仍存在重要问题。本文的动机是通过将量子诱导修正纳入膨胀动力学来解决这些问题。

Method: The method involves employing a quantum-deformed conformal metric that is both perturbatively and tensorially structured and expanded. This approach allows for the reexamination of the dynamics of inflation and the computation of a range of inflationary observables, including scalar and tensor power spectra, their spectral tilts, runnings, and the tensor-to-scalar ratio, among other parameters, in the presence of quantum-induced corrections. The method provides a closed and internally consistent set of analytical formulas for these observables.

该方法采用一种既具有微扰结构又具有张量结构的量子变形共形度规。这种方法允许重新审视膨胀的动力学，并在量子诱导修正存在的情况下计算一系列膨胀可观测量，包括标量和张量功率谱、它们的谱倾斜、运行以及张量与标量比等其他参数。该方法为这些可观测量提供了一组封闭且内部一致的解析公式。

Result: The results include a set of analytical formulas for the scalar and tensor power spectra, along with their spectral tilts, runnings, and the tensor-to-scalar ratio, all computed in the presence of quantum-induced corrections. These quantum corrections provide a clear physical interpretation related to measure scaling and momentum-induced kinetic deformation, which facilitates modifications to the inflationary observables in a controlled and predictive manner. The results maintain the classical limits while offering a well-defined phenomenological perspective on potential quantum-gravitational structures in the early Universe.

结果包括一组在量子诱导修正存在下计算出的标量和张量功率谱及其谱倾斜、运行和张量与标量比的解析公式。这些量子修正提供了与度规缩放和动量诱导动能变形相关的清晰物理解释，这有助于以可控和可预测的方式修改膨胀可观测量。结果保持了经典极限，同时对早期宇宙中的潜在量子引力结构提供了明确的现象学视角。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the use of a quantum-deformed conformal metric enables the reexamination of inflationary dynamics and the derivation of analytical formulas for various inflationary observables, taking into account quantum-induced corrections. These corrections provide a physical interpretation and allow for modifications to the observables, thereby offering a new perspective on the potential role of quantum gravity in the early Universe. The results suggest that such an approach could be a promising avenue for further exploration of the quantum-gravitational structure of the early Universe.

研究得出结论，使用量子变形共形度规能够重新审视膨胀动力学，并推导出考虑量子诱导修正的各种膨胀可观测量的解析公式。这些修正提供了物理解释，并允许对可观测量进行修改，从而为早期宇宙中量子引力的潜在作用提供了新的视角。结果表明，这种途径可能是进一步探索早期宇宙量子引力结构的一个有前景的方向。

Abstract: Based on the conventional metric tensor and driven by a nearly constant energy density, cosmic inflation, characterized by a remarkably accelerated expansion, was proposed as an early epoch in the Universe. The energy density is typically modeled through a slow-rolling scalar field, whose potential energy dominates the dynamics. This mechanism addresses horizon, flatness, and relic problems, while also generating quantum fluctuations that are stretched to cosmological scales, leading to emergence of primordial curvatures and tensor perturbations. Despite its empirical success, significant questions remain regarding identity of the inflaton, origin of the potential, and role of quantum gravity. A quantum-deformed conformal metric that is both perturbatively and tensorially structured and expanded is employed to reexamine the dynamics of inflation, thus enabling the computation of a range of inflationary observables in presence of quantum-induced corrections. We have established a closed and internally consistent set of analytical formulas for scalar and tensor power spectra, including their spectral tilts, runnings, and the tensor-to-scalar ratio, among other parameters. The quantum corrections appear to provide a clear physical interpretation related to measure scaling and momentum-induced kinetic deformation, which facilitates modifications to the inflationary observables in a controlled and predictive manner. While maintaining the classical limits, these corrections provide a well-defined phenomenological perspective on potential quantum-gravitational structures in the early Universe.

### [72] [Shirokov and Shapiro Effects in the Hartle-Thorne Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01639)
*Anuar Idrissov,Kuantay Boshkayev,Serzhan Momynov,Hernando Quevedo,Daniya Utepova,Ainur Urazalina,Bagila Baitimbetova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the Shirokov and Shapiro effects in the Hartle-Thorne spacetime, considering the influence of rotation and quadrupole deformations. It uses geodesic deviation equations to analyze the oscillatory motion of test particles and compares the results with those from Lense-Thirring and Zipoy-Voorhees metrics. The study also examines the Shapiro time delay for two limiting configurations and performs a full numerical analysis without the weak-field approximation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how the rotation and quadrupole deformations of compact objects affect relativistic observables such as the Shirokov effect and the Shapiro time delay. The authors aim to provide a comprehensive analysis by comparing the results with different spacetime metrics and by performing a full numerical analysis without the weak-field approximation.

动机是理解致密天体的旋转和四极矩形变如何影响相对论可观测现象，例如Shirokov效应和Shapiro时间延迟。作者旨在通过比较不同时空度量的结果，并在不使用弱场近似的情况下进行全面数值分析，提供一个全面的分析。

Method: The method involves using the Hartle-Thorne spacetime, which describes the exterior gravitational field of slowly rotating, slightly deformed celestial objects. Geodesic deviation equations are employed to analyze the oscillatory motion of neighboring test particle trajectories. The combined impact of angular momentum $J$ and quadrupole moment $Q$ on the Shirokov effect is studied. Additionally, the Shapiro time delay is examined for two limiting configurations: (i) the Lense-Thirring frame-dragging case and (ii) the static quadrupolar case. A full numerical analysis is performed without the weak-field approximation.

方法涉及使用Hartle-Thorne时空，该时空描述了缓慢旋转、轻微变形的天体的外部引力场。采用测地线偏离方程来分析邻近测试粒子轨迹的振荡运动。研究了角动量$J$和四极矩$Q$对Shirokov效应的联合影响。此外，还针对两种极限构型检查了Shapiro时间延迟：(i) Lense-Thirring框架拖拽情况和(ii)静态四极矩情况。在没有弱场近似的情况下进行了完整的数值分析。

Result: The results show that the combined impact of angular momentum $J$ and quadrupole moment $Q$ affects the Shirokov effect, leading to consistent trends in the coupling between radial and azimuthal oscillations. For the Shapiro time delay, the effect persists for both positive and negative values of the angular momentum in the Lense-Thirring frame-dragging case. In the static quadrupolar case, more oblate sources produce a stronger gravitational time delay with increasing distance. The full numerical analysis without the weak-field approximation reveals mimicking effects produced by the quadrupole deformation and the angular momentum of the compact object.

结果表明，角动量$J$和四极矩$Q$的联合影响改变了Shirokov效应，导致径向和方位角振荡之间的耦合趋势一致。对于Shapiro时间延迟，在Lense-Thirring框架拖拽情况下，无论角动量取正值还是负值，效应都持续存在。在静态四极矩情况下，更扁平的源在距离增加时产生更强的引力时间延迟。在没有弱场近似的情况下进行的完整数值分析揭示了由四极矩形变和致密天体的角动量产生的模拟效应。

Conclusion: The deformation and rotation of compact objects significantly influence the relativistic observables in the surrounding spacetime. The study provides a detailed analysis of the Shirokov and Shapiro effects, showing how the angular momentum and quadrupole moment affect these phenomena. The full numerical analysis without the weak-field approximation highlights the importance of considering the exact spacetime geometry for accurate predictions of relativistic effects.

致密天体的形变和旋转显著影响周围时空中的相对论可观测现象。该研究详细分析了Shirokov效应和Shapiro时间延迟，展示了角动量和四极矩如何影响这些现象。在没有弱场近似的情况下进行的完整数值分析强调了考虑精确时空几何以准确预测相对论效应的重要性。

Abstract: We investigate the influence of rotation and quadrupole deformations of astrophysical compact objects on the Shirokov and Shapiro effects within the Hartle-Thorne spacetime, which describes the exterior gravitational field of slowly rotating, slightly deformed celestial objects. Using geodesic deviation equations, we analyze the oscillatory motion of neighboring test particle trajectories and show how the combined impact of angular momentum $J$ and quadrupole moment $Q$ affects the Shirokov effect. The results are compared with our previous analysis for the Lense-Thirring and Zipoy-Voorhees metrics, revealing consistent trends in the coupling between radial and azimuthal oscillations. For the Shapiro time delay, we examine two limiting configurations: (i) the Lense-Thirring frame-dragging case with $J^2=0$, $Q=0$ and $J\neq0$, where the effect persists for both positive and negative values of the angular momentum; and (ii) the static quadrupolar case with $J=0$ and $Q\neq0$, where more oblate sources produce a stronger gravitational time delay with increasing distance. We also study these effects in the Hartle-Thorne spacetime without employing the weak-field approximation, performing a full numerical analysis. In particular, we examine the mimicking effects produced by the quadrupole deformation and the angular momentum of the compact object. These results illustrate how the deformation and rotation of compact objects influence the relativistic observables in the surrounding spacetime.

</details>


### [73] [Axial $w$-modes of anisotropic neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01737)
*Sushovan Mondal*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the axial $w$-mode oscillations of anisotropic neutron stars using two realistic equations of state (BSk21 and SLy4) and two pressure anisotropy prescriptions (Horvat and Bowers-Liang). The frequencies and damping times of these modes are computed, showing a dependence on stellar mass, compactness, and the nature of anisotropy. Empirical expressions for the frequency and damping time as functions of compactness and anisotropy strength are provided.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study aims to understand the behavior of axial $w$-mode oscillations in anisotropic neutron stars, which can provide insights into the internal structure and stability of these stars. By using different equations of state and anisotropy prescriptions, the authors seek to explore how these factors influence the oscillation properties, specifically the frequencies and damping times of the $w$-modes.

该研究旨在了解各向异性中子星的轴向$w$-模式振荡的行为，这可以提供有关这些恒星内部结构和稳定性的见解。通过使用不同的状态方程和各向异性假设，作者希望探讨这些因素如何影响振荡特性，特别是$w$-模式的频率和阻尼时间。

Method: The authors construct stellar configurations using two realistic equations of state, BSk21 and SLy4, and apply two prescriptions for pressure anisotropy, the Horvat ansatz and the Bowers-Liang ansatz. They compute the axial $w$-mode frequencies by solving the linearized perturbation equations using a continued-fraction method. The damping times associated with the axial $w$-modes are also analyzed. Empirical expressions for the axial $w$-mode frequency and damping time as functions of stellar compactness and anisotropy strength are derived.

作者使用两种现实的状态方程（BSk21 和 SLy4）构建恒星构型，并应用两种压力各向异性假设（Horvat 假设和 Bowers-Liang 假设）。他们通过使用连分式方法求解线性化扰动方程来计算轴向 $w$-模式频率。还分析了与轴向 $w$-模式相关的阻尼时间。推导出轴向 $w$-模式频率和阻尼时间作为恒星紧致度和各向异性强度函数的经验表达式。

Result: For each fixed anisotropy strength, the axial $w$-mode frequency decreases monotonically with increasing stellar mass along the stable branch, and its magnitude depends on both the equation of state and the nature of the anisotropy. At low stellar masses, configurations with dominant radial pressure ($p_r > p_t$) exhibit higher frequencies than those with dominant tangential pressure, whereas at the upper end of the stable branch, this ordering is reversed. The axial $w$-mode frequency displays an approximately linear dependence on compactness, with anisotropy modifying both the slope and the intercept. The Bowers-Liang ansatz produces a wider spread in the frequency values compared to the Horvat ansatz. The damping times increase with stellar mass, with a rapid rise toward the upper end of the stable branch. At a fixed mass, increasing the tangential pressure relative to the radial pressure leads to shorter damping times, while configurations with dominant radial pressure exhibit longer damping times. The sensitivity of the damping time to anisotropy is more pronounced for more compact stars, and the Bowers-Liang ansatz yields systematically larger damping times than the Horvat ansatz.

对于每个固定的各向异性强度，沿稳定分支随着恒星质量的增加，轴向 $w$-模式频率单调递减，其大小取决于状态方程和各向异性的性质。在低恒星质量下，径向压力占主导的构型（$p_r > p_t$）比切向压力占主导的构型表现出更高的频率，而在稳定分支的高端，这种顺序被逆转。轴向 $w$-模式频率对紧致度显示出近似线性依赖关系，各向异性同时修改斜率和截距。Bowers-Liang 假设相比 Horvat 假设产生了更宽的频率分布。阻尼时间随恒星质量增加而增加，在稳定分支的高端迅速上升。在固定质量下，相对于径向压力增加切向压力会导致更短的阻尼时间，而径向压力占主导的构型则表现出更长的阻尼时间。阻尼时间对各向异性的敏感性在更紧致的恒星中更为明显，Bowers-Liang 假设系统地产生比 Horvat 假设更大的阻尼时间。

Conclusion: The axial $w$-mode oscillations of anisotropic neutron stars are significantly influenced by the equation of state, the nature of anisotropy, and the stellar compactness. The empirical expressions derived for the axial $w$-mode frequency and damping time as functions of compactness and anisotropy strength can be used to predict the behavior of these oscillations in different astrophysical scenarios. The results highlight the importance of considering anisotropy in the study of neutron star oscillations and provide a framework for further theoretical and observational investigations.

各向异性中子星的轴向 $w$-模式振荡受到状态方程、各向异性性质和恒星紧致度的显著影响。推导出的轴向 $w$-模式频率和阻尼时间作为紧致度和各向异性强度函数的经验表达式可用于预测不同天体物理场景中这些振荡的行为。结果强调了在中子星振荡研究中考虑各向异性的重要性，并为进一步的理论和观测研究提供了框架。

Abstract: We investigate the axial $w$-mode oscillations of anisotropic neutron stars. Stellar configurations are constructed using two realistic equations of state, BSk21 and SLy4, with two prescriptions for pressure anisotropy, the Horvat ansatz and the Bowers-Liang ansatz. The axial $w$-mode frequencies are computed by solving the linearized perturbation equations using a continued-fraction method. For each fixed anisotropy strength, the axial $w$-mode frequency decreases monotonically with increasing stellar mass along the stable branch, with its magnitude depending on both the equation of state and the nature of the anisotropy. At low stellar masses, configurations with dominant radial pressure ($p_r>p_t$) exhibit higher frequencies than those with dominant tangential pressure, whereas toward the upper end of the stable branch this ordering is reversed, and configurations with $p_t>p_r$ attain higher frequencies at the same mass. The axial $w$-mode frequency displays an approximately linear dependence on compactness, with anisotropy modifying both the slope and the intercept. The Bowers-Liang ansatz produces a wider spread in the frequency values compared to the Horvat ansatz. We also analyze the damping times associated with the axial $w$-modes and find that they increase with stellar mass, with a rapid rise toward the upper end of the stable branch. At a fixed mass, increasing the tangential pressure relative to the radial pressure leads to shorter damping times, while configurations with dominant radial pressure exhibit longer damping times. The sensitivity of the damping time to anisotropy is more pronounced for more compact stars, and the Bowers-Liang ansatz yields systematically larger damping times than the Horvat ansatz. Finally, we provide empirical expressions for the axial $w$-mode frequency and damping time as functions of stellar compactness and anisotropy strength.

### [74] [Polarization structure of gravitational waves in extended relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01802)
*Yaakov Friedman*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the polarization structure of gravitational waves in Extended Relativity (ER) using the deviation tensor. It provides a unified treatment for detector responses, including interferometric detectors and pulsar timing arrays (PTAs). The key finding is that the relative amplitudes of tensor, vector, and scalar contributions to the polarization are fixed by the source geometry, leading to a constrained family of polarization states and PTA correlation patterns.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of the paper is to explore the polarization structure of gravitational waves within the framework of Extended Relativity (ER) and to express the deviation tensor in a form that allows for a unified treatment of detector responses. This approach aims to provide a direct connection between the theoretical structure of ER and observable signatures, which can be crucial for understanding the nature of gravitational waves and their sources.

该论文的动机是在扩展相对论（ER）框架内探索引力波的极化结构，并将偏差张量表示成一种形式，从而允许统一处理探测器响应。这种方法旨在在ER的理论结构与可观测特征之间建立直接联系，这对于理解引力波及其源的性质至关重要。

Method: The method involves starting from the point-source solution to derive the radiation field of a compact binary in the wave zone. The deviation tensor is expressed such that its spacetime dependence is carried entirely by the retarded phase, with the tensorial coefficients depending only on the inclination angle of the source. For interferometric detectors, the signal is governed by the tidal matrix, which depends on second derivatives of the deviation tensor. For pulsar timing arrays (PTAs), the response follows from null geodesic propagation and reduces to boundary terms, with the observable determined by the projection $k^\mu k^\nu h_{\mu\nu}$ evaluated at the emission and reception points.

该方法从点源解开始，推导出波区内紧凑双星系统的辐射场。偏差张量被表示为：其时空依赖性完全由延迟相位携带，而张量系数仅依赖于源的倾角。对于干涉测量探测器，信号由潮汐矩阵控制，该矩阵依赖于偏差张量的二阶导数。对于脉冲星计时阵列（PTAs），响应遵循零测地线传播，并简化为边界项，可观测值由发射和接收点处的投影$k^\mu k^\nu h_{\mu\nu}$确定。

Result: The key result is that the polarization components are not independent; instead, the relative amplitudes of tensor, vector, and scalar contributions to the polarization are fixed by the source geometry. This leads to a constrained family of polarization states and corresponding PTA correlation patterns. The formulation provides a direct connection between the theoretical structure of ER and observable signatures, enabling a more comprehensive understanding of gravitational wave signals.

主要结果是极化分量不是独立的；相反，极化的张量、矢量和标量贡献的相对振幅是由源几何固定的。这导致了一组受约束的极化状态和相应的PTA相关模式。该公式提供了ER理论结构与可观测特征之间的直接联系，使我们能够更全面地理解引力波信号。

Conclusion: The conclusion drawn from the analysis is that the polarization structure of gravitational waves in Extended Relativity (ER) is characterized by a constrained family of polarization states, where the relative amplitudes of different polarization components are determined by the source geometry. This has implications for the interpretation of gravitational wave signals detected by various observatories, including interferometric detectors and pulsar timing arrays (PTAs).

分析得出的结论是，在扩展相对论（ER）中，引力波的极化结构具有一组受约束的极化状态，其中不同极化分量的相对振幅由源几何决定。这对包括干涉测量探测器和脉冲星计时阵列（PTAs）在内的各种天文台检测到的引力波信号的解释具有重要意义。

Abstract: We analyze the polarization structure of gravitational waves in the framework of Extended Relativity (ER), using the deviation tensor as the fundamental observable quantity. Starting from the point-source solution, we derive the radiation field of a compact binary in the wave zone and express the deviation tensor in a form in which the spacetime dependence is carried entirely by the retarded phase, while the tensorial coefficients depend only on the inclination angle of the source.
  This representation allows for a unified treatment of detector responses. For interferometric detectors, the signal is governed by the tidal matrix, which depends on second derivatives of the deviation tensor. For pulsar timing arrays (PTAs), the response follows from null geodesic propagation and reduces to boundary terms, so that the observable is determined by the projection $k^μk^νh_{μν}$ evaluated at the emission and reception points.
  A key result is that the polarization components are not independent: the relative amplitudes of tensor, vector, and scalar contributions are fixed by the source geometry. This leads to a constrained family of polarization states and corresponding PTA correlation patterns. The formulation provides a direct connection between the theoretical structure of ER and observable signatures.

TL;DR: The paper proposes a K-inflation framework with a field-dependent non-canonical kinetic term $G(φ)$ to reconcile $α$-attractor T-models and natural Inflation models with the latest observational constraints. It includes a refined calculation of the reheating equation-of-state parameter $w_{\rm re}$, avoids standard power-law approximations, and tests Swampland Distance and de Sitter Conjectures. The additional friction from the non-minimal kinetic coupling shifts both models into favored observational regions, with specific predictions for matter-like and stiff reheating, and gravitational-wave backgrounds.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent ACT data suggest a higher scalar spectral index $n_s$, which places models such as $α$-attractor T-models and natural Inflation in tension with current observations. The motivation is to propose a K-inflation framework that can reconcile these models with the latest Planck-ACT-LB-BK18 constraints while also testing their consistency with the Swampland Distance and de Sitter Conjectures.

最近的ACT数据表明标量谱指数$n_s$较高，这使得$α$-吸引子T模型和自然膨胀模型与当前观测结果存在张力。本文的动机是提出一个K-膨胀框架，该框架可以将这些模型与最新的Planck-ACT-LB-BK18约束相协调，并同时测试它们与Swampland距离和de Sitter猜想的一致性。

Method: The authors use a K-inflation framework with a field-dependent non-canonical kinetic term $G(φ)$. They perform a refined calculation of the reheating equation-of-state parameter $w_{\rm re}$, avoiding standard power-law approximations. Additionally, they test the consistency of the models with the Swampland Distance and de Sitter Conjectures. The method involves analyzing the effects of the non-minimal kinetic coupling on the inflationary dynamics and the resulting observational signatures, including the scalar spectral index $n_s$ and the tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$.

作者使用具有场依赖非规范动能项$G(φ)$的K-膨胀框架。他们对重热方程状态参数$w_{\rm re}$进行了精细计算，避免了标准幂律近似。此外，他们还测试了这些模型与Swampland距离和de Sitter猜想的一致性。该方法包括分析非最小动能耦合对膨胀动力学的影响以及由此产生的观测特征，包括标量谱指数$n_s$和张量-标量比$r$。

Result: The results show that the additional friction from the non-minimal kinetic coupling shifts both the $α$-attractor T-models and natural Inflation models into the favored observational regions. Abstract: Recent ACT data favor a higher scalar spectral index $n_s$, placing models such as $α$-attractor T-models and natural Inflation in tension with current observations. We propose a K-inflation framework with a field-dependent non-canonical kinetic term $G(φ)$ that reconciles these models with the latest Planck-ACT-LB-BK18 constraints. Our analysis includes a refined calculation of the reheating equation-of-state parameter $w_{\rm re}$, avoids standard power-law approximations, and tests consistency with the Swampland Distance and de Sitter Conjectures. We find that the additional friction from the non-minimal kinetic coupling shifts both models into the favored observational regions. For the $α$-attractor T-model with $n=2$, viable solutions occur for $β\sim \mathcal{O}(10)$, with Swampland consistency favoring $α\gtrsim \mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$. This case predicts matter-like reheating and a red-tilted gravitational-wave background that is unlikely to be detected soon. In contrast, natural Inflation with $n=4,5$ is compatible with CMB constraints for $α\lesssim 7,8$ and $β\lesssim -1$, respectively, leading to stiff reheating and a blue-tilted gravitational-wave background potentially observable by LISA, Cosmic Explorer, Einstein Telescope, DECIGO, and BBO while satisfying BBN and $ΔN_{\rm eff}$ bounds.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to provide a consistent matter source for a previously proposed effective metric by deriving it from a fundamental action. The authors aim to explore the properties of a black hole geometry supported by a magnetically charged NED field coupled to a scalar field, and to analyze its horizon structure, photon sphere, and thermodynamic behavior, including phase transitions and topological properties. Additionally, the paper seeks to connect these theoretical findings to observational constraints, such as those from the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT).

Method: The authors use a dimensional consistency approach to reduce the parameter space to a single magnetic charge. They employ an inverse construction formalism to derive a one-parameter family of electromagnetic Lagrangians, $\mathcal{L}(F)=F^{n+1}/(n+1)$, which includes both linear and nonlinear electrodynamics. The horizon structure, critical magnetic charge, and photon sphere are analyzed, and the shadow radius is computed. The solution's thermodynamic properties, including the first law and Smarr relation, are examined in the extended phase space, and the Hawking-Page phase transition is identified. Result: The analysis reveals that the black hole geometry can be either a black hole or a horizonless configuration, depending on the value of the magnetic charge. The critical magnetic charge separating these configurations is determined. The shadow radius of the photon sphere is calculated, and observational bounds from the EHT for Sagittarius A* constrain the allowed range of the magnetic charge. The solution satisfies the first law and Smarr relation in extended phase space thermodynamics and exhibits a Hawking-Page phase transition without van der Waals-type critical behavior. The topological properties show that the photon sphere carries a total topological charge $Q_{\text{tot}}=-1$, and the thermodynamic vector field has a global winding number $W=0$, indicating the same topological class as the Reissner-Nordström black hole.

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the non-minimal coupling framework provides a versatile theoretical support for the black hole geometry, allowing for the connection between theoretical solutions and observational settings within strong-field gravity. The results highlight the importance of the magnetic charge in determining the nature of the space-time and the topological properties of the solution, which are similar to those of the Reissner-Nordström black hole.

Abstract: We reconstruct a static and spherically symmetric black hole geometry originally proposed as an effective metric by identifying a consistent matter source derived from a fundamental action. The space-time is supported by a magnetically charged nonlinear electrodynamics (NED) field non-minimally coupled to a scalar field. Dimensional consistency reduces the parameter space to a single magnetic charge, and the inverse construction formalism yields a one-parameter family of electromagnetic Lagrangians $\mathcal{L}(F)=F^{n+1}/(n+1)$, encompassing both linear and nonlinear electrodynamics. We analyze the horizon structure and determine the critical magnetic charge separating black hole and horizonless configurations. The photon sphere and the corresponding shadow radius are computed, and observational bounds from the Event Horizon Telescope for Sagittarius A* constrain the allowed range of the magnetic charge. In the extended phase space thermodynamics, the solution satisfies the first law and the Smarr relation, exhibits a Hawking-Page phase transition, and presents a single change in stability without van der Waals-type critical behavior. We also investigate the topological properties of both the photon sphere and the thermodynamic parameter space. The photon sphere carries a total topological charge $Q_{\text{tot}}=-1$, while the thermodynamic vector field yields a global winding number $W=0$, placing the solution in the same topological class as the one of the Reissner-Nordström black hole. We finally discuss the versatility of this non-minimal coupling framework in both providing theoretical support to previously introduced solution and also to connect them to observational settings within strong-field gravity.

### [79] [The radiation zone in general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01951)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: The paper employs a theoretical approach to analyze the radiation zone in electrodynamics, focusing on the dominance of the $1/r$ component of the field over the $1/{r^2}$ piece. It then applies this understanding to address two specific problems in general relativity, using the equivalence principle and an examination of astrophysical versus man-made sources of gravitational waves.

Result: By applying the concept of the radiation zone, the paper elucidates why a static charge in a gravitational field does not actually radiate, thereby resolving the apparent paradox. Additionally, it explains the challenges in creating man-made sources of gravitational radiation, contrasting them with the naturally occurring astrophysical sources.

Conclusion: The radiation zone in electrodynamics, where the $1/r$ part of the field dominates, is crucial for understanding two puzzling aspects of general relativity: the apparent paradox of a static charge radiating in a gravitational field and the lack of man-made sources of gravitational radiation. This analysis provides a deeper insight into the interplay between electromagnetic and gravitational fields, highlighting the importance of the radiation zone concept in resolving these issues.

Abstract: The radiation zone in electrodynamics is the region far enough away from the charges that the $1/r$ part of the field dominates over the $1/{r^2}$ piece. This concept is key in explaining two puzzling aspects of general relativity: The first is an old paradox that invokes the equivalence principle to argue that a static charge in a gravitational field will radiate. The second is the fact that while there are astrophysical sources of gravitational radiation, we do not have any man-made sources.

### [81] [Pole Structure of Kerr Green's Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01964)
*Hayato Motohashi,Yuto Suichi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the pole structure of Kerr black-hole perturbations in the frequency domain, focusing on the Green's function for the radial Teukolsky equation. It establishes the Matsubara pole structure and identifies higher-order zero-frequency singularities, clarifying their role in the Teukolsky formalism and providing a foundation for understanding prompt response in time-domain ringdown waveforms.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the pole structure of Kerr black-hole perturbations in the frequency domain, particularly the Matsubara poles and zero-frequency singularities, within the Teukolsky formalism. This understanding is crucial for interpreting time-domain ringdown waveforms in Kerr spacetime.

动机是理解克尔黑洞扰动在频率域中的极点结构，特别是在Teukolsky形式主义中的Matsubara极点和零频奇点。这对于解释克尔时空中的时域振铃波形至关重要。

Method: The authors investigate the homogeneous radial solutions, connection coefficients, and the Green's function for the radial Teukolsky equation. They show that the homogeneous solutions and local connection coefficients develop simple poles at the Matsubara frequencies. They also identify higher-order zero-frequency singularities in the decomposed Green-function contributions, which cancel collectively in the total radial Green's function.

作者研究了径向Teukolsky方程的齐次径向解、连接系数和格林函数。他们表明，齐次解和局部连接系数在Matsubara频率处发展出简单极点。他们还识别了分解的格林函数贡献中的高阶零频奇点，这些奇点在总径向格林函数中集体抵消。

Result: The key results are the explicit establishment of the Matsubara pole structure within the Teukolsky formalism for asymptotically flat subextremal Kerr black holes and the identification of higher-order zero-frequency singularities in the decomposed Green-function contributions. These singularities scale as $ω^{-2l-1}$ and cancel collectively in the total radial Green's function.

主要结果是在渐近平坦次极端克尔黑洞的Teukolsky形式主义中明确建立了Matsubara极点结构，并识别了分解的格林函数贡献中的高阶零频奇点。这些奇点按$ω^{-2l-1}$缩放并在总径向格林函数中集体抵消。

Conclusion: The study clarifies how Matsubara poles and sectoral zero-frequency singularities arise in the Teukolsky formalism and provides a frequency-domain foundation for understanding prompt response in time-domain ringdown waveforms in Kerr spacetime. This work contributes to a deeper understanding of the mathematical structure underlying black hole perturbations.

该研究阐明了Matsubara极点和扇区零频奇点如何在Teukolsky形式主义中出现，并为理解克尔时空中的时域振铃波形的即时响应提供了频率域基础。这项工作有助于更深入地理解黑洞扰动背后的数学结构。

Abstract: We investigate the pole structure of Kerr black-hole perturbations in the frequency domain, focusing on the building blocks of the Green's function for the radial Teukolsky equation: the homogeneous radial solutions, the connection coefficients, and the Green's function itself. We show that the homogeneous solutions and the local connection coefficients develop simple poles at the Matsubara frequencies, thereby establishing the Matsubara pole structure explicitly within the Teukolsky formalism for asymptotically flat subextremal Kerr black holes. At the level of the local fixed-sector connection formula, the explicit Matsubara-pole factors cancel in the ratio of connection coefficients entering a decomposed Green-function contribution. We also identify higher-order zero-frequency singularities in the decomposed Green-function contributions, which scale as $ω^{-2l-1}$ and cancel collectively in the total radial Green's function. These results clarify how Matsubara poles and sectoral zero-frequency singularities arise in the Teukolsky formalism and provide a frequency-domain foundation for understanding prompt response in time-domain ringdown waveforms in Kerr spacetime.

### [82] [Ergosphere Geometry and Thermodynamic Properties of Boosted Kerr-Taub-NUT Solutions in Kaluza-Klein Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02000)
*Hasan Oguz,Goksel Daylan Esmer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores the effects of a Kaluza-Klein boost on the Kerr-Taub-NUT spacetime, leading to an Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton black hole. The study reveals that while the coordinate location of the stationary limit surface remains invariant, the physical ergoregion volume increases. The first law of black-hole thermodynamics is verified with both electric and magnetic Kaluza-Klein work terms. The results show a clear distinction between boost-invariant horizon thermodynamics and boost-dependent global geometric properties, highlighting the role of higher-dimensional momentum in rotating black hole spacetimes.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to investigate the impact of a Kaluza-Klein boost on the Kerr-Taub-NUT spacetime, specifically focusing on the resulting four-dimensional geometry and thermodynamics. The authors aim to understand how the boost affects the black hole's physical properties, such as the ergoregion volume and the first law of black-hole thermodynamics, and to distinguish between boost-invariant and boost-dependent properties.

本文的动机是研究Kaluza-Klein提升对Kerr-Taub-NUT时空的影响，特别是关注四维几何和热力学。作者旨在了解提升如何影响黑洞的物理属性，如能层体积和黑洞热力学第一定律，并区分提升不变和提升依赖的属性。

Method: The method involves applying a Kaluza-Klein boost to the Kerr-Taub-NUT spacetime and studying the resulting four-dimensional geometry and thermodynamics after dimensional reduction. The authors analyze the invariance of the stationary limit surface under the boost and the enlargement of the physical ergoregion. They also verify the first law of black-hole thermodynamics by including both electric and magnetic Kaluza-Klein work terms and distinguishing the seed mass parameter from the asymptotic ADM mass and the horizon Komar mass.

该方法包括将Kaluza-Klein提升应用于Kerr-Taub-NUT时空，并在维度约化后研究得到的四维几何和热力学。作者分析了静态极限面在提升下的不变性以及物理能层的扩大。他们还通过包含电性和磁性的Kaluza-Klein功项来验证黑洞热力学第一定律，并区分种子质量参数、渐近ADM质量和视界Komar质量。

Result: The results show that the coordinate location of the stationary limit surface, defined by the condition $g_{tt}=0$ in the Einstein frame, is invariant under the Kaluza-Klein boost. However, the physical ergoregion volume, measured by the proper spatial volume on constant-time hypersurfaces, significantly increases. The first law of black-hole thermodynamics is verified with both electric and magnetic Kaluza-Klein work terms, and a clear separation is established between boost-invariant horizon thermodynamics and boost-dependent global geometric properties. Higher-dimensional momentum enhances the effective inertial-frame rotation and ergoregion volume without changing the horizon radius, entropy, or temperature.

结果表明，在Einstein框架下由条件$g_{tt}=0$定义的静态极限面的坐标位置在Kaluza-Klein提升下保持不变。然而，通过常时间超曲面上的适当空间体积测量的物理能层体积显著增加。黑洞热力学第一定律通过电性和磁性的Kaluza-Klein功项得到了验证，并且建立了提升不变视界热力学和提升依赖全局几何属性之间的清晰分离。高维动量增强了有效惯性系旋转和能层体积，而不会改变视界半径、熵或温度。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the application of a Kaluza-Klein boost to the Kerr-Taub-NUT spacetime leads to an Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton black hole with distinct geometric and thermodynamic properties. The boost does not affect the horizon radius, entropy, or temperature but significantly enlarges the physical ergoregion volume and enhances the effective inertial-frame rotation. This provides a clean geometric signature of extra dimensions in rotating black hole spacetimes.

论文得出结论，将Kaluza-Klein提升应用于Kerr-Taub-NUT时空会导致具有独特几何和热力学特性的Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton黑洞。提升不会影响视界半径、熵或温度，但会显著增大物理能层体积并增强有效惯性系旋转。这为旋转黑洞时空中额外维度提供了清晰的几何特征。

Abstract: We investigate rotating black holes obtained by applying a Kaluza-Klein boost to the Kerr-Taub-NUT spacetime and study the resulting four-dimensional geometry and thermodynamics after dimensional reduction. The boost along the compact direction generates an Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton black hole in which the electric charge originates purely from higher-dimensional momentum rather than from an independent matter source.
  We demonstrate that the coordinate location of the stationary limit surface, defined by the condition $g_{tt}=0$ in the Einstein frame, is invariant under the Kaluza-Klein boost. Nevertheless, the boost induces a substantial enlargement of the \emph{physical} ergoregion, as measured by the proper spatial volume on constant-time hypersurfaces, through its modification of the induced spatial metric. We further verify the first law of black-hole thermodynamics with both the electric and magnetic Kaluza-Klein work terms included -- the latter being a genuinely dyonic feature generated by the interplay of the boost with the NUT charge -- and carefully distinguish the seed mass parameter from the asymptotic ADM mass and from the horizon Komar mass.
  Our results establish a clear separation between boost-invariant horizon thermodynamics and boost-dependent global geometric properties. In particular, higher-dimensional momentum enhances the effective inertial-frame rotation measured by ZAMOs and ergoregion volume without altering the horizon radius, entropy, or temperature, providing a clean geometric signature of extra dimensions in rotating black hole spacetimes.

### [83] [Gravitational baryogenesis in scalar-nonmetricity $f(Q,φ)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02008)
*F. Mavoa,M. C. Sow,M. G. Ganiou,C. S. Touré,C. R. Tefo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores gravitational baryogenesis in scalar-nonmetricity theories, specifically through two modified gravity models. The first model, $f(Q,φ)=Q+ξQ φ^2$, shows a monotonic decrease in the baryon-to-entropy ratio with increasing cosmic expansion parameter $γ$. The second model, $f(Q,φ)=αQ^n + βφQ$, achieves the correct order of magnitude for the baryon asymmetry within a physically reasonable parameter space. The results indicate that scalar-nonmetricity gravity is a viable framework for explaining the baryon asymmetry of the Universe.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to investigate the feasibility of generating the observed baryon asymmetry of the Universe within the framework of scalar-nonmetricity theories. By extending standard $f(Q)$ gravity with nonminimal couplings between the scalar field and the nonmetricity scalar, the authors aim to explore how these modifications can influence the cosmological dynamics and, in particular, the efficiency of baryogenesis. The goal is to determine if such models can naturally reproduce the observed baryon-to-entropy ratio without requiring fine-tuning of parameters.

本文的动机是研究在标量非度规理论框架内生成可观测宇宙重子不对称性的可行性。通过在标准$f(Q)$引力中引入标量场与非度规标量之间的非最小耦合，作者旨在探讨这些修改如何影响宇宙动力学，特别是重子生成的效率。目标是确定这些模型是否可以自然地重现观测到的重子与熵比，而无需对参数进行微调。

Method: The method involves analyzing two classes of modified gravity models: $f(Q,φ)=Q+ξQ φ^2$ and $f(Q,φ)=αQ^n + βφQ$. These models are extensions of $f(Q)$ gravity that include nonminimal couplings between the scalar field and the nonmetricity scalar. The authors analyze the evolution of the baryon-to-entropy ratio in terms of the cosmic expansion parameter $γ$, assuming a power-law behavior of the scale factor. For each model, the authors derive the baryon-to-entropy ratio as a function of the model parameters and compare it with observational constraints.

该方法涉及分析两类修正引力模型：$f(Q,φ)=Q+ξQ φ^2$ 和 $f(Q,φ)=αQ^n + βφQ$。这些模型是$f(Q)$引力的扩展，包括标量场与非度规标量之间的非最小耦合。作者假设尺度因子具有幂律行为，分析了重子与熵比随宇宙膨胀参数$γ$的变化。对于每个模型，作者推导出重子与熵比作为模型参数的函数，并将其与观测约束进行比较。

Result: For the first model, $f(Q,φ)=Q+ξQ φ^2$, the baryon-to-entropy ratio decreases monotonically with increasing $γ$, and the observed baryon asymmetry is reproduced for $γ\approx 0.2$--$0.3$ without fine-tuning. For the second model, $f(Q,φ)=αQ^n + βφQ$, the baryon asymmetry is achieved for physically reasonable values of $α\sim 10^{-3}$ to $10^{-2}$ and $β\sim 10^{-2}$ to $10^{-1}$. The results show that both models can successfully explain the baryon asymmetry of the Universe within their respective parameter spaces.

对于第一个模型 $f(Q,φ)=Q+ξQ φ^2$，重子与熵比随着$γ$的增加而单调减少，在$γ\approx 0.2$--$0.3$时，无需微调即可重现观测到的重子不对称性。对于第二个模型 $f(Q,φ)=αQ^n + βφQ$，当$α\sim 10^{-3}$ 到 $10^{-2}$ 和 $β\sim 10^{-2}$ 到 $10^{-1}$ 时，可以实现重子不对称性。结果表明，这两个模型在其各自的参数空间内都能成功解释宇宙的重子不对称性。

Conclusion: The study concludes that scalar-nonmetricity gravity provides a viable and robust framework for explaining the origin of the baryon asymmetry of the Universe. The interplay between nonlinear geometric terms and scalar field couplings plays a crucial role in controlling the baryogenesis mechanism. The results suggest that the observed baryon asymmetry can be naturally explained within these models without the need for fine-tuning, opening new perspectives in the study of modified gravity and early Universe cosmology.

研究表明，标量非度规引力为解释宇宙重子不对称性的起源提供了一个可行且稳健的框架。非线性几何项与标量场耦合之间的相互作用在控制重子生成机制中起着关键作用。结果表明，这些模型可以在不需微调的情况下自然解释观测到的重子不对称性，为研究修正引力和早期宇宙宇宙学开辟了新的视角。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate gravitational baryogenesis in the framework of scalar-nonmetricity theories by considering two classes of modified gravity models, namely $f(Q,φ)=Q+ξQ φ^2$ and $f(Q,φ)=αQ^n + βφQ$. These models extend standard $f(Q)$ gravity through the inclusion of nonminimal couplings between the scalar field and the nonmetricity scalar, leading to nontrivial modifications of the cosmological dynamics. We analyze the evolution of the baryon-to-entropy ratio in terms of the cosmic expansion parameter $γ$, assuming a power-law behavior of the scale factor. For the first model, we show that the baryon-to-entropy ratio decreases monotonically with increasing $γ$, reflecting the impact of the expansion rate on the efficiency of baryogenesis. The observed baryon asymmetry, of order $10^{-11}$ to $10^{-10}$, is successfully reproduced for $γ\approx 0.2$--$0.3$ without requiring fine-tuning of the model parameters. For the second model, we explore the parameter space of $α$ and $β$, and demonstrate that the correct order of magnitude of the baryon asymmetry can be achieved for physically reasonable values of the parameters. In particular, we find that the baryon-to-entropy ratio lies within observational bounds for $α\sim 10^{-3}$ to $10^{-2}$ and $β\sim 10^{-2}$ to $10^{-1}$, with specific combinations yielding excellent agreement with observations. Overall, our results show that scalar-nonmetricity gravity provides a viable and robust framework for explaining the origin of the baryon asymmetry of the Universe. The interplay between nonlinear geometric terms and scalar field couplings plays a crucial role in controlling the baryogenesis mechanism, opening new perspectives in the study of modified gravity and early Universe cosmology.

### [84] [Non-variational scalar field cosmology: Exact Bianchi I solutions for near-minimal scalar fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02078)
*Joshua Ritchie*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates the exact Bianchi I solutions of the Einstein equations coupled to a non-variational 'near-minimal' scalar field, demonstrating a variety of cosmological phenomena including Big Bang, Big Crunch, and Big Rip singularities, as well as cyclic behavior. The stability analysis against spatially inhomogeneous perturbations shows that oscillatory and crushing singularity solutions are unstable, while Big Rip singularity solutions are stable.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the effects of a non-variational 'near-minimal' scalar field on the cosmological solutions of the Einstein equations, by decoupling the scalar field's self-interaction term from the derivative of its potential. This approach allows for the derivation of new exact solutions and the examination of their stability under perturbations.

动机是探索非变分“近极小”标量场对爱因斯坦方程宇宙学解的影响，通过将标量场的自相互作用项与其势的导数解耦。这种方法允许推导出新的精确解，并检查它们在扰动下的稳定性。

Method: The method involves assuming a quadratic potential and a self-interaction term proportional to the potential, leading to the derivation of four new exact Bianchi I solutions. A numerical stability analysis is then performed to assess the stability of these solutions against spatially inhomogeneous perturbations of the mean curvature.

方法包括假设二次势和与势成比例的自相互作用项，从而推导出四个新的精确Bianchi I解。然后进行数值稳定性分析，以评估这些解在平均曲率的空间不均匀扰动下的稳定性。

Result: The results include the derivation of four new exact Bianchi I solutions, which exhibit a range of cosmological phenomena such as Big Bang, Big Crunch, and Big Rip singularities, as well as oscillatory (cyclic) behavior. The stability analysis reveals that the oscillatory and crushing singularity solutions are unstable, whereas the Big Rip singularity solutions are stable to spatially inhomogeneous perturbations.

结果包括推导出四个新的精确Bianchi I解，这些解表现出一系列宇宙学现象，如大爆炸、大挤压和大撕裂奇点，以及振荡（循环）行为。稳定性分析表明，振荡和挤压奇点解是不稳定的，而大撕裂奇点解在空间不均匀扰动下是稳定的。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the non-variational 'near-minimal' scalar field coupling model can lead to a diverse set of cosmological solutions with interesting properties, such as infinite proper time singularities and cyclic behavior. However, only the Big Rip singularity solutions are stable to spatially inhomogeneous perturbations, indicating that they may be more physically relevant in this context.

结论是非变分“近极小”标量场耦合模型可以导致具有一系列有趣性质的宇宙学解，如无限固有时奇点和循环行为。然而，只有大撕裂奇点解在空间不均匀扰动下是稳定的，这表明在这种情况下它们可能具有更大的物理相关性。

Abstract: The purpose of this work is to investigate spatially homogeneous and flat cosmological solutions of the Einstein equations coupled to a non-variational ``near-minimal'' scalar field. This coupling model represents a minimal departure from standard theory by decoupling the scalar field's self-interaction term from the derivative of its potential. By assuming a quadratic potential and a self-interaction term that is proportional to the potential, we derive four new exact Bianchi I solutions. We demonstrate that these solutions produce a diverse range of cosmological phenomena, including Big Bang, Big Crunch, and Big Rip singularities, as well as oscillatory (``cyclic'') behaviour. For our exact solutions, these singularities occur in infinite proper time and hence are never truly reachable by an observer. To assess the stability of these cosmologies, we perform a numerical stability analysis against spatially inhomogeneous perturbations of the mean curvature. We find that the oscillatory solution is unstable to perturbations of this type, as are solutions in possession of a crushing singularity. Conversely, solutions with a Big Rip singularity (at infinity) are stable to spatially inhomogeneous perturbations of the mean curvature.
