### [85] [Spinning charged test particle dynamics around a Schwarzschild black hole embedded in a homogeneous magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02084)
*Misbah Shahzadi,Martin Kolos,Ondrej Zelenka,Georgios Lukes-Gerakopoulos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the motion of spinning charged test particles around a Schwarzschild black hole in a uniform magnetic field, focusing on the interplay between spin-curvature and electromagnetic interactions. It provides analytical expressions for conserved quantities and effective potentials in the equatorial plane, while off-equatorial dynamics are studied using numerical methods and show chaotic behavior under certain conditions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study aims to understand the complex dynamics of spinning charged test particles in the vicinity of a Schwarzschild black hole immersed in a uniform magnetic field. This setup is relevant for modeling particle motion in magnetized astrophysical environments near compact objects, where both spin-curvature coupling and electromagnetic interactions can significantly influence the trajectories. The goal is to provide a comprehensive analysis that distinguishes the contributions of these interactions to the overall dynamics.

该研究旨在理解在浸没于均匀磁场中的Schwarzschild黑洞附近的带电自旋测试粒子的复杂动力学。这种设置对于建模靠近紧致天体的磁化天体物理环境中的粒子运动是相关的，在这种环境中，自旋-曲率耦合和电磁相互作用都可以显著影响轨迹。目标是提供一个全面的分析，以区分这些相互作用对整体动力学的贡献。

Method: The authors use a combination of analytical and numerical techniques. For the equatorial plane, they derive analytical expressions for conserved energy, angular momentum, radial and orbital frequencies, as well as the effective potential. These expressions are functions of the spin parameter and magnetic field strength. For off-equatorial configurations, the system is non-integrable, and the authors employ numerical methods, including four-dimensional Poincaré surface sections (PSs) and recurrence analysis, to investigate the phase space and identify chaotic behavior.

作者使用了分析和数值技术的组合。对于赤道平面，他们推导出守恒能量、角动量、径向和轨道频率以及有效势的解析表达式。这些表达式是自旋参数和磁场强度的函数。对于非赤道构型，系统是非可积的，作者采用数值方法，包括四维Poincaré截面(PS)和回归分析，来研究相空间并识别混沌行为。

Result: In the equatorial plane, the authors find that the motion remains integrable with conserved quantities associated with spacetime symmetries and the alignment of the magnetic field. Analytical expressions for the conserved energy, angular momentum, and frequencies are derived. Off-equatorial motion, however, shows a more complex, non-integrable dynamical system, and the analysis reveals the presence of chaotic behavior for specific parameter values and initial conditions. The phase space is explored using four-dimensional PSs and recurrence analysis.

在赤道平面上，作者发现运动保持可积性，与时空对称性和磁场对齐相关的守恒量。推导出了守恒能量、角动量和频率的解析表达式。然而，非赤道运动显示出更复杂的非可积动力系统，并且分析揭示了在特定参数值和初始条件下存在混沌行为。使用四维Poincaré截面(PS)和回归分析探索了相空间。

Conclusion: The paper concludes by comparing the dynamics of spinning charged test particles with the limiting cases of spinning neutral and non-spinning charged particles. The results highlight the distinct contributions of spin-curvature and electromagnetic interactions to the overall dynamics, particularly in the context of chaotic behavior observed in off-equatorial motion. The study provides a deeper understanding of the interplay between these fundamental forces in the vicinity of compact objects.

论文通过比较带电自旋测试粒子的动力学与自旋中性粒子和非自旋带电粒子的极限情况得出结论。结果突出了自旋-曲率和电磁相互作用对整体动力学的不同贡献，特别是在观察到非赤道运动中的混沌行为的情况下。该研究提供了对这些基本力在紧致天体附近相互作用的更深入理解。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of spinning charged test particles orbiting a Schwarzschild black hole immersed in a test uniform magnetic field. This setup provides a simple but physically relevant framework for modeling particle motion in magnetized astrophysical environments near compact objects, where both spin-curvature coupling and electromagnetic interactions can play a significant role. The particle trajectories are obtained numerically in both equatorial and off-equatorial configurations, allowing us to examine the influence of spin-curvature and Lorentz forces on the motion. In the equatorial plane, assuming the particle's spin vector is orthogonal to the orbital plane, we derive analytical expressions for the conserved energy and angular momentum, as well as for the radial and orbital frequencies as functions of spin parameter and magnetic parameter. We also construct the corresponding effective potential to determine the allowed regions of particle motion. The equatorial dynamics remain integrable due to the existence of conserved quantities associated with the spacetime symmetries and the alignment of the magnetic field. In contrast, the off-equatorial motion constitutes a non-integrable dynamical system. While limiting subcases of the system, i.e., the spinning neutral and non-spinning charged cases, can be analyzed using two-dimensional Poincaré surface of sections (PSs), the combined system can be reduced only up to three degrees of freedom. Hence, to investigate the resulting complexity, we analyze the phase space using four-dimensional PS along with recurrence analysis, revealing the presence of chaotic behavior for particular choices of parameters and initial conditions. Finally, we compare the dynamics of spinning charged test particles with the limiting cases, thereby distinguishing the respective contributions of spin-curvature and electromagnetic interactions.

</details>


### [86] [Helicity-dependent corrections to black-hole shadows from the gravitational spin Hall effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02136)
*C. A. S. Almeida*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores the subleading-order effects on black-hole shadows, showing that the gravitational spin Hall effect of light causes polarized radiation with opposite helicities to trace different shadow boundaries. The correction is universal, scales as $1/ω$, and depends on a geometric function at the photon-sphere radius. The effect is confirmed numerically and extended to Reissner-Nordström and slowly rotating Kerr black holes, where frame dragging can modulate and even reverse the shadow splitting.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation of this paper is to investigate the influence of the gravitational spin Hall effect on the boundary of black-hole shadows, which was previously considered purely geometric in the leading-order approximation. The authors aim to show that the polarization of the probing radiation does affect the shadow's boundary, even in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes.

本文的动机是研究引力自旋霍尔效应对黑洞阴影边界的影响，而在此前的几何光学近似中，黑洞阴影被认为是纯粹几何的。作者旨在展示探测辐射的极化确实会影响阴影的边界，即使在静态、球对称时空也是如此。

Method: The authors derive the corrections to the critical impact parameter using the spin Hall equations of motion, which are then confirmed through numerical ray-tracing calculations. They extend their analysis to include Reissner-Nordström black holes and develop a perturbative treatment for slowly rotating (Kerr) spacetimes. The perturbative approach reveals how frame dragging affects the shadow splitting, introducing a $\cos\varphi$ modulation.

作者使用自旋霍尔运动方程推导了临界撞击参数的修正，并通过数值光线追踪计算进行了验证。他们将分析扩展到Reissner-Nordström黑洞，并为缓慢旋转（Kerr）时空开发了一种微扰处理方法。微扰方法揭示了框架拖拽如何影响阴影分裂，引入了$\cos\varphi$调制。

Result: The results show that the gravitational spin Hall effect shifts the critical impact parameter by a helicity-dependent amount, causing polarized radiation with opposite helicities to trace slightly different shadow boundaries. The correction is universal and scales as $1/ω$. For Reissner-Nordström black holes, the effect is amplified by up to a factor of $2.5$ at extremality. In slowly rotating Kerr spacetimes, frame dragging introduces a $\cos\varphi$ modulation of the shadow splitting, which can reverse its sign for spins $χ\gtrsim 0.21$.

结果显示，引力自旋霍尔效应使临界撞击参数发生了依赖于螺旋性的偏移，导致具有相反螺旋性的极化辐射会描绘出略有不同的阴影边界。修正项是普遍的，并且按$1/ω$缩放。对于Reissner-Nordström黑洞，在极端情况下，这种效应最多可以放大$2.5$倍。在缓慢旋转的Kerr时空中，框架拖拽引入了$\cos\varphi$调制，这可以在自旋$χ\gtrsim 0.21$时反转阴影分裂的符号。

Conclusion: The conclusion of the paper is that black-hole shadows are not purely geometric observables. The gravitational spin Hall effect of light introduces a helicity-dependent shift in the critical impact parameter, leading to different shadow boundaries for polarized radiation with opposite helicities. This effect, while small, has significant conceptual implications for the understanding of black-hole shadows and the information they carry about the polarization of the probing radiation.

本文的结论是，黑洞阴影并不是纯粹的几何可观测量。光的引力自旋霍尔效应引入了依赖于螺旋性的临界撞击参数偏移，导致具有相反螺旋性的极化辐射会有不同的阴影边界。尽管这种效应很小，但它对理解黑洞阴影及其携带的探测辐射极化信息具有重要的概念意义。

Abstract: Black-hole shadows are purely geometric in the leading-order geometric-optics approximation: their boundary is set by null geodesics and carries no information about the polarization of the probing radiation. This changes at subleading order. We show that the gravitational spin Hall effect of light shifts the critical impact parameter governing photon capture by a helicity-dependent amount, causing polarized radiation with opposite helicities to trace slightly different shadow boundaries -- even in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes. The correction is analytic, universal, and scales as $1/ω$: it depends only on a single geometric function evaluated at the photon-sphere radius. We derive this result from the spin Hall equations of motion, confirm it numerically through ray-tracing calculations, and extend the analysis to Reissner-Nordström black holes, where electric charge amplifies the effect by up to a factor of $2.5$ at extremality. We further develop a perturbative treatment for slowly rotating (Kerr) spacetimes, showing that frame dragging introduces a $\cos\varphi$ modulation of the shadow splitting that can reverse its sign on one side of the image for spins $χ\gtrsim 0.21$. Although the magnitude of the effect is small, the conceptual implication is clear: black-hole shadows are not purely geometric observables.

### [87] [Bondi and Novikov-Thorne accretion in regular black holes and Simpson-Visser spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02425)
*Serena Gambino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper compares the Bondi spherical accretion model and the Novikov-Thorne thin disc formalism around regular black holes and Simpson-Visser spacetimes, using various equations of state. The Bondi model is more sensitive to changes in spacetime geometry and the equation of state, making it better for distinguishing between regular and classical solutions. For Simpson-Visser solutions, increasing the regularization parameter $\ell$ shifts critical point positions, while the charge $Q$ has a lesser effect.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore how different accretion models (Bondi and Novikov-Thorne) respond to variations in spacetime geometry and fluid properties, particularly around regular black holes and Simpson-Visser spacetimes. This comparison aims to understand which model is more effective in distinguishing between regular and classical black hole solutions, and how the parameters $\ell$ and $Q$ influence the critical points in these models.

动机是探索不同的吸积模型（邦迪和诺维科夫-索恩）如何响应时空几何和流体性质的变化，特别是在规则黑洞和辛普森-维瑟时空周围。这种比较旨在了解哪种模型在区分规则和经典黑洞解方面更有效，以及参数$\ell$和$Q$如何影响这些模型中的临界点。

Method: The authors use the Bondi spherical accretion model and the Novikov-Thorne thin disc formalism to analyze the behavior of accreting fluids around regular black holes and Simpson-Visser spacetimes. They employ several equations of state for the accreting fluids and vary the parameters $\ell$ and $Q$ to observe their effects on the critical points.

作者使用邦迪球形吸积模型和诺维科夫-索恩薄盘形式来分析规则黑洞和辛普森-维瑟时空周围的吸积流体的行为。他们采用了多种状态方程来描述吸积流体，并改变参数$\ell$和$Q$以观察它们对临界点的影响。

Result: The Bondi model is found to be significantly more sensitive to the spacetime geometry and the equation of state, making it more effective at distinguishing between regular and classical solutions. For Simpson-Visser solutions, increasing the regularization parameter $\ell$ causes the critical points to shift both inward and outward. However, the charged Simpson-Visser extension, characterized by the charge $Q$, does not produce an effect as significant as that of $\ell$.

结果表明，邦迪模型对时空几何和状态方程的敏感性显著更高，使其在区分规则和经典解方面更为有效。对于辛普森-维瑟解，增加正则化参数$\ell$会导致临界点向内和向外移动。然而，由电荷$Q$表征的带电辛普森-维瑟扩展并没有产生与$\ell$相同程度的影响。

Conclusion: The study concludes that the Bondi spherical accretion model is more effective in distinguishing between regular and classical black hole solutions due to its higher sensitivity to spacetime geometry and the equation of state. The regularization parameter $\ell$ in Simpson-Visser spacetimes has a significant impact on the critical points, while the charge $Q$ has a lesser effect. These findings provide insights into the behavior of accreting fluids around different types of black holes and the role of specific parameters in these systems.

研究得出结论，由于邦迪球形吸积模型对时空几何和状态方程的敏感性更高，因此在区分规则和经典黑洞解方面更为有效。辛普森-维瑟时空中的正则化参数$\ell$对临界点有显著影响，而电荷$Q$的影响较小。这些发现为不同类型的黑洞周围吸积流体的行为以及这些系统中特定参数的作用提供了见解。

Abstract: We compare the Bondi spherical accretion model and the Novikov-Thorne thin disc formalism around regular black holes and Simpson-Visser spacetimes, using several equations of state for the accreting fluids. The Bondi model is significantly more sensitive to spacetime geometry and the equation of state, making it more effective at distinguishing between regular and classical solutions. For the Simpson-Visser solutions, however, increasing the regularisation parameter, $\ell$, shifts critical point positions both inward and outward. However, the charged Simpson-Visser extension, modeled by the charge $Q$, does not produce an effect comparable to that of $\ell$.

*Phuwadon Chunaksorn,Ratchaphat Nakarachinda,Pitayuth Wongjun*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper explores the thermodynamics of Reissner-Nordström black holes using Tsallis non-extensive statistical mechanics, revealing a $q$-generalized entropy and Van der Waals-like phase transitions. It also establishes an optical-thermodynamic correspondence, suggesting potential observational probes in future experiments.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to investigate how non-extensive statistical mechanics, which accounts for long-range gravitational correlations through the parameter $q$, can be applied to black hole thermodynamics. The goal is to understand the resulting thermodynamic behavior and its connection with astrophysical optics.

Method: The method involves applying Tsallis non-extensive statistical mechanics to a near-horizon photon-gas model of Reissner-Nordström black holes. A $q$-generalized entropy is derived, and the thermodynamic properties are analyzed, including phase transitions. Additionally, an optical-thermodynamic correspondence is established by mapping photon-sphere observables to thermodynamic quantities.

Result: The results show that the $q$-generalized entropy is consistent with the area law and leads to three branches of black hole solutions (small, intermediate, and large) with Van der Waals-like phase transitions. The optical-thermodynamic correspondence reveals that photon-sphere observables, such as orbital periods and Lyapunov exponents, can qualitatively reproduce the thermodynamic phase structure.

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the framework of Tsallis non-extensive statistical mechanics provides a new perspective on black hole thermodynamics, connecting non-extensive entropy, phase transitions, and astrophysical optics. This approach may offer potential observational probes for future interferometric experiments.

Abstract: We investigate black hole thermodynamics within Tsallis non-extensive statistical mechanics using a near-horizon photon-gas model. We derive a $q$-generalized entropy for Reissner--Nordström black holes that is consistent with the area law while incorporating long-range gravitational correlations via the non-extensivity parameter $q$. The resulting thermodynamics exhibits three branches (small, intermediate, and large black holes) with Van der Waals-like phase transitions characterized by mean-field critical exponents. Furthermore, we demonstrate an optical--thermodynamic correspondence by mapping photon-sphere observables, such as orbital periods and Lyapunov exponents, to thermodynamic quantities. The optical signatures qualitatively reproduce the thermodynamic phase structure, suggesting potential observational probes in future interferometric experiments. This framework connects non-extensive entropy, phase transitions, and astrophysical optics, providing a new perspective on strong-gravity thermodynamics.

### [89] [Testing General Relativity Through Gravitational Wave Classification: A Convolutional Neural Network Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02453)
*Lavinia Heisenberg,Shayan Hemmatyar,Hector Villarrubia-Rojo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: A machine learning framework is developed to test general relativity (GR) using gravitational wave signals from binary black hole mergers. The study introduces a response function formalism and uses convolutional neural networks (CNNs) on different input representations, achieving improved classification sensitivity. The framework is extended to physically motivated theories, such as massive gravity, where deviations are detected for specific graviton masses.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a robust method for testing the validity of general relativity (GR) by analyzing gravitational wave signals from binary black hole (BBH) mergers. By introducing a systematic framework that can quantify the response of observables to modifications of GR, the authors aim to improve the sensitivity of detecting potential deviations from GR, which could be indicative of new physics beyond the standard model.

动机是通过分析来自双黑洞（BBH）合并的引力波信号，开发一种测试广义相对论（GR）有效性的稳健方法。通过引入一个可以量化可观测量对GR修改响应的系统框架，作者旨在提高检测潜在偏离GR的灵敏度，这可能表明标准模型之外的新物理。

Method: The method involves generating simulated GR waveforms and constructing beyond-GR (BGR) waveforms with controlled phase deformations. A response function formalism is introduced to quantify how any observable responds to GR modifications. Convolutional neural networks (CNNs) are trained on two types of input: whitened waveforms and a response function type observable derived from waveform mismatch. The performance of the CNNs is compared against single feature classifiers, and the framework is extended to the parameterized post-Einsteinian (ppE) formalism to study physically motivated theories like massive gravity.

该方法涉及生成模拟的GR波形，并通过受控相位变形构建超越GR（BGR）的波形。引入了响应函数形式来量化任何可观测量对GR修改的响应。卷积神经网络（CNNs）在两种类型的输入上进行训练：白化波形和从波形失配中得出的响应函数类型可观测量。CNNs的表现与单特征分类器进行了比较，并且该框架扩展到了参数化后爱因斯坦（ppE）形式，以研究像大质量引力这样的物理动机理论。

Result: Using the response function as the CNN input improves the classification sensitivity by a factor of approximately 33 compared to whitened waveforms. The CNN outperforms the best single feature approach at all deformation scales. In the context of massive gravity, the classifier detects deviations for graviton masses of order $m_g \sim 10^{-23}\;\mathrm{eV}/c^2$ with aLIGO design sensitivity.

使用响应函数作为CNN输入比使用白化波形提高了大约33倍的分类灵敏度。在所有变形尺度下，CNN的表现优于最佳单特征方法。在大质量引力的背景下，分类器能够检测到量级为$m_g \sim 10^{-23}\;\mathrm{eV}/c^2$的引力子质量的偏差，具有aLIGO设计灵敏度。

Conclusion: The machine learning framework, particularly the use of response functions as inputs to CNNs, significantly enhances the sensitivity in detecting deviations from GR. This approach not only outperforms traditional methods but also provides a powerful tool for probing new physics beyond GR. The application to massive gravity demonstrates the practical utility of this method in exploring specific beyond-GR scenarios.

机器学习框架，特别是使用响应函数作为CNN的输入，显著增强了检测偏离GR的灵敏度。这种方法不仅优于传统方法，而且还提供了一个强大的工具来探测超出GR的新物理。应用于大质量引力展示了该方法在探索特定超出GR场景中的实际效用。

Abstract: We present a machine learning framework for testing general relativity (GR) with gravitational wave signals from binary black hole mergers. Using the source parameters of 173 BBH events from the GWTC catalog as a realistic astrophysical population, we generate simulated GR waveforms and construct beyond GR (BGR) waveforms by applying controlled phase deformations. We introduce a response function formalism that provides a systematic framework for quantifying how any observable responds to modifications of GR. We train convolutional neural networks (CNNs) on two input representations: whitened waveforms and a response function type observable derived from the waveform mismatch, which isolates the effect of phase deviations from the bulk signal. Using response functions as the CNN input improves the classification sensitivity by a factor of approximately 33 compared to whitened waveforms, demonstrating that the choice of observable representation is as important as the classifier architecture. We study the fundamental limits of this classification through Bayes optimal error analysis, averaging methods that reveal coherent patterns hidden in noise, and a comparison between CNN accuracy and a single feature classifier as a proxy for human performance. At all deformation scales, the CNN outperforms the best single feature approach. We extend the framework to physically motivated theories using the parameterized post Einsteinian (ppE) formalism and apply it to massive gravity, where the classifier detects deviations for graviton masses of order $m_g \sim 10^{-23}\;\mathrm{eV}/c^2$ with aLIGO design sensitivity.

### [91] [Exact solutions for slowly rotating wormholes in the presence of an anisotropic fluid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02555)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

This work aims to provide a more realistic and detailed description of wormholes, considering their rotation and the effects of anisotropic matter.

The results offer new insights into the behavior of these exotic objects and their potential observable signatures.

Abstract: We construct slowly rotating traversable wormholes in the presence of an anisotropic fluid. Starting from a Teo-type stationary, axisymmetric extension of the Morris-Thorne metric, we perform a slow-rotation expansion, fix a gauge that preserves the geometric meaning of the radial coordinate, and introduce two complementary prescriptions for treating the throat (fixed and free). Within this framework, the Einstein equations and conservation laws form a closed system, from which we obtain analytic expressions for the leading frame dragging and for the second-order rotational backreaction. We apply the construction to the spatial-Schwarzschild and Morris-Thorne wormholes, derive the induced corrections to the stress-energy tensor, analyse the redistribution of null energy condition (NEC) violations, and characterise quadrupolar deformations, curvature diagnostics, and possible ergoregions.

### [92] [Axial tidal Love numbers of black holes in matter environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02633)
*Simone D'Onofrio,Sayak Datta,Andrea Maselli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates the axial (magnetic) tidal Love numbers of a Schwarzschild black hole surrounded by anisotropic fluids, representing dark matter. The authors use both a small-compactness expansion and numerical integration to compute these Love numbers for various density profiles. They find that density profiles without compact support produce logarithmic terms in the perturbation variable, complicating the standard tidal matching procedure. This work emphasizes the importance of the asymptotic structure of the matter distribution in defining tidal observables for black holes with surrounding matter.

本文研究了被各向异性流体（代表暗物质）包围的史瓦西黑洞的轴向（磁性）潮汐Love数。作者使用小致密性展开和数值积分两种方法来计算不同密度分布下的这些Love数。他们发现，没有紧支撑的密度分布会在扰动变量的渐近展开中产生对数项，从而复杂化标准的潮汐匹配过程。这项工作强调了在定义带有周围物质的黑洞的潮汐可观测量时，物质分布的渐近结构的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the response of a Schwarzschild black hole to external tidal fields when it is surrounded by a spherically symmetric matter distribution, such as dark matter. The study aims to provide a general framework for computing the axial tidal Love numbers, which are essential for understanding the gravitational interactions between the black hole and its environment. The authors also aim to highlight the importance of the asymptotic behavior of the matter distribution in the context of tidal deformations.

动机是理解当史瓦西黑洞被球对称物质分布（如暗物质）包围时，它对外部潮汐场的响应。研究旨在提供一个通用框架来计算轴向潮汐Love数，这对于理解黑洞与其环境之间的引力相互作用至关重要。作者还旨在强调在潮汐形变背景下物质分布的渐近行为的重要性。

Method: The authors employ two complementary methods: a small-compactness expansion, which provides closed-form analytic expressions, and direct numerical integration of the perturbation equations. They specialize in the case of anisotropic fluids as a proxy for dark matter distributions, and they compute the Love numbers for different astrophysically relevant density profiles. The authors also discuss the connection between different formulations of fluid perturbations and the resulting Love numbers, and they analyze the impact of the asymptotic structure of the matter distribution on the tidal matching procedure.

作者采用了两种互补的方法：一种是小致密性展开，提供了封闭形式的解析表达式；另一种是直接数值积分扰动方程。他们专门研究了各向异性流体作为暗物质分布的代理，并计算了不同天体物理相关密度分布下的Love数。作者还讨论了流体扰动的不同表述与所得Love数之间的联系，并分析了物质分布的渐近结构对潮汐匹配过程的影响。

Result: The results show that the axial tidal Love numbers can be computed analytically and numerically for different density profiles. The authors find that density profiles lacking compact support, such as power-law distributions, produce logarithmic terms in the asymptotic expansion of the perturbation variable, which complicate the standard tidal matching procedure. These logarithmic terms arise due to the absence of a strictly vacuum exterior. The findings underscore the importance of the asymptotic structure of the matter distribution in the context of tidal deformations.

结果表明，可以为不同的密度分布解析地和数值地计算轴向潮汐Love数。作者发现，缺乏紧支撑的密度分布（例如幂律分布）会在扰动变量的渐近展开中产生对数项，这会复杂化标准的潮汐匹配过程。这些对数项是由于严格真空外部区域的缺失而产生的。这些发现强调了在潮汐形变背景下物质分布的渐近结构的重要性。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the asymptotic structure of the matter distribution significantly affects the computation of tidal Love numbers for black holes surrounded by matter. The presence of logarithmic terms in the perturbation variable for non-compact-support density profiles indicates the need for a more careful treatment of the boundary conditions in the tidal matching procedure. The general framework developed in this work can be applied to other spherically symmetric environments, providing a robust method for studying tidal deformations in the presence of surrounding matter.

结论是，物质分布的渐近结构显著影响被物质包围的黑洞的潮汐Love数的计算。对于非紧支撑密度分布，扰动变量中对数项的存在表明需要更仔细地处理潮汐匹配过程中的边界条件。本文开发的通用框架可以应用于其他球对称环境，为研究有周围物质存在时的潮汐形变提供了一种稳健的方法。

Abstract: We study the axial (magnetic) tidal Love numbers of a Schwarzschild black hole surrounded by a spherically symmetric matter distribution. While the formalism developed here is general, we specialize to the case of anisotropic fluids as a proxy for dark matter distributions, computing the Love numbers for different density profiles of astrophysical interest. We employ two complementary methods: a small-compactness expansion, yielding closed-form analytic expressions, and direct numerical integration of the perturbation equations. We discuss the connection between different formulations of the fluid perturbations and the resulting Love numbers. We further show that density profiles lacking compact support generically produce logarithmic terms in the asymptotic expansion of the perturbation variable, which obstruct the standard tidal matching procedure and whose origin we trace to the absence of a strictly vacuum exterior. Our findings highlight the importance of controlling the asymptotic structure of the matter distribution when defining tidal observables for black holes dressed by matter, and provide a general framework that can be applied to other spherically symmetric environments.

</details>


### [93] [Hadronic lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02807)
*Fabrizio Canfora,Cristóbal Corral,Borja Diez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper introduces an analytic approach to study gravitational lensing in the presence of a hadron distribution, using a nonlinear sigma model coupled to Maxwell theory. The authors derive the modified Raychaudhuri equation and integral curves for probe photons, and apply their method to a black hole sourced by superfluid pionic vortices, obtaining corrections to the deflection angle.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop an analytic framework for understanding gravitational lensing in the presence of hadrons, which can be compared to the propagation of photons in a medium with a Cooper-pair condensate. This setup allows for the derivation of transport properties such as the refractive index without relying on phenomenological models, providing a more fundamental description of the phenomenon.

动机是开发一个解析框架，用于理解在强子存在的情况下引力透镜效应，这可以与光子在具有库珀对凝聚态的介质中传播的情况进行比较。这种设置允许推导出传输特性，如折射率，而无需依赖唯象模型，从而提供对现象更基本的描述。

Method: The authors use a nonlinear sigma model minimally coupled to Maxwell theory to describe the hadrons. They derive the modified Raychaudhuri equation that includes hadronic corrections and determine the integral curves of probe photons in the eikonal approximation. The analytical expressions for the refractive index and other transport properties are derived from the hadronic density.

作者使用最小耦合到麦克斯韦理论的非线性sigma模型来描述强子。他们推导了包括强子修正的修正Raychaudhuri方程，并确定了探针光子在几何光学近似下的积分曲线。从强子密度中推导出折射率和其他传输特性的解析表达式。

Result: The results include the derivation of the modified Raychaudhuri equation, the integral curves of probe photons, and the analytical expressions for the refractive index. The authors also provide an example of hadronic lensing produced by a black hole sourced by superfluid pionic vortices, and they calculate the hadronic correction to the deflection angle in the weak-field limit.

结果包括修正的Raychaudhuri方程的推导、探针光子的积分曲线以及折射率的解析表达式。作者还提供了一个由超流π介子涡旋源产生的黑洞引起的强子透镜效应的例子，并计算了弱场极限下偏转角的强子修正。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that the proposed analytic approach provides a consistent and fundamental framework for studying gravitational lensing in the presence of a hadron distribution. The method allows for the explicit calculation of the refractive index and other transport properties, and it can be applied to specific cases, such as the hadronic lensing by a black hole sourced by superfluid pionic vortices.

论文得出结论，提出的解析方法为研究强子分布存在情况下的引力透镜效应提供了统一且基本的框架。该方法允许显式计算折射率和其他传输特性，并可应用于特定情况，例如由超流π介子涡旋源产生的黑洞引起的强子透镜效应。

Abstract: We introduce an analytic approach to study gravitational lensing in the presence of a distribution of hadrons. The situation is analogous to the propagation of photons in a medium with a nontrivial Cooper-pair condensate, where the photon acquires an effective mass term that may depend on the coordinates if the condensate is not homogeneous. As a result, photons generally do not follow null geodesics in the hadronic medium. In this setup, hadrons are described by the nonlinear sigma model minimally coupled to Maxwell theory. The modified Raychaudhuri equation, including hadronic corrections, is derived, along with the integral curves of probe photons in the eikonal approximation. These results are consistent with the theory of gravitational lensing in plasma media, with the advantage that transport properties, such as the refractive index, can be expressed analytically in terms of the hadronic density without assuming a phenomenological modeling thereof. As an example, we study the hadronic lensing produced by an analytic black hole sourced by superfluid pionic vortices, and we obtain the hadronic correction to the deflection angle in the weak-field limit.

</details>


### [94] [Derivation of the Smarr formula from the Komar charge in Einstein-nonlinear electrodynamics theories and applications to regular black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02813)
*Gabriele Barbagallo,Tomás Ortín*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper constructs a generalized Komar charge for non-linear electrodynamics (NLED) theories in 4 dimensions, coupled to Einstein gravity. It includes the contribution of the coupling constant by treating it as a dynamical field. The derived Smarr formula is tested on various Einstein--NLED theories and used to analyze the thermodynamics of the regular Bardeen black hole.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to extend the concept of Komar charge to non-linear electrodynamics (NLED) theories and to include the contribution of the dimensionful coupling constant. This is achieved by promoting the coupling constant to a dynamical field and using a Lagrange multiplier to keep it constant on-shell. The goal is to derive a Smarr formula that accounts for the coupling constant's contribution and to test its validity on a broad class of Einstein--NLED theories, including the regular Bardeen black hole.

动机是将Komar电荷的概念扩展到非线性电动力学（NLED）理论，并包括维度耦合常数的贡献。这是通过将耦合常数提升为一个动力学场并使用拉格朗日乘数使其在壳上保持恒定来实现的。目标是推导出一个考虑耦合常数贡献的Smarr公式，并在广泛的Einstein--NLED理论中测试其有效性，包括正则Bardeen黑洞。

Method: The method involves constructing the generalized Komar charge for generic NLED theories in 4 dimensions coupled to Einstein gravity. The coupling constant is treated as a dynamical field and forced to be constant on-shell using a Lagrange multiplier. The derived Smarr formula is then applied to asymptotically-flat black-hole and soliton solutions. The thermodynamics of the regular Bardeen black hole is analyzed using the conservation of the generalized Komar charge.

方法涉及构建与爱因斯坦引力耦合的四维通用NLED理论的广义Komar电荷。耦合常数被视为一个动力学场，并使用拉格朗日乘数使其在壳上保持恒定。然后将推导出的Smarr公式应用于渐近平坦的黑洞和孤子解。使用广义Komar电荷的守恒来分析正则Bardeen黑洞的热力学。

Result: The result is a generalized Smarr formula that includes the contribution of the coupling constant. This formula is tested on a broad class of Einstein--NLED theories, and it is used to analyze the thermodynamics of the regular Bardeen black hole. The analysis provides insights into the regularity of regular black holes inside the event horizon.

结果是一个包含耦合常数贡献的广义Smarr公式。该公式在广泛的Einstein--NLED理论中进行了测试，并用于分析正则Bardeen黑洞的热力学。分析提供了关于事件视界内正则黑洞规则性的见解。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that the generalized Komar charge and the derived Smarr formula provide a consistent framework for understanding the thermodynamics of black holes and solitons in NLED theories. The inclusion of the coupling constant's contribution is essential for a complete description, and the analysis of the regular Bardeen black hole demonstrates the utility of this approach in understanding the regularity of black holes.

结论是广义Komar电荷和推导出的Smarr公式为理解NLED理论中黑洞和孤子的热力学提供了一致的框架。包含耦合常数的贡献对于完整描述是必不可少的，正则Bardeen黑洞的分析展示了这种方法在理解黑洞规则性方面的实用性。

Abstract: We construct the generalized Komar charge of generic, non-linear theories of electrodynamics (NLED) in 4 dimensions coupled to Einstein gravity. The contribution of the dimensionful coupling constant present in all these theories is obtained by promoting it to a dynamical field which is forced to be constant on-shell by a Lagrange multiplier. We use this charge to derive a Smarr formula for asymptotically-flat black-hole and soliton solutions of these theories that includes the contribution of the coupling constant. Previously, this contribution had been found using homogeneity arguments. We test our results on a broad class of Einstein--NLED theories and analyze in detail the thermodynamics of the regular Bardeen black hole using the conservation of the generalized Komar charge to understand the regularity of regular black holes inside the event horizon.

</details>


### [95] [Gravitational-Bumblebee perturbations: Exact decoupling and isospectrality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02820)
*Hui-Fa Liu,Wentao Liu,Yu-Xiao Liu,Qi Su,Ding-fang Zeng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper presents the exact decoupling of metric and bumblebee field perturbations in a Schwarzschild-like background, resulting in four decoupled master equations. The gravitational modes are immune to Lorentz-violating coupling, while the vector modes' propagation speed is modified. This work provides a theoretical basis for testing spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking using black hole perturbations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation behind this work is to explore the effects of Lorentz-violating couplings on the perturbations of a Schwarzschild-like spacetime, specifically through the interaction with a bumblebee field. The aim is to understand how such violations influence the gravitational and vector sectors, and to identify potential observational signatures that could be used to test these theories in the context of multi-messenger astronomy.

本文的动机是探索洛伦兹违反耦合对类史瓦西时空扰动的影响，特别是通过与bumblebee场的相互作用。目的是理解这种违反如何影响引力和矢量部门，并识别可用于在多信使天文学背景下测试这些理论的潜在观测特征。

Method: The authors perform an exact decoupling of the full metric and bumblebee field perturbations in a Schwarzschild-like background. They derive four decoupled master equations, two for each parity sector, which describe the gravitational and Lorentz-violating vector modes. The method involves a detailed analysis of the coupled system, leading to the discovery of the dynamical immunity of the gravitational modes to the non-minimal Lorentz-violating coupling.

作者在一个类史瓦西背景中进行了全度规和bumblebee场扰动的精确解耦。他们推导出四个解耦的主方程，每个奇偶性部门两个，描述了引力模式和洛伦兹违反矢量模式。该方法涉及对耦合系统的详细分析，从而发现了引力模式对非最小洛伦兹违反耦合的动力学免疫性。

Result: The result of the analysis shows that the gravitational master modes exhibit dynamical immunity to the non-minimal Lorentz-violating coupling, while the vector modes' propagation speed is affected by the Lorentz violation. Importantly, the odd- and even-parity perturbations remain strictly isospectral, indicating that the gravitational ringdown spectrum is not altered by the Lorentz-violating couplings. This finding suggests a possible timing signature due to the mismatch in propagation speeds, which could be used to test for spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking.

分析结果表明，引力主模式对非最小洛伦兹违反耦合表现出动力学免疫性，而矢量模式的传播速度受到洛伦兹违反的影响。重要的是，奇偶性扰动仍然严格等谱，这表明引力环降谱不受洛伦兹违反耦合的影响。这一发现暗示了由于传播速度不匹配而可能产生的时序特征，这可以用来测试自发洛伦兹对称性破缺。

Conclusion: The conclusion of the paper is that the presence of Lorentz-violating couplings can reshape the field reconstruction without altering the gravitational ringdown spectrum. This unique behavior offers a theoretical route to testing spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking in the era of multi-messenger astronomy, potentially through the observation of timing signatures in black hole perturbations.

论文的结论是，洛伦兹违反耦合的存在可以在不改变引力环降谱的情况下重塑场重建。这种独特的行为为在多信使天文学时代测试自发洛伦兹对称性破缺提供了一条理论途径，可能通过观察黑洞扰动中的时序特征来实现。

Abstract: In this paper, we present the exact decoupling of the full metric and bumblebee field perturbations in a Schwarzschild-like background. The coupled system reduces to four decoupled master equations, revealing in each parity sector a Schwarzschild-like gravitational sector and a Lorentz-violating Maxwell-like vector sector. While Lorentz violation modifies the propagation speed of the emergent vector modes, we demonstrate that the gravitational master modes exhibit a ``dynamical immunity'' to the non-minimal Lorentz-violating coupling, and that the odd- and even-parity perturbations remain strictly isospectral. Our work provides a rare example in which Lorentz-violating couplings reshape the field reconstruction while leaving the gravitational ringdown spectrum intact. This mismatch in propagation speeds suggests a possible timing signature of bumblebee vector dynamics in black hole perturbations, offering a theoretical route to testing spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking in the era of multi-messenger astronomy.

</details>
